### Jersey Sour

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Apple brandy is possibly the best spirit on which to base a sour.

* 1½ shot Laird's Straight Bottled in Bond applejack
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Lavender Margarita

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Lavender lime and tequila combine harmoniously.

* 2 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Le Sirop de Monin Lavandie - Lavender Sugar Syrup
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### The Last Word cocktail

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Chartreuse devotees will love this balanced, tangy drink. I'm one.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ⅔ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ⅔ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ⅔ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lime twist (discarded) and Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Lisa's Special Daiquiri

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Reminiscent of a Hemingway Special, this flavoursome, vanilla laced Daiquiri has a wonderfully tangy, bitter sweet finish.

* 2½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%) (infused with vanilla)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Vanilla sugar syrup
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Mai Tai (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** We love Daiquiris and this is basically a classic Daiquiri with a few bells and whistles: Orange curaçao, lime juice, almond syrup, amaretto, falernum, 
white crème de menthe and absinthe.

* 1 shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* 1 shot Pineapple rum
* ½ shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Giffard Sirop de Orgeat (Almond) Syrup
* ¼ shot Disaronno Originale Amaretto liqueur
* ¼ shot John D. Taylor's Velvet Falernum Liqueur
* 1/12 shot Giffard Menthe Pastille white crème de menthe liqueur
* 2 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* Garnish: Mint sprigs, lime shell & fruit stick

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into glass filled with crushed ice.

---

### Margarita on-the-rocks (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** This is how we prefer our margaritas to be served. Tangy citrus and tequila with a hint of balancing sweetness and a faint salty undertone. We also prefer the subtlety of half a pinch of salt in the drink to a salt laden glass rim.

* 1½ shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¾ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1 spoon AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* ½ pinch Salt
* 4 drop Difford's Margarita Bitters by Bob's Bitters (optional)
* Garnish: Salt rim (optional) & lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Martinez #1  (Original Genever)

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Medium dry, rounded and superbly complex. Your choice of jenever will make or break this fabulous cocktail - choose with care.

* 2 shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ¼ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¼ shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Mary Pickford Cocktail

* ⅛ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Aviation Cocktail (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Benefits from a long shake/dilution. Citrus, floral gin with a slightly sour finish.

* 1¾ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ¼ shot Créme de violette liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (& optional sugar rim)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Missionary's Downfall

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Superbly balanced and refreshing rum, lime, mint and a hint of peach.

* 12 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Original Peachtree Liqueur Buy from amazon
* 1½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 2 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE mint (just to bruise) in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and strain into glass filled with crushed ice.

---

### Mojito Cocktail

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** When well made, this Cuban cousin of the Mint Julep is one of the world's greatest and most refreshing cocktails.

* 12 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE mint (just to bruise) in base of glass. Add rum, lime juice and sugar. Half fill glass with crushed ice and CHURN (stir) with bar spoon. Fill glass with more crushed ice and CHURN some more. TOP with soda, stir and serve with straws.

---

### Negroni Cocktail

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Bitter and dry, but very tasty. This no namby-pamby drink is traditionally assembled and mixed directly in the glass. There is something about a Negroni that does not suit fussing about with mixing glasses and strainers. To garnish with a lemon slice is a heinous crime but I am quite partial to a fat orange wedge.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1½ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* 1½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into ice-filled glass and STIR.

---

### Oh Gosh!

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur

* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Orange Brulée

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A great looking, beautifully balanced after-dinner drink.

* 1½ shot Disaronno Originale Amaretto liqueur
* 1½ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* ¾ shot Cognac
* ¼ shot Single cream / half-and-half
* Garnish: Dust with chocolate powder

**Instructions:** SHAKE first three ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. FLOAT thin layer of cream over drink and turn glass to spread evenly.

---

### Pisco Punch (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A tangy, balanced combination of rich flavours. The quality of pisco used is crucial to the success of a Pisco Punch.

* 2 dried Clove
* 2 shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* 1 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge

**Instructions:** MUDDLE cloves in base of shaker. ADD next 5 ingredients, SHAKE with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with champagne.

---

### Pisco Punch (Prosser's recipe)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** An aromatic take on the Pisco Punch.

* 20 fresh Seedless white grapes
* 2½ shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* 1 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ⅛ shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* Garnish: White grapes

**Instructions:** MUDDLE grapes in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Poet's Dream

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Subtle, honeyed and herbal.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Polish Martini

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** In Poland Bison Grass vodka and apple juice are a classic combo, here also with an additional splash of Polish honey liqueur.

Adjust the quantity of apple juice and honey liqueur to suit your palate. We played around with this recipe a lot over the years, (it's one of our favs) and for us, equal parts (preferably with freshly pressed green apple juice) is perfectly balanced.

* ¾ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ¾ shot Bison grass vodka
* ¾ shot Honey liqueur - Spiced
* ¾ shot Pressed apple juice
* Garnish: Apple slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Ramos Gin Fizz

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** One of the great classic cocktails. The perfect balance of sweet and sour is enhanced by the incredibly smooth, almost fluffy mouthfeel.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¾ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ⅛ shot Orange flower water
* 3 drop Vanilla extract (optional)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* 1 shot Single cream / half-and-half
* Top up with Soda from siphon
* Garnish: Lemon slice & mint sprig

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 8 ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE without ice and strain into chilled glass (no ice in glass). TOP with soda from siphon. 

Some recipes for a Ramos Gin Fizz, and indeed Henry’s original recipe, calls for old tom gin, in which case you may need to reduce the amount of sugar syrup depending on your old tom.

---

### Red Snapper

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Looks like a Bloody Mary, and tastes a lot like a Bloody Mary, but features gin's aromatic botanicals.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 4 shot Tomato juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 4 dash Worcestershire sauce
* 7 drop Hot pepper sauce
* 2 grind Black pepper
* 2 pinch Celery salt
* Garnish: Salt & pepper rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. Serve with straws.

---

### Royal Mojito

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A mojito topped with champagne instead of soda water. There's posh.

* 12 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE mint (just to bruise) in base of glass. Add rum, lime juice and sugar. Half fill glass with crushed ice and CHURN (stir) with bar spoon. Fill glass with more crushed ice and CHURN some more. TOP with champagne, stir and serve with straws.

---

### Rum Punch

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** In Jamaica, the spiritual home of the Rum Punch, they like their rum overproof (more than 57% alc./vol.) and serving over crushed ice dilutes and tames this very strong spirit.

* 2¼ shot White overproof rum
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 3 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* 3 shot Chilled water
* Garnish: Orange slice & cherry on stick (sail)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into glass filled with crushed ice.

---

### Santiago Daiquiri

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** This Daiquiri is particularly delicate in its balance between sweet and sour.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Basil & Honey Daiquiri

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Basil adds dry vegetable notes to a honeyed Daiquiri.

* 2 spoon Runny honey
* 2½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 3 fresh Basil leaves
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Basil leaf

**Instructions:** STIR honey and rum in base of shaker until honey dissolves. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Widow's Kiss

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

* ¾ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* ¾ shot Chartreuse Jaune (Yellow Chartreuse) Liqueur

### Addington

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Substituting vermouths, such as Martini Reserva Rubino, dramatically alters the character of this cocktail.

* 2 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* Top up with Soda from siphon
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE first two ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. TOP with just the merest squirt of soda from chilled siphon.

---

### Bacardi Special

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Hit the perfect proportions and you will strike a wondrous balance of flavoursome rum, gin botanicals, limey sourness and fruity sweetness.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ¾ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Daiquiri No.1 natural (Embury's 8:2:1 formula)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Traditionally a Natural Daiquiri should always be based on light rum but if I should feel like breaking with tradition and using aged rum, I find Embury's 8:2:1 formula works particularly well.

* 2 shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Difford's Fruit Cup No.1 (gin based & Pimm's Cup-like)

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** This long refreshing fruity cocktail mimics the characteristics of a Pimm’s Cup but with the punch and fullness of flavour reminiscent of distant decades when Pimm’s No.1 carried a full 9% more alc./vol. that it does today. Predictably, my version is a good deal boozier. If you find too boozy for a summer's afternoon then knock each of the first 3 ingredients a tad (1/4oz / 7.5ml) and add a splash more (1/2oz / 15ml) to the last 2 ingredients.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* 2 shot Ginger ale
* 2 shot Coca-Cola
* Garnish: Lemon, orange & strawberry slices, mint sprig & borage in drink

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into glass. Half fill glass with ice. Add a citrus slice and a couple of mint leaves from garnish before filling to brim with ice. Finish with rest of garnish.

---

### Picador

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** The name might be more masculine but it still tastes just like a classic Margarita.

* 2 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* 1 shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur

* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Ampersand Cocktail

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** A boozy brandy influenced wet, sweet Martini with a hint of orange. Only discerning drinkers need apply. Those after sweet, less challenging drinks should refrain.

* 1 shot Tanqueray Old Tom gin
* 1 shot Cognac
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ⅛ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Bloody Mary (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A Bloody Mary Cocktail with a hint of bell pepper freshness and a touch of sherry.

* ½ ring Yellow bell pepper (chopped)
* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 3 shot Tomato juice
* ½ shot Amontillado sherry
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 pinch Celery salt
* 3 grind Black pepper
* 10 drop Hot pepper sauce
* 4 dash Worcestershire sauce
* Garnish: Dust with freshly grated black pepper & place celery stick in glass (optional salt & pepper rim)

**Instructions:** MUDDLE pepper in base of shaker. Add other ingredients and ice then ROLL (rotate) rather than shake and strain into ice-filled glass. Use ice fresh from freezer (rather than ice-machine) to fill glass to avoid unwanted dilution.

---

### Breakfast Club

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Slightly smoky with incredible depth of flavour. A perfectly balanced delight.

* 1 spoon English orange marmalade
* 1 spoon Runny honey
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Cold Lapsang Souchong tea
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR honey and marmalade with rum until dissolved. Add tea, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Casino #1

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Basically, an Aviation without crème de violette, dried and made more complex with a dash of orange bitters.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Daiquiri No.1 on-the-rocks (Difford's 10:3:2 formula)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Light and refreshing. No one flavour predominates - sweet and sour are in harmony with the rum.

* 2½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Lime slice & Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Daiquiri No.1 frozen (Difford's 16:6:6:1 formula)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Blend with too much ice and you will have a tasteless slushy drink that will give you brain-ache if you drink it too fast. However, made correctly and fine strained this is a superbly refreshing drink on a hot day.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¾ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ⅛ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** BLEND well all ingredients with 6oz scoop of crushed ice. STRAIN blended drink through a fine strainer to remove ice fragments.

---

### Daiquiri No.3

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A Daiquiri No.1 with a tang of grapefruit and hint of maraschino. Essentially a Hemingway Special Daiquiri (Papa Doble Daiquiri) for folk without the great author's constitution or love of the sours.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ⅛ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Damn It Jimmy

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Delicately flavoured and ever so very slightly sweet. Made with Bacardi Carta Blanca (as it originally was) this delicate cocktail has complex notes of blue cheese with faint salty sherry and herbal dry vermouth complexity. it is probably the best drink I've created - although i'd like to think I've a good few more in me

* 1½ shot Junmai ginjō sake
* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ¼ shot Fino sherry
* ¼ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Blue cheese stuffed olive

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Aged Honey Daiquiri

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Sweet honey replaces sugar syrup in this natural Daiquiri. Try experimenting with different honeys. We favour orange blossom honey.

* 2 shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* 1½ spoon Runny honey
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Chilled water
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** STIR honey with rum in base of shaker until honey dissolves. Add lime juice and water, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Left Bank Martini

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** An aromatic, dry blend. Modern bartending convention would suggest that this drink should be stirred. However, it’s much better shaken. Go easy with the spray of lime zest oils - this delicate drink is easily over powered with any more than a fine mist.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* ½ shot Chardonnay (Chablis) white wine
* ¼ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

* ⅛ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

---

### Martinez (made with Old Tom)

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Use an authentic tasting distilled old tom gin that's balanced rather than overly sweet and you'll have a fabulous cocktail.

We've used dry vermouth to balance the sweet vermouth but if you're looking for simplicity and less ingredients then you might want to omit the dry vermouth and balance by reducing the sweet vermouth and maraschino while also doubling the bitters as follows:

2 shot Old Tom Gin
2/3 shot Sweet vermouth
1/8 shot Maraschino
2 dashes of orange bitters

* 2 shot Tanqueray Old Tom gin
* ¼ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¾ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ¼ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (discarded) & Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** STIR ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Mezcal Margarita

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** A smokin' Margarita.

* 1½ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* ¾ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1/12 shot AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* ½ pinch Salt
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Mojito Cocktail (Difford's method)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** All the flavour of the Mojito but without unattractive mint leaves trapped in crushed ice. This only works when fresh, cold crushed ice is used. Otherwise the drink will be overly diluted.

* 12 fresh Mint leaves
* 2½ shot Bacardi Carta Oro Superior Gold Rum
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ⅛ shot Giffard Menthe Pastille white crème de menthe liqueur
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass. CHURN (stir) with bar spoon. Fill glass with more crushed ice and CHURN some more. Keep adding ice and churning until drink fills glass. Serve with straws.

---

### Dry Martini (Montgomery's 15:1 ratio)

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Bone dry - a superbly cleansing Martini. Through experimentation we have found that 15:1 Martinis are better shaken rather than stirred. Conversely 3:1 Martinis are better stirred rather than shaken. I also prefer an orange zest twist to the more usual lemon zest or olive.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ⅛ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Negroni Spumante

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A Negroni lengthened with sparkling wine. Every Negroni drinker should try this variation

* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1 shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* Top up with Spumante (or brut champagne)
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** POUR first 3 ingredients into ice-filled glass. TOP with spumante and lightly STIR.

---

### Pyramid Punch

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Tangy, fruity and packed with flavour. Clove spice, fragrant floral pisco and elderflower with a hint of sweet pineapple and sour grapefruit.

* 2 dried Clove
* 2 shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* 1 shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* 2 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge

**Instructions:** MUDDLE cloves in base of shaker. ADD other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Reversed Vesper & Tonic

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Martini in style but with the hard edges smoothed and a hint of eastern spice added. Worryingly, it took 14 attempts and 13 wasted drinks to arrive at the above formula but it seemed like an idea worth pursuing.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot Lillet Blanc French aperitif wine
* ⅛ shot Becherovka Original (Carlsbad Becher) Liqueur
* ⅛ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* ½ shot Tonic water
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Reverse Martini

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Simply a Dry Martini with the proportions reversed to make a dripping Wet Martini.

* 2 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* Garnish: Chilled olive on stick or lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Rose-Hyp Cocktail

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Created in 2006 by yours truly (Simon Difford) in London, England.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¼ shot Rose petal liqueur
* Garnish: Edible flower

**Instructions:** THROW all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Rum Swizzle

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Dark rich sugar, equally dark and richly flavoured rum, sweetened and spiced with the clove and cinnamon flavours of falernum and freshened with citrus juice. All served long with crushed ice.

* 2 shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* ⅔ shot John D. Taylor's Velvet Falernum Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Demerara sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Mint sprig & orange slice

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into chilled glass and two-thirds fill with crushed ice. SWIZZLE with a swizzle stick (or churn with a barspoon). Add more crushed ice to fill and SWIZZLE some more. Serve with straws.

---

### The Stig

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Whiter than white but yet mysterious.

* ¾ shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* ¾ shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* 1 shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* 1 shot Sauvignon blanc white wine
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Giblet (Tequila Gimlet)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Tequila and lime are divine, and this riff on the usually gin-based original Gimlet is as good, although very different with the earthiness of the tequila adding an extra dimension which more than compensates for the lack of gin's botanical complexity.

* 2 shot Patrón Silver Tequila (green seal) 100% agave tequila
* ⅙ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* ⅙ shot Rose's lime cordial
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ⅙ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅙ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Vesper Dry Martini

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Many bartenders advocate that a Martini should be stirred and not shaken, some citing the ridiculous argument that shaking will “bruise the gin.” If you like your Martinis shaken then avoid the possible look of distaste from your server and order a Vesper. This particular Dry Martini is always shaken, an action that aerates the drink, and makes it colder and more dilute than simply stirring. It also gives the drink a slightly clouded appearance and can leave small shards of ice on the surface of the drink - easily prevented by the use of a fine strainer when pouring.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ⅔ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ⅓ shot Lillet Blanc French aperitif wine
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Daiquiri Elixir

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Freshly pressed sugar cane syrup and the French elixir Chartreuse add complexity to the classic Daiquiri.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Clément Sirop Sucre de Canne (sugar cane juice syrup)
* ⅛ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Periscope

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Fabulously light, almost creamy, and very refreshing.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* ⅛ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅛ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### The Puritan

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Vermouth enhances the aromatics; Chartreuse and orange bitters add a hint of sweetness and complexity; gin underpins the whole.

* 1¾ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¼ shot Chartreuse Jaune (Yellow Chartreuse) Liqueur
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

### Chanticleer Cocktail

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Wonderfully aromatic orange with a complex balance of gin and vermouth.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ½ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** DRY SHAKE all ingredients (without ice). SHAKE again with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Cuban Liberal

* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### The Money Penny

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Fresh grapefruit and gin soured with a splash of grapefruit and balanced with the merest touch of sugar.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 dash Bittermens Hopped Grapefruit Bitters
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Rum Old Fashioned

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** The flavour of the overproof rum greatly adds to the character of this Old Fashioned. There are many rum Old Fashioned riffs but this is the recipe that made this cocktail both special and famous.

* 2 shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* ½ shot White overproof rum
* ¼ shot John D. Taylor's Velvet Falernum Liqueur
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR rum with three ice cubes in a glass. ADD sugar, falernum, bitters and two more ice cubes. STIR lots more and add more ice.

---

### Hollywood

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** This drink is deliciously different. Rum, grapefruit and pomegranate smoothed with egg white and spice with nutmeg.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ⅛ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Dust with grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** DRY SHAKE all ingredients without ice to emulsify. SHAKE again with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### King's Jubilee

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** If there is such a thing as a 'Rum Aviation', then this is surely it.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ¾ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Amatitan Twist

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** The sublime taste of great añejo tequila mellowed and delicately flavoured with maraschino, chartreuse and grapefruit bitters.

* 2 shot Patrón Añejo Tequila
* ¼ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ¼ shot Chartreuse Jaune (Yellow Chartreuse) Liqueur
* 2 dash Bittermens Hopped Grapefruit Bitters
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Cognac Julep

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A truly deliciously refreshing cocktail. Woody rancio notes in the cognac are freshened by the mint. Those with a dry palate may want to reduce the sugar a touch.

* 12 fresh Mint leaves
* 2½ shot Cognac
* ⅔ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into julep cup half filled with crushed ice. CHURN (stir) the drink with the crushed ice using a bar spoon. Top up the cup with more crushed ice and CHURN again. Repeat this process until the drink fills the cup and serve.

---

### La Perla

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Simple yet complex, this beautifully balanced cocktail has faint saltiness from the manzanilla, delicate pear fruit and well integrated fortifying tequila.

* 1½ shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* 1½ shot Manzanilla Sherry
* ¾ shot Poire William pear liqueur
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### El Presidente No.1 #2

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** This rose pink tinted coloured drink harnesses a delicate balance between light rum and vermouth with a touch of pomegranate fruity sweetness.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¼ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Salty Martini

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** As the name suggests, fino sherry and caper brine add saltiness but this 'Salty Martini' also has a distinct nuttiness from the sherry. We'd suggest both a long stir for generous dilution, and serving with grilled almonds.

* 2½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ¼ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¼ shot Fino sherry
* ⅛ shot Caper brine (from jar)
* Garnish: Large caperberry on pick

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Dry Martini #4 (Embury’s 7:1 ratio)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Readers of Embury will know he had a bone dry palate and Martinis made to his specification are just that, and with the correct dilution, fabulous.

* 2½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ⅓ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* Garnish: Chilled olive on stick or lemon zest twist.

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Gin Salad Dry Martini

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A Gin Salad is made like a regular Dry Martini but with three olives and two cocktail onions as garnish. They should be pushed onto the stick in the following order: olive-onion-olive-onion-olive.

* 2½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters (optional)
* Garnish: 3 chilled olives and 2 cocktail onions

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Malty Dry Martini

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Using a genuinely malty oude jenever produces a deliciously retro take on the modern Dry Martini.

* 2½ shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* Garnish: Chilled olive or lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Breakfast Martini

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** The success or failure of this tangy drink is partly reliant on the quality of marmalade used.

* 1 spoon English orange marmalade (fine sliced)
* 1⅔ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Garnish: Orange zest twist & slice of toast on rim

**Instructions:** STIR marmalade with gin in base of shaker until it dissolves. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### General Harrison's Nogg

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A whole raw egg contributes body to this filling, flavoursome, wintry, delicate cocktail. The retained CO2 fizz of the cider adds essential body and balancing acidy but demands the use of a specialised shaker.

* 1½ shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* 2 shot Medium dry apple cider
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Dale DeGroff's Pimento Aromatic Bitters
* 1 fresh Egg (white & yolk)
* Garnish: Dust with freshly grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** Using an especially designed ‘fizz’ shaker (such as Perlini) that’s designed to be carbonated. SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into glass (without ice). Be sure to shake well to completely emulsify the egg.

---

### Gin Basil Smash / Gin Pesto

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Jörg, the creator of this cocktail, says, "Better too much, than not enough basil in this drink". He also specifies that the basil is muddled rather than just broken by the action of shaking as this produces a greener drink.

He also says, "keep in mind:
5 cl Gin is not enough.
6 cl Gin is the recipe
7 cl Gin is LOVE."

* 12 fresh Basil leaves
* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: 3 basil sprigs

**Instructions:** Gently muddle basil in base of SHAKER with Gin (and ideally leave to stand for 10 minutes). ADD other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Nelson's Blood #2

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** The pungent flavours of naval rum contribute to this tasty, fruity rum punch with will warm your cockles – m' hearties!

* 2 shot Navy rum (54.5% alc./vol.)
* 2 shot Cranberry juice
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water) (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 3 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice.

---

### New Orleans Gin Fizz

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** The full flavour of Old Tom gin adds an extra dimension to this classic Gin Fizz. Indeed, it is probably the original Gin Fizz.

* 2¼ shot Tanqueray Old Tom gin
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¾ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water) (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ⅛ shot Orange flower water
* 1 shot Pasteurised egg white
* 1 shot Single cream / half-and-half
* Top up with Soda from siphon
* Garnish: Lemon slice & mint sprig

**Instructions:** 1. Vigorously SHAKE first 7 ingredients with ice and pour back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass (no ice in glass). TOP with soda water from siphon.

ALTERNATIVELY, 2. Flash BLEND first 7 ingredients without ice (to emulsify mix). Then pour contents of blender into shaker and SHAKE with ice. Strain into chilled glass (no ice in glass) and TOP with soda from siphon.

---

### Huckle my buff

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** To quote Jamie Oliver, “the Huckle-my-buff is not a Dodo but a Phoenix”.

* 1 fresh Egg yolk
* 5 shot Harveys Porter 1859
* 1 shot Cognac
* ¼ shot King's Ginger Liqueur
* ¾ shot Demerara sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Freshly grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** Gently BLEND all ingredients on a slow speed then warm in a saucepan, gently stirring with a whisk (or microwave for 30 seconds and stir), then pour into warmed glass. If you make several servings in one batch, keep warm and serve from a sous-vide or heated soup kettle at to 60°C.

---

### Reality Check

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Raspberry fruit, herbal complexity and dry hoppy beer with a splash of zesty lime. Fabulously refreshing.

* 5 fresh Raspberries
* ⅔ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ⅔ shot Becherovka Original (Carlsbad Becher) Liqueur
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 2¾ shot Budweiser Budvar Pilsner
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** MUDDLE raspberries in base of large shaker tin. Add ice and other ingredients then THROW (strain from a height into a second strainer). Repeat four times and then strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Honey Bee Mine

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Honey and vanilla laced with white rum and charged with champagne. Perfect for Valentine's Day.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 3 spoon Runny honey
* ⅛ shot Vanilla extract
* ¾ shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (discarded) & honeycomb on rim

**Instructions:** STIR honey with rum in base of shaker to dissolve honey. Add vanilla essence, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. TOP with champagne.

---

### Pina Colada (Difford’s recipe)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A splash of cachaça adds some Latin flavour, lime adds a citrusy bite while a splash of fresh cream makes this Piña Colada creamy white.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca
* 3½ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ¾ shot Cream of coconut
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Single cream / half-and-half
* 1 pinch Salt
* Garnish: Parasol, pineapple wedge & Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** BLEND all ingredients with 6oz scoop crushed ice and serve with paper straws.

---

### Ford Cocktail

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** The Ford Cocktail is a Martini-style cocktail sweetened by both the use of old tom gin and Bénédictine D.O.M. liqueur (not B&B) served ‘wet’ with a generous splash of dry vermouth. The orange bitters and zest are essential to the drink’s success.

* 2 shot Tanqueray Old Tom gin
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ⅓ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Tequila Old Fashioned

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A hint of agave syrup sweetness knocks and dilution from the stirred ice knock back the spirit's fire while opening and releasing flavours.

* 2½ shot Patrón Añejo Tequila
* ¼ shot AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* 3 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR one shot of tequila with three ice cubes (dry to the touch frozen ice, not wet ice) in a glass. Add sugar syrup and Angostura bitters and two more ice cubes. STIR some more and add another two ice cubes and the rest of the tequila. STIR some more, and if you have room, add more ice.

---

### Bamboo Cocktail (Difford's 'Perfect' recipe)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Sweet vermouth counters dry sherry with dry vermouth further enhancing the vinous flavours and balance. Orange bitters and an orange zest twist add citrus freshness and enhances the delicate bittersweet balance.

* 1½ shot Fino sherry
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ¾ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### April Fool

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** To quote Karen Fick, "you can't beat a glass of water". Hence we have foolishly scored this drink 5+/5.

* 3 shot Chilled water
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (discarded) & olive

**Instructions:** STIR with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Special Brew Martini

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Hopefully it's ‘Special’! ‘Brew’ refers to both the use of Byrrh (pronounced beer) and sake (which is brewed). To be a true ‘Martini’ a cocktail should have both gin and vermouth – we tried gin but vodka worked so much better. Byrrh doesn’t qualify as a vermouth as while an aromatised wine it lacks wormwood – an omission made up for in this drink with a dash of absinthe.

* 1¼ shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1¼ shot Byrrh Grand Quinquina Aromatized Wine
* 1¼ shot Junmai ginjō sake
* 1 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Marsala Martini

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Tony C’s original recipe calls for 50ml London dry gin, 10ml marsala dolce (dry marsala), 5ml dry vermouth and 3 dashes 69 Colebrooke Row made almond bitters. Sadly we didn’t have the 69 Colebrooke Row lab kit or the patience to use it, so we subbed amaretto for almond bitters and then dried the combo by using dry marsala in place of sweet marsala.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ⅓ shot Marsala Superiore DOC secco wine
* ⅓ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ⅛ shot Disaronno Originale Amaretto liqueur
* Garnish: Pickled almond

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Byrrh & Beer on-the-rocks

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** I love a good beer and I love Byrrh – a marriage made in Bermondsey. Best served as an aperitif cocktail.

* 2 shot Byrrh Grand Quinquina Aromatized Wine
* 2 shot Fuller’s Chiswick Bitter
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into ice-filled glass and stir.

---

### English Marmalade

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** The addition of Campari and aromatic bitters to the classic recipe from the 1930 Savoy Cocktail Book, lifts the Marmalade Cocktail to a new level of bittersweet complexity.

* 1 spoon English orange marmalade
* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¼ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR marmalade with gin in base of shaker so as to dissolve marmalade. ADD other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### La Poire des Benedictines

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Pear and cognac are a match made in heaven. Bénédictine adds honeyed sweetness and herbal complexity to this after dinner cocktail.

* ¾ shot Pear flavoured vodka
* ¾ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* ¾ shot Cognac
* ¼ shot Chilled water
* Garnish: Pear wedge speared with cube of Roquefort cheese

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Bermondsey Minute

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Tequila and lavender are a match made in heaven, made more complex with herbal wine notes from the vermouth, aromatised by delicately fruity maraschino cherry.

* 2 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ⅔ shot Carpano Antica Formula Vermouth
* ¼ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ¼ shot Le Sirop de Monin Lavandie - Lavender Sugar Syrup
* ½ shot Chilled water
* Garnish: Lemon & orange zest twists (discarded) and float 3 coffee beans

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

### Southside Rickey

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** A gin based Mojito served over cracked ice meets the classic Southside. The result is refreshing and easy drinking.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¾ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 5 fresh Mint leaves
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Lime and mint sprigs

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

### Sandy The Showgirl

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Tequila based with complex mezcal smokiness, rich maraschino cherry and floral lavender bitters. It’s a drink that likes dilution so consider serving on the rocks. Sandy’s that kind a girl.

* 1½ shot Patrón Añejo Tequila
* ½ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* ½ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* 1 spoon AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* 8 drop Bob's Lavender Bitters
* ¾ shot Chilled water
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Petanque cocktail

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** The game this drink is named after is French while the main ingredients are Spanish and Italian, but they do play Pétanque in the Basque region of Spain. However, both the creator of this drink and the Peychaud's bitters used in it come from the States - perhaps it took a non-European to bring these ingredients - fino sherry and amaretto - harmonious together.

* 2½ shot Fino sherry
* 1 shot Disaronno Originale Amaretto liqueur
* 2 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* 1 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** STIR first 3 ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass. Then FLOAT half spoon absinthe on surface of drink.

---

### Caipirinha

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** If you are European or in North America you're probably used to this drink being served with crushed ice, but until you have tried it with cubed ice you have not really experienced a Caipirinha. Be sure to muddle the lime and sugar well and stir both before adding ice and after.

* ½ fresh Fresh lime (chopped wedges)
* 3 spoon Caster sugar
* ¾ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* 2 shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca (from freezer)
* Garnish: Stirrer (spoon, wooden lolly stick or stick cut from sugar cane)

**Instructions:** 1. Cut lime in half (from pole to pole) and slice on half into 3-4mm thick half-moon shaped segments and drop into the base of a robust rocks glass.

2. Add 3 bar spoons caster sugar (or ½oz / 15ml sugar syrup 2:1) and MUDDLE.

3. If using cubed ice straight from the freezer, add chilled water (or optionally add fruit of choice) and MUDDLE some more. If using watery ice then omit water.

4. When sure fruit juice is fully extracted and the sugar dissolved, POUR the muddled fruit and sugar into serving glass (preferably a 30cl / 10oz hi-ball glass).

5. POUR cachaça (stored in the freezer) into the rocks glass (the glass used to muddle) and swirl to rinse glass before pouring cachaça into serving glass. STIR to mix with other ingredients.

6. If using cubed ice, crack (rather than crush) four to five large ice cubes and drop into serving glass. STIR before topping with more ice and serve with a stirrer (but no straws).

---

### Suzie Cocktail

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Pisco, pineapple and Sauvignon Blanc wine are a match made in heaven, while gentian liqueur provides complex underlying gentian bittersweet notes.

* 1½ shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* ⅓ shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* 1¼ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Sauvignon blanc white wine
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge on rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

### Naked & Famous

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Salmon pink in colour. Mezcal adds earthy complexity to this bittersweet, citrusy fresh, aperitivo cocktail.

### French 125 (French '75' with cognac)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Cognac makes for a heavier cocktail than a French 75 made with gin, yet this cocktail remains enlivening, refreshing and quaffable.

The use of powdered sugar instead of sugar syrup adds an attractive sherbet note to this cocktail. However, the drink also works well with sugar syrup – use ¼oz/7.5ml sugar syrup in place of the 1½ spoons of powdered sugar.

* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 1½ spoon Powdered sugar (or use 5ml of 2:1 sugar syrup per spoon)
* 1½ shot Cognac
* 2½ shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist on rim

**Instructions:** STIR powdered sugar with lemon juice in base of shaker until sugar dissolves. Add cognac, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. TOP with champagne and lightly stir. (Consider pouring half the champagne into the glass first to help reduce foaming.)

---

### Ultima Palabra

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** This riff on the Last Word is named after the direct Spanish translation of Last Word, hence the use of mezcal in place of gin. Pineapple juice, another distinguishing feature of this riff on the classic, works brilliantly – adding a fruity sweetness and complexity.

* ¾ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* ¾ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ¾ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ¾ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Chilled water
* Garnish: Thyme sprig

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Santa Marta Daiquiri

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** A float of Kirsch eau-de-vie adds wonderfully fruity aromatics to an otherwise classic Natural Daiquiri.

* 2⅓ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Chilled water
* ⅙ shot G. Miclo Kirsch Vieux Grande Reserve Eau de Vie
* Garnish: Lime wedge on rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 3 ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. FLOAT spoon of kirsch eau de vie on surface of drink.

---

### Thin Pink Line

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A subtly almond influenced brandy sour served straight-up and set apart by its namesake ‘Thin Pink Line’ of Peychaud’s bitters which floats on top of the cocktail but beneath the foam.

* 1⅔ shot Cognac
* ⅔ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ⅙ shot Giffard Sirop de Orgeat (Almond) Syrup
* ⅔ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Slowly pour 2 spoons (10ml) Peychaud’s bitters onto a spot in the centre of the drink. After about a minute or so, a 'Thin Pink Line' of bitters develops below the foam.

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Grappa Espresso Martini

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** You’ve almost certainly enjoyed the modern classic that is the Espresso Martini but switch the base spirit from vodka to aged grappa and you’ve an even more delightful drink. Grappa has a more intense favour that does more than fortify, it stands up to espresso coffee’s robust flavours to emerge triumphant in the finished cocktail.

For extra depth and a more complex flavour, try making with a good aged grappa.

* 1½ shot Bepi Tosolini I Legni Rovere Barrique Aged Grappa
* ¾ shot Coffee liqueur
* ¾ shot Espresso coffee (freshly made & hot)
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Float 3 coffee beans

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

* 2 drop Dr. Adam Elmegirab's Boker's Bitters
* 1½ shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR first 4 ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass. Top with chilled champagne.

### Mexican in Manhattan

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** I tried making my usual Sweet Manhattan but with añejo tequila as the base spirit and it was not half bad, but there’s something about tequila that says ‘white’ rather than ‘red’ vermouth. I also started with my favourite addition to a Sweet Manhattan: a half spoon of syrup from the maraschino cherry jar, but añejo tequila is so much more suited to maraschino liqueur. So I switched sweet vermouth for bianco vermouth and Angostura Bitters for lavender bitters. (I love the combination of tequila and lavender.)

* 2½ shot Patrón Añejo Tequila
* 1/12 shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* 1 shot Martini Bianco Vermouth
* 3 dash Bob's Lavender Bitters
* Garnish: Luxardo maraschino cherry on stick

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

### Difford's Fruit Cup No.4 (Rum based)

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** There’s a splash of cola in this fruit cup and the classic marriage of rum and cola sings out in this flavoursome summery, almost tropical, fruit cup. Light golden rum seems to work best, but light white and aged rums also make a great fruit cup.

* 1 shot Bacardi Carta Oro Superior Gold Rum
* 1 shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* 2 shot Ginger ale
* 2 shot Coca-Cola
* Garnish: Lemon, orange & strawberry slices, mint sprig & borage

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into glass. Half fill glass with ice. Add a citrus slice and a couple of mint leaves from garnish before filling to brim with ice. Finish with rest of garnish.

---

### Difford's Fruit Cup No.7 (Tequila based)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Despite being in a relatively small proportion to all the other ingredients in this summery cocktail, tequila’s distinctive notes shine through in the finished drink. We’ve used a reposado tequila but the drink it works equally well, and slightly differently, with a blanco or añejo tequilas.

* 1 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* 1 shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 2 dash Bob's Lavender Bitters
* 2 shot Ginger ale
* 2 shot Coca-Cola
* Garnish: Lemon, orange & strawberry slices, mint sprig & borage

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into glass. Half fill glass with ice. Add a citrus slice and a couple of mint leaves from garnish before filling to brim with ice. Finish with rest of garnish.

---

### Difford's Fruit Cup No.10 (Cachaça based)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A fruit cup is just not as fruity when made with any other spirit – yes cachaça is distilled from fermented sugar cane juice rather than fruit, but in this cocktail it seems to amplify fruity and sweet notes. While it may not go down well at Wimbledon, we’re sure it would be a hit in Rio.

* 1 shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca
* 1 shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* 2 shot Ginger ale
* 2 shot Coca-Cola
* Garnish: Lemon, orange & strawberry slices, mint sprig & borage

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into glass. Half fill glass with ice. Add a citrus slice and a couple of mint leaves from garnish before filling to brim with ice. Finish with rest of garnish.

---

### Difford's Fruit Cup No.13 (Calavdos based)

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** While apple slices are a poor choice of garnish in a fruit cup due to their propensity to turn brown (dehydrated slices are the answer), the crisp dry apple freshness that calvados brings to this fruity long drink makes it one of the best base spirits to opt for.

* 1 shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* 1 shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* 2 shot Ginger ale
* 2 shot Coca-Cola
* Garnish: Lemon, orange & strawberry slices, mint sprig & borage

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into glass. Half fill glass with ice. Add a citrus slice and a couple of mint leaves from garnish before filling to brim with ice. Finish with rest of garnish.

---

### French 75 (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** I’ve Colin Field to thank for my French 75 epiphany. One evening in early June 2017 I was sat at his bar (Bar Hemingway) and he showed me the vintage 75ml gum cartridge he keeps there and pointed out how it is shaped like a tall Collins glass and not a flute. The French 75 was originally served in a tall cartridge shaped glass, and I now agree with Colin – it is a drink that should pack a punch and should be served in a Collins glass. 

So, there you have it, it took a man called Colin to persuade me to use a Collins glass. Incidentally, Colin’s bar lies a 5-minute walk away from where the ‘75’ Cocktail is thought to have been created and he serves a truly superb French 75 in a Collins glass.

* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 2 spoon Powdered sugar (or use 5ml of 2:1 sugar syrup per spoon)
* ½ shot Tanqueray Old Tom gin
* ½ shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* ½ shot Cognac
* ⅙ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* 2 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 3 shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR powdered sugar with lemon juice in base of shaker until sugar dissolves. Add next 5 ingredients (all but champagne), SHAKE with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with champagne and lightly stir. (Consider pouring half the champagne into the glass first to help reduce foaming and eliminate need to stir.)

---

### Old Friend

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Tart, dry and lightly bitter, but with just enough underlying sweetness to stroke the palate and make another sip so very desirable – a complex, bittersweet taste sensation. Brilliant as an aperitif on a hot summer’s evening.

* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Raisin' Cane

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Adapted from a recipe created by Myles Worrell at The Esquire Tavern in San Antonio, USA. Myles’ original recipe called for 2oz Pineau des Charentes rouge, ½oz Paranubes Oaxacan rum, ½oz amontillado sherry and 1 dash Xocolatl Mole bitters.

* 2 shot Pineau des Charentes rouge
* ½ shot Martinique agricole rhum vieux (extra aged)
* ½ shot Amontillado sherry
* 1 dash Xocolatl Mole bitters
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

### Dutch Tea Cocktail

### Grassoide Ferro Cocktail

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** This simple but brilliantly complex aperitif come digestive cocktail dates from the 1930s when it, and most other cocktails were shaken. Don’t allow modern bartending convention to stir such a cocktail detract from its sublimeness.

* ⅔ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Baliva Ferro China quinine liqueur
* 1⅓ shot Martini Bianco Vermouth
* 3 drop Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### The Haiti Cocktail

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** This vintage aperitif is lightly bitter and wonderfully complex with distinctive Ferro China, vermouth and Demerara rum favours.

* ⅔ shot Baliva Ferro China quinine liqueur
* ⅔ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ⅓ shot Martini Riserva Speciale Rubino Vermouth di Torino
* ⅙ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* ⅙ shot Navy rum (54.5% alc./vol.)
* 3 drop Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredient with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Ferrobaldi Cocktail

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** This riff on the classic Garibaldi is a great brunch drink. Why take vitamin c and iron supplement with your breakfast when you can sip on a couple of these.

* 1½ shot Baliva Ferro China quinine liqueur
* 4 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* Garnish: Orange wedge rested across rim

**Instructions:** Squeeze orange juice using pillar or elbow press and fine strain to remove any flesh. Then blend freshly squeezed juice at high speed (without ice) to make “fluffy”. Pour Ferro China and half the fluffy orange juice into glass over 2 cubes of ice and STIR. Fill glass with more ice (3 cubes) and rest of fluffy orange juice.

---

### Fire & Brimstone

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A refreshing riff on a Mezcal Margarita with enlivening chilli heat.

* 2 slice Jalapeño or Fresno chilli pepper (fine sliced)
* 1½ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* ½ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur (infused with Earl Grey tea)
* ⅔ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* ¼ shot AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** MUDDLE chillies in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Banana Calling

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** This short sharp cocktail is best described as a Banana & Fino Sherry Gin Sour. The fino and banana notes are subtle, so subtle that it is not obviously a banana cocktail – although the name should serve as a clue.

* 1⅔ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ⅖ shot Giffard Banane du Brésil crème de banane liqueur
* ⅓ shot Fino sherry
* ⅚ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: None (but perhaps serve with banana chips)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Jerezana Cocktail

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Adapted from a recipe created in 2016 by Rhys Wilson at Happiness Forgets, London, England.

* ⅚ shot Manzanilla Sherry
* ⅚ shot Amontillado sherry
* ⅖ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ⅖ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ⅓ shot Vanilla sugar syrup
* 6 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Iron Negroni

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** Black in colour and with a flavour that’s recognisably part of the Negroni family but with a flat coke-like smoothness that makes a classic Negroni taste harsh in comparison.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Baliva Ferro China quinine liqueur
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Tuxedo No. 2 (Flora Bar's recipe)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Sweet white vermouth and generous maraschino liqueur mellow the usual Tuxedo bone dryness while also adding aroma and flavour.

* 1/12 shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 2¼ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Martini Bianco Vermouth
* ¼ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* 4 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist & Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** RINSE glass with absinthe and discard excess. STIR other ingredients with ice and strain into absinthe rinsed chilled glass.

---

### Tuxedo Cocktail (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Inspired by the numerous other Tuxedo recipes, this combines the best of them all (besides the sherry) but with a faint hint of sweetness (from the bianco vermouth and old tom) to balance generous dashes of absinthe and bitters.

* 1½ shot Tanqueray Old Tom gin
* ¾ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¾ shot Martini Bianco Vermouth
* 1/24 shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* 2 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist & Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Cherry Martinez

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Spirit-led and very slightly sweet, this makes for a delicious late-night tipple.

* 1⅔ shot Luxardo Sour Cherry Gin
* ⅔ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1/12 shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist & Luxardo maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Singapore Sling (Dale DeGroff’s recipe)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Beautifully balanced, fruity and complex with just enough gin to add a spirituous bite.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Cherry Heering cherry brandy liqueur
* ¼ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* ¼ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* 1½ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1/12 shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Pineapple slice and Luxardo maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Fitzgerald (no sugar & low-calorie)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Zingy candied sherbet lemon with hints of botanical complexity and herbal bitters.

This drink is better with the addition of dashes of aromatic bitters but this will add trace amounts of sugar.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Sugar-free sweetener
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters (optional)
* Garnish: Lemon wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Between the Sheets #2 (Wondrich's formula)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Bènèdictine takes the place of rum in this variation on a classic.

* 1 shot Cognac
* ½ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* ½ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (flamed)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Daiquiri No.1 Natural (Difford's 10:3:2 recipe)

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Crisp, light and refreshing. Perfectly balanced complexity of flavours.

* 1⅔ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 2 spoon Powdered sugar (or use 5ml of 2:1 sugar syrup per spoon)
* ⅓ shot Chilled water
* 4 drop Difford's Daiquiri Bitters by Bob's Bitters (optional)
* Garnish: Lime zest twist (discarded) & lime wedge on rim

**Instructions:** Cut zest from your lime prior to squeezing for juice. SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Dry Ice Martini

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Icewine has fabulously rich concentrated flavours due to being made using grapes frozen on the vine in Canada’s harsh and early winters. Thanks to Icewine, despite the name, this Martini is slightly honeyed rather than being bone dry.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¾ shot Canadian icewine
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Dry Martini #1 (Preferred 5:1 ratio)

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** We have chosen a 5:1 ratio as our ‘preferred’ Dry Martini specification in deference to David Embury who writes of this drink in his “The Fine Art of Mixing Drinks, “After extensive experimentation I have arrived at the ratio of 5 to 1 as the proportion most pleasing to the average palate. Personally I like a ratio of about 7 to 1 even better, and I know some who prefer a ratio as high as 10 to 1.”

The proportion of gin to vermouth is a matter of taste; some say 5 to 1, others that one drop is sufficient. I recommend you ask the drinker how they would like their Martini, in the same manner that you might ask how they have their steak.

* 2½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters (optional)
* Garnish: Chilled olive on stick or lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### East India #1

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Wonderfully complex and rounded - a serious drink for serious drinkers.

* 2½ shot Cognac
* ⅛ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* ⅛ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ¼ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Espresso Martini

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Forget the 'Vodka Red Bull', this is the cocktail connoisseur's way of combining caffeine and vodka.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot Espresso coffee (freshly made & hot)
* ⅔ shot Coffee liqueur (optional)
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 pinch Salt
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (discarded) plus float 3 coffee beans on surface

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Fish House Punch #1

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** This fruit laced mix is neither too sweet, nor too strong. It is perfect.

* 1 shot Cognac
* 1 shot Bacardi Carta Oro Superior Gold Rum
* ¾ shot Crème de pêche (peach) liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 shot Chilled water
* Garnish: Lemon slice & dust with grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Franklin Dry Martini

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A Dry Martini named after Franklin Roosevelt and garnished with two olives.

* 2½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* Garnish: Two olives on stick

**Instructions:** STIR vermouth with ice and strain to DISCARD excess, leaving the glass and ice coated with vermouth. POUR gin over vermouth coated ice, STIR and strain into chilled glass.

---

### French 75 Cocktail

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Fresh, clean, sophisticated – dangerously quaffable.

The use of powdered sugar instead of sugar syrup adds an attractive sherbet note to this cocktail. However, the drink also works well with sugar syrup – use ¼oz/7.5ml sugar syrup in place of the 1½ spoons of powdered sugar.

* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 1½ spoon Powdered sugar (or use 5ml of 2:1 sugar syrup per spoon)
* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 2½ shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist on rim

**Instructions:** STIR powdered sugar with lemon juice in base of shaker until sugar dissolves. Add gin, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. TOP with champagne and lightly stir. (Consider pouring half the champagne into the glass first to help reduce foaming.)

---

### Garibaldi

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** A fabulous brunch cocktail.

How you squeeze (and blend) your oranges is key to achieving the "fluffy" orange juice that makes this drink special. At New York City's Dante they famously use a high-speed juicer which aerates the juice. Alternatively, juicing with a pillar or elbow press adds bitter zesty oils from the skin to the juice, hence our use of a smidgen of sugar syrup to balance.

* 1½ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* 1/12 shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 4 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* Garnish: Orange wedge rested across rim

**Instructions:** Squeeze orange juice using pillar or elbow press and fine strain to remove any flesh. Then blend the freshly squeezed juice at high speed (without ice) to make “fluffy”. Pour Campari, sugar syrup and half of the orange juice into glass over 2 cubes of ice and STIR. Fill glass with more ice (3 cubes) and fill with rest of fluffy orange juice.

---

### Gimlet Cocktail (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 5 / 5)

**Comment:** The Gimlet is usually stirred but unless you've super strained/clarified your freshly squeezed citrus juice then even if stirred this cocktail won’t be perfectly clear. So do as Harry Craddock directs in his 1930 Savoy Cocktail Book and use some elbow grease to shake and invigorate this upper decks cocktail.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* ⅙ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅙ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ⅙ shot Rose's lime cordial
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Express 3 lime zests into glass and discard before pouring drink. Lime wedge on rim.

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Grog

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Strong, flavoursome navy rum with a splash of scurvy-inhibiting lime. Properly mixed at the right dilution, this is a great drink. However, too many and you'll be groggy in the morning.

* 2 shot Navy rum (54.5% alc./vol.)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Demerara sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 shot Chilled water
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Honeysuckle Daiquiri

(Rating: 5.0 / 5)

**Comment:** Honey, I love it!

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 4 spoon Runny honey
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* Garnish: Mint leaf

**Instructions:** STIR honey with rum in base of shaker until honey dissolves. Add lemon and orange juice, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Mango slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into glass.

### Japanese Pear

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Originally made with Poire William liqueur, hence this version calls for a little sugar. We've also taken the liberty of adding a dash of Peychaud's Bitters for added complexity and the merest salmon pink tint of colour.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ⅓ shot Poire William eau de vie
* 1½ shot Junmai ginjō sake
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* Garnish: Pear slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Kamaniwanalaya

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Try saying the drinks name after a few of these rum laced, tropical pineapple concoctions.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Disaronno Originale Amaretto liqueur
* ½ shot Navy rum (54.5% alc./vol.)
* ¼ shot White overproof rum
* 3 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1 shot Martini Prosecco D.O.C.
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge & Luxardo Maraschino cherry & mint sprig

**Instructions:** Method; SHAKE first 6 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled (cubed ice) tiki mug (or large Collins glass). Top with crushed ice and then top with prosecco.

---

### Kir Aperitif

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Traditionally made 1/3 cassis to 2/3 wine, that's too sweet for most modern palates. We recommend a ratio of one part cassis to between five and seven parts Bourgogne Aligoté white wine (13.5% to 20% cassis). The above formula is closer to 7:1 and at this concentration the mix of blackcurrant and wine is clean, crisp and not too sweet.

* 2½ shot Bourgogne Aligoté wine white
* ¾ shot Lejay Creme de Cassis de Dijon liqueur (18%)
* 2½ shot Bourgogne Aligoté wine white
* Garnish: None

**Instructions:** POUR half the chilled wine into chilled glass. POUR cassis into glass and TOP with rest of the chilled wine.

---

### Kir Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Canon Félix Kir's traditional white wine and cassis aperitif with added vodka 'oomph'. A barspoon of pisco adds complexity to this cocktail but if available instead use Marc de Bourgogne, the eau-de-vie Canon Kir would have chosen.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ¾ shot Bourgogne Aligoté wine white
* ⅔ shot Lejay Creme de Cassis de Dijon liqueur (18%)
* ⅛ shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco (optional)
* Garnish: Seasonal berries

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

### Maiden's Blush
