---

### Major Bailey #1

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As Victor says of this gin based Julep, "This is a hell of a drink."

* 12 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE (only to bruise) mint with gin in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into glass half filled with crushed ice. CHURN (stir) drink with ice using a barspoon. Top the glass to the brim with more crushed ice and churn again. Serve with straws.

---

### Major Bailey #2

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Made well this is a long, fruity, brilliant frozen Daquiri.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* 1 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** BLEND all ingredients with one 12oz scoop of crushed ice and serve with straws.

---

### Autumn Punch

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Autumnal in colour with a wonderful meld of complementary flavours.

* 1 fresh Passion fruit (fresh fruit)
* 2 shot Bison grass vodka
* ¼ shot Giffard Passion Fruit (Fruit de la Passion) Syrup
* 1 shot Pressed pear juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Top up with Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Physalis (cape gooseberry)

**Instructions:** Cut passion fruit in half and scoop out flesh into shaker. Add vodka, passion fruit syrup, pear and lemon juice, SHAKE with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with champagne.

### Manhattan Island

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A twist on the classic Harvard, or brandy based Manhattan.

* 2 shot Cognac
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 3 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* ⅛ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Margarita Straight-Up (Standard Recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** For the perfect salt rim, liquidise sea salt to make it finer, then run a lime wedge around the outside edge of the glass before dipping the rim in salt. Rimming only half the glass with salt gives the drinker the option of enjoying the cocktail with or without salt.

* 2 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* 1 shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1 spoon AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* 3 drop Bob's Lavender Bitters (optional)
* Garnish: Salt rim & lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Marny Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This appropriately named, simple drink is one of my favourite Grand Marnier cocktails.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* ½ shot Chilled water
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Martini Special

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Aromatic, very dry and very serious - yet has a frothy head.

* ¼ shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 4 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Top up with Chilled water
* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ⅛ shot Orange flower water
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** Fill glass with ice and POUR absinthe and Angostura over ice. TOP with chilled mineral water and leave to stand. SHAKE gin, vermouth and orange water with ice. DISCARD contents of standing glass and fine strain shaken drink into washed glass.

---

### Medium Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A classic Martini served perfect and very wet. I prefer mine shaken which is the method Harry specifies in his guide.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¾ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass

---

### Merry Widow(er)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Gin laced, dry and aromatic with faint herbal and aniseed.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ⅓ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* 1 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 1 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Mexican Martini (Añejo Margarita)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Basically a top-shelf Margarita garnished with Jalapeño stuffed olives.

* 2 shot Patrón Añejo Tequila
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¼ shot AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* Garnish: Jalapeño stuffed olives

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Mexican Mule

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As the name suggests, this is a tequila based version of the Moscow Mule - simple as that. And very tasty.

* 1½ shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Three Cents Ginger Beer
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 3 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with ginger beer, lightly stir and serve with straws.

---

### Mexican Tea (Hot)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Tiffin will never be the same again.

* 2 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Hot English breakfast tea
* Garnish: Lime slice

**Instructions:** Place bar spoon in warmed glass. POUR all ingredients into glass and stir.

---

### Mexico City

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This pinky-red Margarita benefits from a hint of cranberry.

* 1½ shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¾ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Cranberry juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Mexicano (Hot)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A spicy, flavour-packed hot coffee. Lightly whip or simply shake cream in container before pouring over the bowl of a spoon. It also helps if the cream is gently warmed.

* 1 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ½ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* Top up with Filter coffee (hot)
* Float lightly whipped Single cream / half-and-half
* Garnish: Dust with grated nutmeg & cinnamon

**Instructions:** POUR tequila and liqueur into warmed glass and top with coffee. FLOAT cream over drink.

---

### Mint Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A great grassy, minty digestif with a good balance between acidity and sweetness.

* 12 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Sauvignon blanc white wine
* ¼ shot Giffard Menthe Pastille white crème de menthe liqueur
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Mint leaf

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. (There's no need to muddle mint if a good shake and ice is used.)

---

### Mint Daiquiri

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A short, concentrated Mojito.

* 12 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Mint leaf

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE (just to bruise) mint in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Mint Limeade (Non-alcoholic)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Superbly refreshing, mint and lime served long.

* 12 fresh Mint leaves
* 1½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice

* ¾ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Lemon-lime soda
* Garnish: Mint sprigs

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE (just to bruise) mint in base of shaker. Add next three ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with lemonade, lightly stir and serve with straws.

### Orange Mojito

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Mint and orange combine to make a wonderfully fresh drink.

* 8 fresh Mint leaves
* 1½ shot Ketel One Oranje Vodka
* ½ shot Mandarine Napoleon Grande Liqueur Imperiale
* ½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE mint (just to bruise) in base of glass. Add other ingredients and half fill glass with crushed ice. CHURN (stir) with bar spoon. Fill with more crushed ice and churn some more. TOP with soda, stir and serve with straws.

### Park Lane

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This smooth, frothy concoction hides a mean kick.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot De Kuyper Apricot Brandy Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ⅛ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Passion Fruit Caipirinha

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A very tasty fruity Caipirinha.

* ½ fresh Fresh lime (chopped)
* 3 spoon Caster sugar
* 1 fresh Passion fruit (fresh fruit)
* 2 shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca (from freezer)
* Garnish: Stirrer (spoon, wooden lolly stick or stick cut from sugar cane)

**Instructions:** 1. Cut lime in half (from pole to pole) and then slice one of the halves into eight 3-4mm thick half-moon shaped segments and drop into the base of a robust rocks glass.

2. Add 3 bar spoons caster sugar (or ½oz / 15ml sugar syrup 2:1) and MUDDLE.

3. Chop passion fruit in half and scoop flesh into the rocks glass and MUDDLE some more.

4. When sure fruit juice is fully extracted and the sugar dissolved, transfer the muddled fruit and sugar into serving glass (preferably a 30cl / 10oz hi-ball glass).

5. POUR cachaça (stored in the freezer) into the rocks glass (used to muddle) and swirl to rinse glass before pouring cachaça into serving glass. STIR to ensure all ingredients are well mixed.

6. Crack (rather than crush) four to five large ice cubes and drop into serving glass. STIR before topping with more ice and serve with a stirrer (but no straws).

---

### Bajito

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Basically a Mojito with basil as well as mint.

* 6 fresh Mint leaves
* 6 fresh Basil leaves
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE mint and basil in glass just enough to bruise. Add rum, sugar and lime juice. Half fill glass with crushed ice and CHURN (stir) with bar spoon. Add more crushed ice and CHURN some more. Continue adding crushed ice and churning until glass is full.

---

### Pepper & Vanilla

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Vanilla and pepper seem to complement each other in a sweet and sour kind of way.

* 1 shot Absolut Vanilia Vodka
* ¾ shot Pepper-infused Ketel One vodka
* ¾ shot Tuaca Liqueur
* 1 shot Lightly spiced vanilla liqueur
* 1 shot Yellow bell pepper juice
* Garnish: Yellow pepper strip

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Pichuncho Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This drink craves the best pisco and the best sweet vermouth. Find those and measure carefully and it's sublime.

* 2¼ shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* 1½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Pina Colada Cocktail (Puerto Rican style)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A wonderful creamy, fruity concoction that's not half as sticky as the world would have you believe. Too much ice will detract from the creaminess and kill the drink.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Oro Superior Gold Rum
* 3 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ⅔ shot Cream of coconut
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Parasol, pineapple wedge & Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** BLEND all ingredients with 6oz scoop crushed ice and serve with paper straws.

---

### Pineapple Mojito

---

### Pini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Use a great pisco and you'll have a wonderfully complex drink.

* 2 shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* ½ shot Cognac
* ¼ shot Creme de cacao liqueur (white)
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Pink Gin & Tonic

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Basically a G&T with an extra pep of flavour from Angostura, this has a wider appeal than the original Pink Gin.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 3 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Top up with Tonic water
* Garnish: Lime slice

**Instructions:** POUR gin and Angostura bitters into ice-filled glass, TOP with tonic, lightly STIR and serve with straws.

---

### Pink Lady

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Despite the colour, this drink is sharp and alcoholic.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* ¼ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Pink Palace

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A great drink but rarely done justice at the Polo Lounge.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Pisco Punch (Micheli's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This Pisco Punch is very fruity and slightly on the sweet side but is so tasty that it justifies it's legendary reputation.

* 2 slice Fresh orange
* 3 fresh Marinated pineapple wedges
* 2 shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* ¾ shot Pineapple marinade
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge

**Instructions:** MUDDLE orange and pineapple in base of shaker. ADD pisco and pineapple marinade. SHAKE with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with no more than two shots of soda water.

---

### Pisco Sour (Traditional Recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This blended version of a Pisco Sour is wha

* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 6 spoon Powdered sugar
* 2 shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Float three drops of Amargo Chuncho or Angostura aromatic bitters to signify health wealth and happiness.

**Instructions:** BLEND lime and sugar to dissolve sugar. Add pisco, egg white and 6oz scoop crushed ice and BLEND again. Serve with paper straws.

---

### Pisco Sour (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Traditionally this drink is blended with crushed ice, but I (Simon Difford) prefer it served straight-up. Be sure to drink it quickly while it's still cold.

* 2 shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* 1 dash Orange flower water
* Garnish: Float three drops of Amargo Chuncho or Angostura aromatic bitters to signify health wealth and happiness.

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Playmate cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Apricot and orange laced with cognac. Smooth and easy drinking.

* ¾ shot Cognac
* ¾ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* ¾ shot De Kuyper Apricot Brandy Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist and 2 drops of bitter on foamy head (spread with a cocktail stick)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Pomegranate Margarita

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Pomegranate and tequila combine harmoniously in this Margarita.

* 2 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* 1 shot Pomegranate juice
* ¼ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Pooh'tini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Grassy honey with spicy, slightly tannic, camomile finish.

* 2 spoon Runny honey
* 2 shot Bison grass vodka
* 1½ shot Cold camomile tea
* ½ shot Honey liqueur - Spiced
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR honey with vodka in base of shaker to dissolve honey.  Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Pussyfoot (Non-alcoholic)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Probably the best non-alcoholic cocktail ever.

* 7 fresh Mint leaves
* 4 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* 1 fresh Egg yolk
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** MUDDLE mint in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Banana Smoothie (Non-alcoholic)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Serve with breakfast cereal and you'll be set up for the day. The high fresh banana content means this drink will quickly turn brown if left. This can be countered by adding fresh lemon juice and balancing with more honey but this detracts from the fresh banana flavour.

* 7 spoon Natural yoghurt
* 3 spoon Runny honey
* 1 fresh Banana (peeled)
* 3 shot Pressed apple juice
* Garnish: Banana chunk

**Instructions:** BLEND ingredients with 12oz scoop of crushed ice. Pour into glass and serve immediately with straws.

---

### Red Lion Cocktail (modern recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The sophisticated drinker’s answer to a gin and juice with dry gin and Grand Marnier liqueur made all the more fruity with orange juice, lemon juice and pomegranate syrup.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 1/12 shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* 1/12 shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Half rim glass with orange juice and sugar coated rim & orange zest twist (discarded)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Red Marauder

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Slightly sweet and fruity with a hint of raspberry and cognac's distinctive flavour.

* 2 shot Cognac
* ½ shot Black raspberry liqueur
* 1½ shot Cranberry juice
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Raspberries

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Red Rum Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A beautifully fruity, adult balance of bittersweet flavours.

* 24 fresh Redcurrants
* 2 shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* ½ shot Rutte Sloe Gin liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Vanilla sugar syrup
* Garnish: Redcurrants

**Instructions:** MUDDLE redcurrants a base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Reggae Rum Punch

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Jamaicans have a sweet tooth and love their rum. This drink combines sweetness, strength and a generous amount of fruit.

* 1⅔ shot White overproof rum
* 1⅔ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* 1⅔ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ⅚ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge & Luxardo maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Rosita

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A bittersweet, tequila based, Negroni-like drink.

* 1½ shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* 1 shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into ice-filled glass and stir.

---

### Royal Smile

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This balanced sweet and sour cocktail could put a smile on anyone's face. Unless that is, "one is not amused!" Calvados notes shine through.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ⅙ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Rude Cosmopolitan

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Don't let the pink appearance of this Cosmopolitan (made with tequila in place of vodka) fool you into thinking it's a fluffy cocktail. It's both serious and superb.

* 1 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* 1 shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* 1½ shot Cranberry juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters (optional)
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Rum Punch-Up

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Exactly what the name promises - a rum punch served straight-up. Daiquiri style.

* 1½ shot White overproof rum
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* 1 shot Chilled water (reduce if wet ice)
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Russian Spring Punch

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Well-balanced, complex and refreshing.

* 7 fresh Raspberries
* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ¼ shot Lejay Creme de Framboise (raspberry) Liqueur
* ¼ shot Lejay Creme de Cassis de Dijon liqueur (18%)
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Lemon slice & seasonal berries

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 6 ingredients with ice and strain into glass filled with crushed ice. TOP with champagne, lightly stir and serve with straws.

---

### Sakini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Sake creates an almost wine-like delicacy in this approachable riff on the classic Dry Martini.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1½ shot Junmai ginjō sake
* ¼ shot Martini Bianco Vermouth
* Garnish: Green apple peel

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Sangrita

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** In Mexico the quality of the homemade Sangrita can make or break a bar. This recipe is spicey and slightly sweet and perfect for chasing tequila.

* ½ shot Tomato juice
* ½ shot Pomegranate juice
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ⅛ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* 2 drop Hot pepper sauce
* 2 dash Worcestershire sauce
* 1 pinch Salt
* 1 grind Black pepper
* Garnish: None

**Instructions:** SHAKE ingredients with ice and strain into shot glass. Serve with a shot of tequila. The drinker can either down the tequila and chase it with sangrita or sip the two drinks alternately.

---

### Satan's Whiskers (Straight)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A variation on the Bronx. Perfectly balanced tangy orange.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ½ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters (optional)
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Saturn Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Delicate, beautifully balanced and subtly flavoured.

* 7 fresh Seedless white grapes
* 1½ shot Ketel One Citroen Vodka
* 2 spoon Runny honey
* 1½ shot Sauvignon blanc white wine
* Garnish: White grapes

**Instructions:** MUDDLE grapes in base of shaker. STIR honey with vodka and grapes to dissolve honey. Add wine, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

* Garnish: Mint leaf

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Sidecar Cocktail (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Complex and balanced but still a 'sour'. Those with a sweet tooth may prefer with a sugar rim. Also consider trying what has become something of a standard modern recipe:
1 2/3oz / 50ml) Cognac
1oz / 30ml Triple sec
2/3oz 20ml Lemon juice

* 1½ shot Cognac
* 1 shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Pineau des Charentes blanc
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (some like with a sugared rim)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Basil Bramble Sling

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Wonderfully refreshing and balanced.

* 7 fresh Basil leaves
* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Lejay Creme de Mure (Blackberry) Liqueur
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** MUDDLE basil in base of shaker. Add rest of ingredients, SHAKE with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. Serve with straws.

---

### Sloe Gin Fizz

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** With the right brand of sloe gin and champagne, this citrusy berry cocktail is just on the dry/tart side of balanced (add more sugar or choose your sloe gin according to taste). Obviously when made with soda rather than champagne this is a very different but still tasty cocktail.

We have David Wondrich to thank for uncovering this quote about the Sloe Gin Fizz by Lawton Mackall in the August 1941 issue of Esquire, "Its haunting pink color and fruity opulence are topped with a handsome collar of natural foam which, if the sloe gin be of first quality, is gladsome aplenty." It’s true, there’s no need to add egg white, and its addition detracts from this cocktail.

* 1½ shot Rutte Sloe Gin liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 1 spoon Powdered sugar (or use 5ml of 2:1 sugar syrup per spoon)
* 4 shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Lemon slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 4 ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass (without ice). TOP with champagne (or soda if you’re cheap). Some like to add egg white to enhance foam. (The drink photographed here is without egg white and we prefer without.)

---

### Slow Screw

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Reminiscent of a fruity screwdriver with botanical gin character. When made with a good slow gin and freshly squeezed orange juice this is a great brunch cocktail.

* 1½ shot Rutte Sloe Gin liqueur
* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 3½ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Sodden Grape

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A 'sod' is a piece of turf. Here 'sodden' refers to the Bison grass, the flavour of which combines well with the grapes and icewine.

* 7 fresh Seedless white grapes
* 2 shot Bison grass vodka
* ¾ shot Canadian icewine
* Garnish: White grapes

**Instructions:** MUDDLE grapes in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Sorrel Rum Punch

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This drink harnesses the flavour of sorrelade and combines it with the traditional strength and bitter sweetness of rum punch. Jamaica in a glass.

* 2¼ shot White overproof rum
* 3 shot Sorrelade (see sorrelade recipe)
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into glass filled with crushed ice. Serve with straws.

---

### Sour Apple Martini / Appletini (Deluxe U.S. version)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A sophisticated version of a contemporary classic.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot Sour apple liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white (optional)
* Garnish: Apple slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Adonis

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Delicate, off-dry and aromatic. A great aperitif cocktail.

* 2 shot Fino sherry
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### 75 Cocktail (MacElhone's 1926 recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Like the gun this cocktail is named after, this small drink that packs a hell of a punch, and to ensure it does, MacElhone calls for a couple of dashes of absinthe in place of the lemon juice used in earlier Soixante-Quinze (Seventy-Five) recipes. The result being a dry spirituous drink.

* 1⅓ shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* ⅔ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ⅙ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* 2 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (discarded) & star anise

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Sgroppino / Sorbetto

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Smooth and all too easy to quaff. A great dessert.

* ½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ¼ shot Single cream / half-and-half
* 1½ shot Martini Prosecco D.O.C.
* 2 scoop Lemon sorbet
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** BLEND all ingredients without additional ice and serve in chilled glass.

---

### Slow Comfortable Screw Against The Wall

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Galliano adds the wall (as in Harvey Wallbanger) and some herbal peppermint to this Slow Comfortable Screw. Yes, the name’s corny but made with fresh orange, this drink is a good brunch or summertime option.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Southern Comfort Liqueur
* 3 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ½ shot Rutte Sloe Gin liqueur
* ½ shot Galliano L'Autentico liqueur
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** STIR first 3 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. FLOAT sloe gin on surface so it bleeds into drink. Finish with Galliano FLOAT.

---

### Snowfall Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** An alcoholic version of a vanilla milkshake with tiny black specs from the vanilla.

* ¼ whole Vanilla pod
* 1½ shot Absolut Vanilia Vodka
* 1½ shot Single cream / half-and-half
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Vanilla pod

**Instructions:** Take 1/4 a vanilla pod and cut along its length. MUDDLE this in the base of a shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Southern Tea

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Sweet fruity flavours balanced by tannic bitterness in the tea.

* ½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot De Kuyper Apricot Brandy Liqueur
* ½ shot Giffard Banane du Brésil crème de banane liqueur
* 1 shot Southern Comfort Liqueur
* 2 shot Cold Earl Grey tea
* Garnish: Apricot slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Stairs Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** In London's cockney rhyming slang 'apples and pears' means stairs. Thus this tasty cocktail is appropriately named.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot Pressed pear juice
* 1 shot Pressed apple juice
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Pear slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

* 1 shot Cognac
* 1 shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* 1 shot Single cream / half-and-half
* Garnish: Dust with grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Sunshine Cocktail #1

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Light, fruity and a tad on the sweet side, but could well brighten up your day.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Swizzles Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Somewhat reminiscent of a frozen gimlet – the combination of gin and lime shines in this freshening swizzle.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ⅔ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Crown with few dashes Angostura bitters on drinks ice peak, plus juniper berries

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into chilled glass and two-thirds fill with crushed ice. SWIZZLE with a swizzle stick (or churn with a barspoon). Add more crushed ice to fill and SWIZZLE some more. Serve with straws.

---

### Tatanka

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The taste of this excellent drink (which is equally good served straight-up) is a little reminiscent of Earl Grey tea.

* 2 shot Bison grass vodka
* 2½ shot Pressed apple juice
* ⅙ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Apple slice & or lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Bebbo Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Fresh, clean and fruity with honeyed notes. Choose your honey wisely.

* 2 spoon Runny honey
* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Blood orange juice
* ¼ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR honey with gin in base of shaker until honey dissolves. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Tequila Smash

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

* 7 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¼ shot AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

### Tequila Sour

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A standard sour but with tequila zing.

* 2 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Tequila Sunrise

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Well-balanced tequila and zesty citrus with a sweet treat at the bottom.

* ⅙ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* ⅙ shot Lejay Creme de Cassis de Dijon liqueur (18%)
* 1½ shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¾ shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 2½ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* Garnish: Lime wheel

**Instructions:** POUR grenadine and cassis into ice-filled glass. SHAKE other ingredients and carefully strain into glass to sit on red base layer (to create a sunrise effect).

---

### Ti Punch

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This drink only works when made with authentic rhum agricole and pressed sugar cane juice cane boiled down to make thick and syrupy or demerara sugar syrup (rather than sugar syrup made from refined sugar). Rhum Agricole is a style of rum distilled from fermented cane juice, in contrast to most other styles of rum which are made from fermented molasses. 

As the name suggests – this drink is punchy – the rhum agricole tends to be 50% alc./vol. and even if you choose to add ice then dilution is negligible. However, the all-important sugar cane juice adds flavour and smooths the rum, so yes, its punchy but it’s also very pleasing to drink.

Ti’Punch varies tremendously depending on who is making it, but there are four key elements that make a Ti’Punch a real Ti’Punch – best remembered by 5 x S’s as follows:

Swizzle - the ingredients are mixed in the glass in which the drink will be served using a swizzle stick. Such swizzle sticks tend to be used to mix long drinks with crushed ice, but the Ti’Punch is a very short drink often served without ice. The use of a swizzle stick is simply a quick way of ensuring sugar rum and lime are properly mixed in the base of the glass. A Ti’Punch should never be shaken, blended or even stirred in a mixing glass.
  
Short - Ti’Punch is a very short drink with a liquid volume of less than 2oz /60ml. While a Ti’Punch is basically the size of a shot and often served without ice, it should never be served in a shot glass. The perfect Ti’Punch glass is a very small tumbler with a brim slightly larger than the base so allowing the drinker to appreciate the fragrant aromatics.

Simple - the Ti’Punch is an incredibly simple drink – classically with just three ingredients.

Self - in the Caribbean it is common for bars to serve a Ti’Punch as a shot of rum in a glass with discs of lime and sugar on the side so the drinker can combine exactly to their own tastes. In Martinique they say, “Chacun prépare sa propre mort”, which translates as “prepare your own death”.

Spoon - due to the above, it is also common for Ti’Punch to be served with a small spoon.

Sunrise/Sunset - on the French islands of the Caribbean, a Ti’Punch is often served for breakfast in a similar manor to grappa and espresso in Italy. The Ti’Punch is also served with lunch and dinner – indeed from sunrise to sunset. It’s usual to use rhum blanc (unaged white agricole rum) during the day and rhum vieux (aged agricole rum) during the evening.

* 1½ shot Clément Canne Bleue 2016 Martinique Rhum blanc Agricole
* ¼ shot Clément Sirop Sucre de Canne (sugar cane juice syrup)
* 1 slice Fresh lime
* Garnish: The lime disc in the drink is garnish enough but consider expressing a lime zest twist over the drink and then discarding.

**Instructions:** Traditionally the limes used to make this drink are not cut into slices or wedges. Instead a round disc is cut from the side of the fruit. These are cut large enough that some of the fruits pulp backs the peel on the disc.

POUR the rum and sugar into glass. Then SQUEEZE the lime disc between finger and thumb before dropping into the drink. This expresses the oil from the skin and little of the juice into the Ti’Punch. Lastly SWIZZLE (stir) and consider adding ice - either one of two large cubes depending on glass size or preferably a small chunk of block ice.

---

### Tiki Max

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This drink breaks the golden rule - simple is beautiful. However, it's tasty and packs a punch.

* 1 shot Navy rum (54.5% alc./vol.)

* ½ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* ½ shot De Kuyper Apricot Brandy Liqueur
* ¾ shot Giffard Sirop de Orgeat (Almond) Syrup
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1½ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* 6 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* ½ shot Wood's 100 rum
* Garnish: Mint sprig & lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE first nine ingredients with ice and strain into glass filled with crushed ice. FLOAT overproof rum on drink.

### Tom & Jerry

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A warming and filling winters meal in itself. This recipe will fill six small toddy glasses or Tom & Jerry mugs (each 20cl capacity to brim), and given the faff involved you might as well double or treble the recipe and make for a crowd, or enjoy several each.

* 2 fresh Egg white
* 2 fresh Egg yolk
* 6 spoon Caster sugar
* ½ shot Smith & Cross Traditional Pot Still Jamaican Rum
* 2 pinch Ground cinnamon
* 2 pinch Clove
* 3 pinch Freshly grated nutmeg
* 1½ shot Cognac
* ½ shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* Top up with Boiling water
* Garnish: Dust with freshly grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** 1. Pre-warm six 20cl (6.75oz) toddy glasses or Tom & Jerry mugs with hot water.
2. Using a whisk, BEAT the yolks in a mixing bowl “until they are thin as water." Add sugar, Jamaican rum, spices and STIR thoroughly with whisk.
3. In a separate bowl, use a whisk to BEAT the egg whites "to a stiff froth."
4. Use a tablespoon to FOLD the frothy egg whites into the spiced and beaten yolk mixture. This produces the gloopy base mixture known as ‘Tom & Jerry batter’.
5. To make individual drinks, to each of the warmed glasses or mugs, POUR cognac and rum, and add two table spoons of Tom & Jerry batter. STIR each glass/mug thoroughly with a barspoon while topping with boiling water.
6. Each should end up with frothy head ready to receive the garnish of grated nutmeg. Serve and enjoy.

---

### Tom Collins

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A medium-dry Gin Collins.

* 2 shot Tanqueray Old Tom gin
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Orange slice & cherry on stick (sail)

**Instructions:** SHAKE first three ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with soda, lightly stir and serve with straws.

### Treacle No.1

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Richly flavoured, almost like molasses.

* 2 shot Smith & Cross Traditional Pot Still Jamaican Rum
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pressed apple juice
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR half of the rum, sugar syrup and bitters with two ice cubes in glass. Add rest of rum, another couple of ice cubes and STIR again. Fill glass with ice and STIR again. Finally FLOAT apple juice.

### Toblerone Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Nibble at the garnish as you sip honeyed, chocolate and almond flavoured liquid candy. Yumm.

* 2 spoon Runny honey
* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%) (infused with vanilla)
* ½ shot Disaronno Originale Amaretto liqueur
* ¾ shot Gabriel Boudier Dark Creme de Cacao Liqueur
* ½ shot Single cream / half-and-half
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Dust surface of drink with dark chocolate powder and place two segments of Toblerone chocolate on rim

**Instructions:** STIR honey with vodka in base of shaker until honey dissolves. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and strain into chilled glass.

### Tropic

---

### Tropical Caipirinha

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** In drink circles, tropical usually spells sweet. This drink has a tropical flavour but a definite adult sourness.

* ½ fresh Fresh lime (chopped)
* 3 spoon Caster sugar
* 1½ shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca (from freezer)
* ½ shot Coconut rum liqueur
* ¾ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* Garnish: Stirrer (spoon, wooden lolly stick or stick cut from sugar cane)

**Instructions:** 1. Cut lime in half (from pole to pole) and then slice one of the halves into eight 3-4mm thick half-moon shaped segments and drop into the base of a robust rocks glass.

2. Add 3 bar spoons caster sugar (or ½oz/15ml sugar syrup 2:1) and MUDDLE.

3. When sure fruit juice is fully extracted and the sugar dissolved, transfer the muddled fruit and sugar into serving glass (preferably a 30cl / 10oz hi-ball glass).

4 POUR cachaça (stored in the freezer), coconut liqueur and pineapple juice (also chilled) into the shaker base or glass used to muddle and swirl to rinse before pouring into serving glass. STIR to ensure all ingredients are well mixed.

5. Crack (rather than crush) four to five large ice cubes and drop into serving glass. STIR before topping with more ice and serve with a stirrer (but no straws).

---

### Tuxedo Cocktail Original

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** We’ve tried this recipe with 2 to 3 dashes of Angostura and also orange bitters, but we prefer it with 2 dashes of both Angostura and orange bitters, so honouring Johnson, McElhone, Mahoney and Grohusko. The result is a very aromatic semi-Dry Martini.

* 1½ shot Tanqueray Old Tom gin
* 1½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 1 dash Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* 1 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist & Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Berry Caipirinha

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A fruity version of the popular Brazilian drink.

* ½ fresh Fresh lime (chopped)
* 3 spoon Caster sugar
* 3 fresh Raspberries
* 2 fresh Blackberries
* 3 fresh Blueberries
* 1 fresh Small ripe strawberries (hulled)
* 2 shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca (from freezer)
* Garnish: Stirrer (spoon, wooden lolly stick or stick cut from sugar cane)

**Instructions:** 1. Cut lime in half (from pole to pole) and then slice one of the halves into eight 3-4mm thick half-moon shaped segments and drop into the base of a robust rocks glass.

2. Add 3 bar spoons caster sugar (or ½oz / 15ml sugar syrup 2:1) and MUDDLE.

3. Add mixed berries and MUDDLE some more.

4. When sure fruit juice is fully extracted and the sugar dissolved, transfer the muddled fruit and sugar into serving glass (preferably a 30cl / 10oz hi-ball glass).

5. POUR cachaça (stored in the freezer) into the rocks glass (used to muddle) and swirl to rinse glass before pouring cachaça into serving glass. STIR to ensure all ingredients are well mixed.

6. Crack (rather than crush) four to five large ice cubes and drop into serving glass. STIR before topping with more ice and serve with a stirrer (but no straws).

---

### Between the Sheets #1 (Difford's formula)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Classic proportions to this drink are most often quoted as being: 1 rum, 1 cognac, 1 triple sec and 1/4 lemon juice but three shots of 40% alcohol and a splash of lemon juice make for a tart drink which should not be undertaken lightly. The formula above maintains the essential flavour and ingredients of the classic recipe but is a little more approachable.

* ¾ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ¾ shot Cognac
* ¾ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅛ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### White Lady Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A simple but lovely classic drink with a sour finish.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white (optional)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into the same shaker to remove the ice. SHAKE again without ice (dry shake) and then strain into chilled glass.

### Wibble

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As Dick Bradsell once said to me, "It may make you wobble, but it won't make you fall down." Dick named this cocktail after the 1970s' Weebles children's roly-poly toys which were advertised with the catchphrase, "Weebles wobble, but they don't fall down."

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Rutte Sloe Gin liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ⅓ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅓ shot Lejay Creme de Mure (Blackberry) Liqueur
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Wink

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Reminiscent of a Sazerac but with gin and triple sec. Delicate, remarkably fruity and very sippable.

* ½ shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¼ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ⅛ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (discarded)

**Instructions:** POUR absinthe into ice-filled glass. TOP with chilled water and set to one side. Separately, SHAKE other ingredients with ice. DISCARD contents of glass (absinthe, water and ice) and strain drink into empty absinthe-coated glass.

### Gin Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Bready genever with a hint of orange curacao adding flavour and the merest touch of sweetness balancing Boker’s Bitters. If you don’t have Boker’s to hand try with Peychaud’s Bitters – produces a different drink but works well, I’d go as far as to suggest better. Peychaud’s also produces a cocktail with an attractive pale shade of salmon pink – if you like that kind of thing.

* 2 shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* ⅓ shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* ⅛ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Dr. Adam Elmegirab's Boker's Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Gin Punch  #1

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Light and refreshing, akin to alcoholic real lemonade.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¾ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 shot Chilled water
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and stain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Larchmont

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** I share Embury's appreciation of this fine, delicate Orange Daiquiri. However, we've tweaked his formulation as we found the original somewhat rich and over citrusy.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Mint & Honey Daiquiri

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A fresh-breath-tastic twist on the classic Daiquiri.

* 2 spoon Runny honey
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 3 fresh Mint leaves
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** STIR honey and rum in base of shaker until honey dissolves. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### TNT (Tequila 'N' Tonic)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A simple but very tasty way to enjoy tequila.

* 1½ shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Top up with Tonic water
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into ice-filled glass and STIR.

---

### Amber Room #2

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A subtle, delicately floral Martini.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth (originally Ambre)
* ¼ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Amber Room  #1

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Serious and packed with bold flavours. Fellow Chartreuse fans will approve.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (discarded) & Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Black Bison Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A fragrant cocktail with a dry finish. As the name suggests, also works well with Zubrowka Bison vodka in place of gin.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Berentzen Apfel Korn (apple schnapps) liqueur
* 1½ shot Pressed apple juice
* ¼ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* Garnish: Apple wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Batida Rosa

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Fruity and tropical. A tall refreshing drink for a hot evening or an afternoon beside the pool.

* 2 shot Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* 2 shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca
* 1 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¾ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge

**Instructions:** POUR soda water into ice-filled glass. SHAKE other ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled and soda charged glass.

---

### Biggles Aviation

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A ginger influenced Aviation named after the fictional book Biggles in Borneo about WWII flying heroes Ginger, Algy and Biggles. Inspired  by the ginger used in Canton ginger liqueur being sourced from Borneo.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot King's Ginger Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ¼ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Fresh ginger & lime wheels

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Biggles Sidecar

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The idea was to make a riff on an Aviation (see Biggles Aviation) but ginger cries out for cognac so we also ended up with this ginger Sidecar.

* 2 shot Cognac
* ½ shot King's Ginger Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Fresh ginger & lemon slices

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Blood Sage

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Sage combines wonderfully with gin and orange in this beautifully balanced drink.

* ½ shot Blood orange juice
* 2 fresh Sage leaves
* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Sage leaf

**Instructions:** MUDDLE orange and sage in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Bloody Bronx Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A Bronx made 'bloody' by the use of blood oranges. Fruity yet dry with botanical notes both from the vermouth and the gin.

* 1¾ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ¼ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 1 shot Blood orange juice
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Brandy Daisy

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Yellow Chartreuse notes show through strongly in this short refreshing drink, with cognac providing the base flavour and lemon juice contributing freshening citrus balance.

* 1½ shot Cognac
* ⅔ shot Chartreuse Jaune (Yellow Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 shot Soda (club soda) or sparkling water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Seasonal berries & mint sprig

**Instructions:** STIR first 4 ingredients with ice and strain into glass filled with crushed ice. TOP with a splash of soda and briefly stir.

---

### Black Diamond

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This flavoursome mix of coffee and chocolate is further enhanced if vanilla-infused rum is used.

* 1¼ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1¼ shot Gabriel Boudier Dark Creme de Cacao Liqueur
* 1¼ shot Espresso coffee (freshly made & hot)
* Garnish: Dust with grated white chocolate

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Chartreuse Swizzle

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A swizzle for people like me - Chartreuse lovers. Best enjoyed on a hot summer’s evening.

* 1¼ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ½ shot John D. Taylor's Velvet Falernum Liqueur
* 2 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge & Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into chilled glass and two-thirds fill with crushed ice. SWIZZLE with a swizzle stick (or churn with a barspoon). Add more crushed ice to fill and SWIZZLE some more. Serve with straws.

---

### Clara Astié Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Tangy apricot with hints of maraschino dried by vermouth and fortified by light rum.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 spoon Apricot jam (preserve)
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ⅛ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* 1 dash Bittermens Hopped Grapefruit Bitters
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist (discarded) & dried apricot

**Instructions:** STIR jam with rum until jam dissolves. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Clover Club Cocktail No.3 (Lowe's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Balanced and complex with a fruity blast of raspberry - made interesting due to its inclusion of vermouth.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¾ shot Raspberry (framboise) sugar syrup
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Float raspberry in centre of drink

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Clover Club Cocktail No.3 (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Easy drinking and creamy in texture – with notes of raspberry, gin, citrus and delicate spice.

* 5 fresh Raspberries
* 1¾ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¼ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¼ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (sprayed & discarded)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Coffee Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As the anonymous writer of the 1887 edition of the Professor's book comments, "The name of this drink is a misnomer, as coffee and bitters are not to be found among its ingredients, but it looks like coffee when it has been properly concocted."

* 2 shot Warre's Otima 10 Year Old Tawny Port
* 1 shot Cognac
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 fresh Egg (white & yolk)
* Garnish: Dust with freshly grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Corpse Reviver No.1 (Gilberg's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Boozy, complex and delicious with attractive apple notes and faint anise absinthe influences.

* 1 shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* 1 shot Cognac
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Corpse Reviver Cocktail No.2 (Contemporary Recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Yellow Chartreuse replaces triple sec in this riff on the classic Corpse Reviver Cocktail No.2.

* ¾ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Chartreuse Jaune (Yellow Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ¾ shot Lillet Blanc French aperitif wine
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 1 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Cornwall Negroni

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A Negroni style cocktail served up. Heavy on the gin and relatively light on Campari and vermouth. It's a formula that works but like us, you may prefer yours served on the rocks.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* ½ shot Punt E Mes vermouth
* ½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (flamed)

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ¼ shot Galliano L'Autentico liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)

* ¼ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Daiquiri Noir

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Discovered in 2008 at Hugos Bar Pizza, Sydney, Australia.

* 7 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* ½ shot Drambuie liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE mint in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### La Dolce Vita

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Complex, yet easy to quaff, with a touch of fizz adding some sparkle.

* 4 fresh Seedless white grapes
* 1 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 spoon Runny honey
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Top up with Martini Prosecco D.O.C.
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** MUDDLE grapes in base of shaker. Add vodka, honey and bitters, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. TOP with prosecco.

---

### Don Daisy

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This zesty, silky smooth and easy drink is laced with light rum.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Eighteen '97

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Looks great and, with the citrus freshness of kumquat combined with the oily character of grappa, it also tastes great.

* 5 fresh Kumquats (chopped)
* 1½ shot Bepi Tosolini Grappa di Moscato
* 1¼ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ¼ shot Merlot red wine
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (discarded) & white grapes

**Instructions:** MUDDLE kumquats in base of shaker. Add next three ingredients, shake and fine strain into a chilled glass. FLOAT wine.

---

* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

### Flipping Good

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Simply an aged rum flip with falernum replacing sugar syrup and egg white omitted.

* 2 shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* 1 shot John D. Taylor's Velvet Falernum Liqueur
* 1 fresh Egg yolk
* Garnish: Dust with grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Four Leaf Clover

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Originally based on vodka but seemed a shame not to try it as a Daiquiri.

* 1 dried Clove
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Pressed apple juice
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Honey syrup
* Garnish: Physalis (cape gooseberry)

**Instructions:** MUDDLE clove in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Bling! Bling!

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** An ostentatious little number.

* 7 fresh Raspberries
* ½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Brut Champagne
* Garnish: None

**Instructions:** MUDDLE raspberries in base of shaker. Add vodka, lime and sugar, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into glass. TOP with champagne.

---

### Hoyt's Daiquirí

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Most unusual and interesting. Recognisably a Daiquiri but with creamy mouth-feel and great depth of flavour.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Burnt lime juice
* ¼ shot Jägermeister Liqueur
* ½ shot Vanilla sugar syrup
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Lime slice (seared)

**Instructions:** Sear two halves of lime with a chef's blow torch and squeeze into a shaker. SHAKE all remaining ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Jalisco Flower

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Subtle, fruity and one of my favourite champagne cocktails.

* ½ shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¾ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed ruby grapefruit juice
* Top up with Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE first three ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. TOP with champagne. Lightly stir and serve.

---

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 1 shot Blood orange juice
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Kangaroo Dry Martini

**Comment:** Temperature is key to the enjoyment of this modern classic. Consume while icy cold.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

### Love Unit

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Delicate, complex and balanced with enough fruit and veg to make your five-a-day.

* 2 slice Red bell pepper
* 7 fresh Basil leaves (thai)
* 1 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%) (infused with vanilla)
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Basil leaf & bell pepper

**Instructions:** MUDDLE pepper in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Metropole

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** I've slightly tweaked this recipe from the original as it cried out for sweetness but it remains a dry cognac Manhattan.

* 2 shot Cognac
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 2 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Lillet Blanc French aperitif wine

* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

### Bloody Mary (Modern Recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The classic brunch cocktail.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 4 shot Tomato juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 8 drop Hot pepper sauce
* 4 dash Worcestershire sauce
* 2 grind Black pepper
* 1 pinch Celery salt
* Garnish: Celery stick (optional salt & pepper rim)

**Instructions:** ROLL rather than shake all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. (Use double frozen ice freshly from freezer to fill glass.)

---

### Moonlight Cocktail (Gaz Regan's)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Basically an Aviation but with triple sec in place of maraschino and lime instead of lemon juice. Gaz used lime juice because he didn’t have any lemons but in this adaptation of his recipe I’ve mellowed the citrus sourness by using a combination of both lime and lemon juice.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ½ shot Créme de violette liqueur
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Myrtle Bank Special Rum Punch

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A rich fruity Daiquiri with tangy molasses.

* 2 shot Smith & Cross Traditional Pot Still Jamaican Rum
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ⅛ shot Cherry Heering cherry brandy liqueur
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Oooh Ginger

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Subtle ginger spice flavours this dry tequila martini-esque cocktail.

* 2 shot Patrón Añejo Tequila
* ⅔ shot King's Ginger Liqueur
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* Garnish: Candied ginger

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Old Cuban

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A luxurious, minty Daiquiri topped with a splash of champagne.

* 6 fresh Mint leaves
* 1½ shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ⅔ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* ¾ shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Mint leaf

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE mint in base of shaker (just to bruise). Add next four ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. TOP with champagne.

---

### Orchard Crush

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Apple brandy and damson jam combine brilliantly in this tangy but not at all sweet cocktail.

* 1 spoon Damson jam (preserve)
* 2 shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Seasonal berries

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into an ice-filled glass.

---

### Original Sin

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Sake and vodka with a delicate hint of honey.

* ½ shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* ¾ shot Junmai ginjō sake
* ⅙ shot Honey syrup
* Garnish: Star anise

**Instructions:** POUR absinthe into ice-filled glass and top with water. Leave the mixture to stand in the glass. Separately, STIR all ingredients with ice. Finally discard contents of absinthe-coated glass and fine strain contents of shaker into absinthe washed glass.

---

### Papa Bear

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Delicately spiced and honeyed cognac.

* 1 spoon Honey syrup
* 1½ shot Cognac
* 1½ shot Honey liqueur - Spiced
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Garnish: Honeycomb rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Perfect Lady

### Ranglum

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Estery rum notes predominate with zesty lime and faint sweet clove spice. A Tiki-style drink for a full-on sunny afternoon or to lift a dull winter’s day.

* 1½ shot Goslings Black Seal Rum
* ⅓ shot White overproof rum
* ⅓ shot John D. Taylor's Velvet Falernum Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Sake Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Dry, subtle, and depending on your choice of sake, possibly amazing.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 2 shot Junmai ginjō sake
* ⅛ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* Garnish: Apple slice

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and fine stain into chilled glass.

---

### Sherry Sour

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The huge flavour of sherry is freshened by lemon juice and rounded by egg white.

* 2 shot Palo cortado sherry
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Sol Ardiente

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Red pepper and pineapple influences this twisted Daiquiri.

* 1 spoon Pink peppercorns
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Crushed red peppercorns

**Instructions:** MUDDLE peppercorns in base of shaker. Add next four ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. TOP with splash soda.

---

### Tenner Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Very wet, aromatic Martini.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 2 dash Bittermens Hopped Grapefruit Bitters
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Valencia Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A Martini-style drink but using fino sherry instead of vermouth. Crisp and dry.

* 2½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Fino sherry
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### White Cargo

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A delicious dessert-style drink.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 scoop Vanilla ice-cream
* ¼ shot Chardonnay (Chablis) white wine
* Garnish: Dust with grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Will Of Alan

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Fantastic, spiced, tiki-style twisted Daiquiri.

* 2 shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* ½ shot John D. Taylor's Velvet Falernum Liqueur
* ¾ shot Pineapple (fresh)
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 2 dash Old-fashioned bitters
* ¼ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** DRY SHAKE all ingredients without ice. Add ice, SHAKE again and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Corpse Reviver No.2 (Duffy's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Perhaps a touch sweet but the kill or cure alcohol is well masked.

* ¾ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Carlshamns Flaggpunsch Original Swedish Punsch
* ¾ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* 1 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Daisy Cutter Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Floral, minty and herbal with a dry finish.

* 3 fresh Mint leaves
* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¼ shot Chartreuse Jaune (Yellow Chartreuse) Liqueur
* Garnish: Mint leaf

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE mint in base of shaker (just to bruise). Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Diki-Diki

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Fruity yet tart. The sourness is a challenge initially but very rewarding.

* 2 shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* ½ shot Carlshamns Flaggpunsch Original Swedish Punsch
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* Garnish: Sugar rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

* 2 shot Carlshamns Flaggpunsch Original Swedish Punsch
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Elder Aviator

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin

* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Elder Sour

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** So smooth it's almost fluffy. A great after-dinner drink.

* 2 shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters (optional)
* Garnish: Lemon slice & cherry on stick (sail)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Elderflower Cosmo

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Despite the absence of citrus vodka, orange liqueur and cranberry, this delicate blend is still Cosmopolitan-esque in style.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* ½ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Elderflower Martini #2

* 1 shot Bison grass vodka

---

### Elderflower Mojito

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The enduring classic benefits from a touch of elderflower.

* 12 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE (just to bruise) mint in base of glass. Add other ingredients, half fill glass with crushed ice and CHURN (stir) with bar spoon. Fill glass to brim with more crushed ice and churn some more. Serve with straws.

---

### English Breakfast Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Light and fragrant with black tea, elderflower and the botanical influence of gin.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly brewed cold black English breakfast tea
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### English Channel

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

* ¾ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* ¾ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* 2 shot Cold Earl Grey tea
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Fallen Leaves

* 1½ shot Berneroy Fine Calvados

* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur

* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Gun Club Punch No.1

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This Trader Vic classic is balanced rather than sweet. Fruit juice and ice tone down rum's powerful blast.

* 1 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Navy rum (54.5% alc./vol.)
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1½ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ¼ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¼ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge, Luxardo Maraschino cherry & mint sprig

**Instructions:** BLEND all ingredients with 12oz scoop crushed ice. Serve with straws.

---

### Mojito Parisien

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Those with a sweet tooth may want to add a dash of sugar syrup to taste.

* 12 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1½ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE mint (just to bruise) in base of glass. Add other ingredients, half fill glass with crushed ice and CHURN (stir) with bar spoon. Fill glass to brim with more crushed ice and churn some more. Serve with straws.

---

### Mother Rum

* ¼ shot Maple syrup
* Garnish: Cinnamon stick

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.
