### Pegu Club Cocktail (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Citrusy and refreshing with the gin base providing backbone. Rich zesty orange curacao is accentuated by tart lime.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ⅔ shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* ⅓ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1/12 shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Peruvian Elder Sour

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This tasty sour combines the aromatics of pisco and elderflower in an intriguing variation on the Margarita. Consider smoothing with fresh egg white.

* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1 shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* 2 shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Peto Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** An aromatic classic Martini served 'perfect' with a hint of orange juice and maraschino.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth

* ⅛ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Pomme et Sureau

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Light, long and refreshing apple and elderflower.

* 1 shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* 2 shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Apple wedge

**Instructions:** POUR first 2 ingredients into ice-filled glass, TOP with soda and lightly stir.

---

### Queen's Park Swizzle

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This close relation to the Mojito is drier, more complex and less minty than its sibling.

* 8 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Oro Superior Gold Rum
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Demerara sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lime wedge & mint sprig

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE mint (just to bruise) in base of glass. Use your barspoon to raise the bruised mint up and around the inside of the glass so as to coat with fragrant mint oils. Add other ingredients and two-thirds fill glass with crushed ice. SWIZZLE with a swizzle stick or CHURN (stir) with a bar spoon. Fill glass with more crushed ice and repeat. Serve with straws.

---

### St-Germain Cocktail (Elderflower Spritz)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A long, easy drinking summer cooler.

* 2 shot Sauvignon blanc white wine
* 1½ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Lime slice

**Instructions:** POUR wine and then elderflower liqueur into ice-filled glass. TOP with soda (or champagne), lightly stir and serve with straws.

---

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

* 1½ shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila

* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Lime wedge & salt rim (optional)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Wisecrack Fizz

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Light, balanced and refreshing. The pisco character shines through.

* 1½ shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* 1 shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE first four ingredients with ice and strain into an ice-filled glass. TOP with soda and serve with straws.

---

### Four Aces

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A summery, light, superbly balanced herbal fruit cocktail.

* 6 fresh Seedless white grapes
* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot King's Ginger Liqueur
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 4 fresh Basil leaves (torn)
* Garnish: Basil leaf

**Instructions:** MUDDLE grapes in base of shaker. Add next 5 ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with soda water, stir and serve with straws.

---

### Greyhound's Tooth

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Fresh grapefruit flavours form the backbone of this summer-fresh cocktail.

* ¾ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 2 dash Bittermens Hopped Grapefruit Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

### Buckeye

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A standard Dry Martini - but a Buckeye is always garnished with a black olive instead of a green one.

---

### Mantini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A gin martini-style drink made with beer in place of vermouth. A suitably manly garnish is also called for.

* 2½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Fuller’s Chiswick Bitter
* Garnish: Olive wrapped in bacon

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Porn Star Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A fruity sweet crowd-pleaser with champagne served on the side.

* 1½ fresh Passion fruit (fresh fruit)
* 2 shot Absolut Vanilia Vodka
* ½ shot Passoa 'The Passion Drink' Liqueur
* ½ shot Vanilla sugar syrup
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 2 shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Float half fresh passion fruit

**Instructions:** Wash and cut 2 fresh passion fruits in half, SCOOP out the seeds and flesh of 3 halves into your shaker. (Keep last passion fruit half for garnish). Add next four ingredients (all but champagne), SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

Separately, POUR champagne into chilled shot glass to serve on the side. Instruct drinker to sip alternately from each glass.

---

### The Quad

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Four different orange flavoured ingredients combine in this complex fruity cocktail.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Oranje Vodka
* 1 shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¼ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Sweet Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A gin martini made with sweet vermouth - sweet in name but drier than the cherry garnish might indicate.

* 2½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth

---

### Tijuana Brass

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Pronounced "Tea-You-One-Na" this is basically a Tommy's Margarita topped with cucumber foam.

* 2 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¾ shot AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Cucumber foam

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 3 ingredients with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass. Top with cucumber foam (fill a cream whipper two-thirds full with equal parts cucumber juice, 1:1 simple syrup and egg white, charge with two CO2 cartridges and chill).

---

### Tip Top Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The lemon zest twist is essential to the fine balance of this vermouth (note; no spirit) cocktail.

* 2 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¾ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Sherry Cobbler

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This age old cocktail is said to have been the drink for which the waxed paper straw was invented. To quote Harry Johnson, from his 1882 Bartender's Manual, "It is a very refreshing drink for old and young."

* 2 shot Oloroso sherry
* ½ shot Pedro Ximénez sherry
* ⅙ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ¼ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* Garnish: Lemon & orange wedges

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into a glass filled with crushed ice.

---

### Submarine Kiss

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Looks stunning and gives the drinker the option to sip or swirl to mix the sweet liqueur base into the body of the drink.

* ⅓ shot Créme de violette liqueur
* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (discarded)

**Instructions:** POUR liqueur into base of chilled glass. SHAKE the rest of ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. SHAKE again without ice (dry shake) and slowly fine strain into liqueur primed glass so contents of shaker float over liqueur.

---

### Palomino Flor

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A subtle vegetal note comes from the celery in this unusual aperitif cocktail.

* ½ shot Freshly extracted celery juice
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ⅔ shot Martini Bianco Vermouth
* ⅓ shot Fino sherry
* ⅛ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* Garnish: Short pale yellow stalk and leaf from celery heart

**Instructions:** MUDDLE celery in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### The Hee Bee Jee Bees

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A Margarita with a touch of honey vodka and agave enriched orange liqueur.

* 1 shot Honey flavoured vodka
* 1 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¾ shot Giffard Agave Sec liqueur
* ⅓ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 3 drop Bob's Lavender Bitters
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

* Garnish: Mint leaf pegged to rim or float very tip of mint sprig

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

### Angel's Draft

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A refreshing, minty, light cocktail with herbal complexity.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ¼ shot Chartreuse Jaune (Yellow Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* 1 dash Bittermens Hopped Grapefruit Bitters
* 3 fresh Mint leaves
* ¼ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist (discarded) & mint leaf

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) to emulsify and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Aperol Spritz

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Slightly sweet, herbal and refreshing.

* 3 shot Martini Prosecco D.O.C.
* 2 shot Aperol Aperitivo by Fratelli Barbieri
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into ice-filled glass and lightly stir.

### Caribeño

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A Daiquiri that is light on lime and elongated with coconut water. Delicious and very refreshing.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 4 shot Coconut water
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all the ingredients with ice and strain into a ice-filled glass.

### Comet Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This riff on the Sidecar is lighter, less tart, and altogether more approachable than the original, but some may find it lacks the original’s cleansing zesty bite.

* 1½ shot Cognac
* ¼ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¼ shot Drambuie liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Daiquiri No.1 Natural (Countdown 3:2:1 formula)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Made to the easy-to-remember 3:2:1 Daiquiri (or countdown) formula (45ml rum, 30ml lime & 15ml sugar syrup (2:1), this balanced but limey daiquiri lacks the poise of my preferred 10:3:2 formula.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Gin Twist

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Gin botanicals flavour this delicate citrusy, warming drink.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Boiling water
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into pre-warmed glass and STIR.

---

### Zubrowka Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The grassy notes of Zubrówka and delicate cinnamon shine through in this well-balanced and well-integrated delicately spicy vintage cocktail.

* ¼ shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 1½ shot Bison grass vodka
* ¼ shot Original Danziger Goldwasser Liqueur
* 1½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** POUR absinthe into ice-filled glass, top with water and stand to one side. Separately STIR other ingredients with ice. Dump contents of glass and strain stirred drink into the absinthe washed glass.

---

### Tres Amigos Daiquiri

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Actually this is a navy rum influenced Margarita made to Daiquiri proportions, but whatever it's called, it's damn good.

* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice

* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Strawberry on Acid

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Fruity, slightly sweet strawberry, balanced and made interesting by vodka, balsamic vinegar and black pepper tingle.

* 3 fresh Small ripe strawberries (hulled)
* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ¾ shot Lejay Creme de Fraise (Strawberry) Liqueur
* ⅙ shot Balsamic vinegar of Modena
* 1 pinch Black pepper
* Top up with Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Balsamic covered strawberry

**Instructions:** MUDDLE strawberries in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. TOP with champagne.

---

### Francophile Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A simple variation on the vodka-based 'French Martini' adding gin and dry vermouth to help justify its 'martini' name.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Black raspberry liqueur
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 1 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### French Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A simple riff on the 'French Martini' swapping the usual vodka for the more French cognac. Fruity and easy drinking.

* 2 shot Cognac
* 1½ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Black raspberry liqueur
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### The Matinee

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Created in 2010 by Metinee Kongsrivilai at The Bon Vivant, Edinburgh, Scotland.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Vanilla sugar syrup
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* 2 leaf Kaffir lime (fresh fruit)
* Garnish: Frozen kaffir lime leaf

**Instructions:** DRY SHAKE (without ice) all ingredients. SHAKE again with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Merchant of Venice

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The richness and flavour of honey along with the distinctive taste of Aperol jointly balance lemon citrus notes in this majestic vodka-based drink.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 2 spoon Runny honey
* ½ shot Aperol Aperitivo by Fratelli Barbieri
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR honey with vodka in base of shaker to dissolve. Add other ingredients and DRY SHAKE (without ice). SHAKE again with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### The Mulberry

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Jammy mulberry fruit, Pimm's and gin freshened with mint and lemon, served on the rocks.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 spoon Mulberry jam
* 7 fresh Mint leaves
* 1 shot Pimm's No.1 Cup
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Top up with Elderflower pressé
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** STIR jam and gin in base of shaker to dissolve jam. Add mint, Pimm's and lemon juice, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with elderflower pressé.

### Oaxaca Old-Fashioned

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** An agave based old-fashioned with a wonderful hit of smokiness from the mezcal.

* 1½ shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ½ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* 1 spoon AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (flamed)

**Instructions:** STIR tequila with three ice cubes in a glass. Add other ingredients and STIR with more ice. Top up ice and STIR some more.

---

### Rhine Wine Cobbler

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Light, grapey, fruit and very refreshing. One for a summer's afternoon.

* 3 fresh Seedless white grapes
* 2 wedge Pineapple (fresh) (cored, skinned and chopped)
* 3 shot Reisling wine
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: A grape, orange and pineapple slice

**Instructions:** MUDDLE grapes and pineapple in base of shaker and fine strain (without shaking) into glass filled with crushed ice. POUR other ingredients into glass and cobble (churn/stir) with barspoon to thoroughly mix.

---

### Sourise

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Almond, cognac and raspberry harmoniously sit together to flavour this sour-style cocktail.

* 5 fresh Raspberries
* 2 shot Cognac
* ¼ shot Giffard Sirop de Orgeat (Almond) Syrup
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Raspberries

**Instructions:** DRY SHAKE all ingredients (without ice). SHAKE again with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Creamy Vanilla Colada

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

* 2 shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* 1½ shot Fruko Schulz Yoghurt Liqueur

---

### Satan's Whiskers (Enroulée)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Enroulée is the French word for ‘curled’ and this particular version of Satan's Whiskers is ‘curled’ by the use of mandarine liqueur in place of the Grand Marnier found in the ‘straight’ version.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ½ shot Mandarine Napoleon Grande Liqueur Imperiale
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Satan's Whiskers (Marcelled)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This variation on the classic Satan’s Whiskers calls for it not to be ‘curled’ (as is the case when you use triple sec), but to be ‘marcelled’, apparently a deep soft wave in one’s hair (for those that still have some) created with curling tongs and popular in the 1920s and 1930s.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1¼ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ⅛ shot John D. Taylor's Velvet Falernum Liqueur
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Satan's Whiskers (Curled)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This variation on the ‘Straight’ Satan’s Whiskers is made curly by the use of triple sec. It seems strangely counter intuitive as you’d think the slightly richer Grand Marnier would be what made it curly.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ½ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Brandy Alexander

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This after dinner classic is rich, creamy and subtly chocolaty.

* 1½ shot Cognac
* ½ shot Gabriel Boudier Dark Creme de Cacao Liqueur
* ½ shot Creme de cacao liqueur (white)
* ¾ shot Single cream / half-and-half
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white (optional)
* Garnish: Dust with freshly grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Vodka Daisy

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Dependent on your raspberry syrup (homemade is best) you'll either have a beautifully fruity and refreshing drink, or one that's a tad on the sweet side. Adjust to taste.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Raspberry (framboise) sugar syrup
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Lemon slice & raspberry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into glass filled with crushed ice. CHURN (stir) drink with ice and serve with straws.

---

### Slutty Mary

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A Bloody Maria given extra spice with chipotle chilli.

* 2 spoon Homemade paste
* 2 shot Patrón Silver Tequila (green seal) 100% agave tequila
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 3 shot Tomato juice
* Garnish: Salt/pepper rim and garnish with lime, coriander and celery.

**Instructions:** ROLL (turn shaker over repeatedly rather than shake) all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.
To make paste, blend:
1 can of La Costena Chipotle Chili in Adobo Sauce
2 large bunches of fresh coriander
1 tablespoon of salt
1 tablespoon of black pepper
100ml Agavero tequila liqueur
500ml Worcestershire sauce

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Creme de cacao liqueur (white)
* ⅛ shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* Garnish: Float mint leaf

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Alamagoozlum Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Even Mr Embury would approve of this version. Overproof Jamaican rum and copious amounts of bitters make this drink.

* 1 shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* ¾ shot Chartreuse Jaune (Yellow Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ¾ shot White overproof rum
* ¼ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* ¾ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 shot Chilled water
* ¼ shot Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white (optional)
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge

**Instructions:** DRY SHAKE (without ice) all ingredients to emulsify. Add ice, SHAKE again and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Brandy Crusta

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This old classic zings with fresh lemon and is beautifully balanced by the cognac base.

* 1¾ shot Cognac
* ¼ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¼ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Some merely shove a wide long piece of lemon peel around the inside of the glass rim, leaving the drinker to push the peel down into the glass in order to sip from the drink. Instead I prefer the peel to become a watertight extension to the glass.

Find a lemon which fits snugly in the top of a small wine, flute or sour glass. Cut off both ends of the fruit and carefully remove the pulp to leave a barrel-shaped shell of skin. Place in the top of the glass. Wet the edge of the glass and exposed fruit shell with sugar syrup and dip in caster sugar to frost the edge of both peel and glass. Leave for a couple of hours to form a hard crust that helps secure the peel.

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into pre-prepared glass.

---

### Brandy Fix

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This wonderful classic is slightly on the tart side of well-balanced.

* 2 shot Cognac
* ½ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ⅛ shot Chartreuse Jaune (Yellow Chartreuse) Liqueur
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into glass filled with crushed ice.

---

### Dry Martini #3 (3:1 ratio)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Three to one may be unfair odds in a fight but vermouth shines in this stirred off-dry Martini. Through experimentation we have found that 3:1 Martinis are better stirred rather than shaken. Conversely 15:1 Martinis are better shaken rather than stirred.

* 2¼ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* Garnish: Chilled olive on stick or lemon zest twist.

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 4 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. TOP up with soda.

### Brandy Sour

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** After the Whisky Sour, this is the most requested sour. Try it and you'll see why - but don't omit the egg white.

* 2 shot Cognac
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 3 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Lemon slice & cherry on stick (sail)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Kopstoot

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** In the worthy pursuit of responsible drinking I must stress that when enjoying a Kopstoot you should repeatedly take a sip from each glass – savour the combination rather than shooting the genever in one gulp.

* ½ shot Rutte Old Simon Genever (chilled)
* ½ pint Belgium dubbel abbey ale
* Garnish: None

**Instructions:** POUR genever into shot glass and beer into beer glass. To enjoy, simply sip a shot of ice-cold genever from a small, tulip-shaped glass, then follow with a sip of beer.

---

### Death Flip

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** With a whole egg, a shot of tequila, Jägermeister and Chartreuse, this is both a Death Flip and your last meal. Challenging herbal and bitter complexity yet with endearing sweet creaminess.

* 1 shot Patrón Silver Tequila (green seal) 100% agave tequila
* ½ shot Jägermeister Liqueur
* ½ shot Chartreuse Jaune (Yellow Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water) (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 whole Egg (white & yolk)
* 1 pinch Freshly grated nutmeg
* Garnish: Dust with freshly grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Betsy Ross

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Deep burgundy red and boozy. Based on the classic combination of port and brandy, this is a drink to finish a night. (Benefits from some dilution so stir well.)

* 1½ shot Cognac
* 1½ shot Ruby port
* ½ shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Kirsch Cosmo

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As the name suggests this is a riff on the classic Cosmopolitan using kirsch eau-de-vie in place of vodka.

* 1 shot G. Miclo Kirsch Vieux Grande Reserve Eau de Vie
* 1 shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* 1½ shot Cranberry juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### French Maid

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As Jim Meeham said when he gave us this recipe, “This hybrid of Audrey Saunders Gin Gin Mule substitutes cognac for gin and adds falernum and cucumber. Milk & Honey barman Sam Ross has a similar drink made with Bourbon dubbed the Kentucky Maid: consider this her spicy French sister.”

* 3 slice English cucumber peeled
* 8 fresh Mint leaves
* 1½ shot Cognac
* ½ shot John D. Taylor's Velvet Falernum Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 shot Three Cents Ginger Beer
* Garnish: Mint sprig speared cucumber slice

**Instructions:** MUDDLE cucumber in base of shaker. Add next 5 ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with ginger beer.

---

### Silk Road

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As the name suggests, the Silk Road harnesses the exotic herbs and spices found in the gin and Bénédictine to deliver a harmonious, flavoursome drink with a silky delivery.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ⅓ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* ⅓ shot De Kuyper Apricot Brandy Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Garden, Grain & Grape

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Pale green lime with frothy white head, this delicate wine and grape flavoured drink is laced with a large splash of vodka.

* 5 fresh Seedless white grapes
* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ¾ shot Sauvignon blanc white wine
* 1 dash Pasteurised egg white (optional)
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** MUDDLE grapes in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, DRY SHAKE (without ice). SHAKE again with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### The Salty Bird

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Salty Bird hardly suggests a sweet fruity drink but perfectly befits this bittersweet rum laced pineapple and Campari sipper.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ¾ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* 1½ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 pinch Salt
* Garnish: Dehydrated pineapple

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Northern Glow

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A White Lady with grapefruit juice and so an extra dash of sugar to balance. Tasty.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ⅓ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 3 dash Rhubarb bitters
* Garnish: Pink grapefruit zest

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Bijou Cocktail (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** It is not uncommon to see this drink stipulated with equal parts gin, Chartreuse and sweet vermouth, as called for in Harry Johnson's Bartender’s Manual. In fact that's the norm. Equal parts works, but it makes for a drink strong enough to drop a rhinoceros with Chartreuse overly dominant (and I love Chartreuse).

The level of booze in this drink makes dilution key, so don’t hesitate to up the amount of water if using huge chunks of ice fresh out the freezer.

* 1¼ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur
* 1¼ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* ¼ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (discarded) & Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### The Cappa Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Dry, balanced and delicate with a balanced marriage of gin, fortified wine and maraschino.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1½ shot Pineau des Charentes blanc
* ½ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Hocus Pocus

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Bittersweet with gin’s botanical complexity and orange zest freshness.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Carpano Antica Formula Vermouth
* ¾ shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* ⅛ shot Fernet Branca digestive bitter liqueur
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Mezzo E Mezzo

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Slightly on the bitter side of bittersweet, this classic aperitivo is light and palate cleansing. Best made with equal parts Nardini Rosso, Nardini Rabarbaro and soda.

* 1½ shot Nardini Rosso
* 1½ shot Rabarbaro
* 2 shot Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into ice-filled glass and briefly stir.

---

### Monet's Moment

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Cognac and aromatised wine lifted with a splash of absinthe. Complex and refreshing.

* 1½ shot Cognac
* 1 shot Byrrh Grand Quinquina Aromatized Wine
* ⅛ shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 dash Creole bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (discarded)

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass (preferably with one large hand-cracked cube)

---

### Paloma (Simple)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Long, fruity and refreshing.

* 2 shot Patrón Silver Tequila (green seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 4 shot Three Cents Pink Grapefruit Soda
* Garnish: Salt rim (optional) & pink or red grapefruit wedge

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into ice-filled glass and gently stir.

---

### Rhubarb Lucca Negroni

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A rhubarb-influenced rift on the classic Negroni.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* ½ shot Carpano Antica Formula Vermouth
* ½ shot Rabarbaro
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (discarded) and rhubarb stirrer

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into ice-filled glass and STIR.

---

### Rocky Left Bank

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Slightly sweet, crowd pleasing combo of gin, elderflower and white wine.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1½ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* 1½ shot Chardonnay (Chablis) white wine
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Sangaree (Sangre)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Either drink through the layers or stir before consuming. Fabulously old-school in style, this sweetened port and old tom gin drink resembles chilled mulled wine.

* 2 shot Tanqueray Old Tom gin
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 shot Warre's Otima 10 Year Old Tawny Port
* Garnish: Dust with freshly grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** SHAKE gin and sugar with ice and strain into chilled glass. Lastly POUR the port wine which will sink through drink and mix, leaving a thin clear layer at the top.

---

### Teqroni

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Lighter and slightly sweeter than a classic gin-based Negroni with Campari. However, this Italian and Mexican trio make for pleasing cross continental bedfellows.

* 1 shot Patrón Silver Tequila (green seal) 100% agave tequila
* 1 shot Aperol Aperitivo by Fratelli Barbieri
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into ice-filled glass and stir.

---

### Voyager Vodka Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Why have your Martini dampened by just vermouth when the Japanese and the Peruvians have so much more to give?

* 2½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ½ shot Junmai ginjō sake
* ⅛ shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* Garnish: Frozen green grape on stick (place on stick then freeze)

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Waldorf Daiquiri

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Walnut, celery and apple are essential elements to both a Waldorf Salad and this tasty Daiquiri.

* 2 inch Freshly extracted celery juice
* 2 shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* ½ shot Creme de cacao liqueur (white)
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Pressed apple juice
* Garnish: A walnut, apple wedge and chunk of blue cheese on the side

**Instructions:** MUDDLE celery in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Tomatini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A sweet and sour sipper that has to be tried. Delicate and yet assertive, this is an ‘out there’ recipe!

* 1 fresh Cherry tomato (chopped)
* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot White balsamic vinegar
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 pinch Black pepper
* Garnish: Pepper half rim & cherry tomato

**Instructions:** MUDDLE tomato in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Perfect Guest

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Clean grainy vodka forms the back bone of this floral and herbal delicate dessert Vodkatini-style drink.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ⅔ shot Lillet Blanc French aperitif wine
* ⅓ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* 1 dash Fee Brothers Celery Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Honey Bubble

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Light and delicate, a great aperitif cocktail.

* 2 spoon Runny honey
* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* Top up with Martini Prosecco D.O.C.
* Garnish: Mint sprig in top of hulled strawberry

**Instructions:** STIR honey with gin in base of shaker until honey dissolves. ADD other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Elle Loves cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Fruity, very slightly sweet and suitably pink in colour.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%) (infused with vanilla)
* 1 shot White Zinfandel rose wine
* 1¼ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ¼ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* Garnish: Dried rose petals

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Ramos Chocolate Fizz cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Creamy chocolate vanilla fudge with faint orange and a hint of gin.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1½ shot Creme de cacao liqueur (white)
* ⅛ shot Orange flower water
* ⅛ shot Vanilla extract
* 1 shot Pasteurised egg white
* 1 shot Single cream / half-and-half
* 1 shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Chocolate truffle on rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 6 ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass. TOP with champagne slowly poured into glass from a height to create thick foamy head.

---

### Gl'amour Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Berry richness fortified with cognac and balanced with lemon juice. A dash of sugar adds richness while egg white smooths.

* 1½ shot Cognac
* 1 shot Black raspberry liqueur
* ⅔ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ⅛ shot Rose water
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Edible flower or dried rose petals

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Red Gemma

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Red berry flavours with light red wine tannins, liqueur sweetness and botanical depth courtesy of gin, all refreshed with fizz. Berry fizz!

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Black raspberry liqueur
* 1 shot Shiraz red wine
* 3 shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Raspberry on rim

**Instructions:** STIR first 3 ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass. TOP with Champagne and gently stir.

* Garnish: Orange zest twist

* ⅛ shot Orange flower water
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

### Sangre Dulce Cocktail

* 1 shot Blood orange juice
* ¼ shot Cinnamon sugar syrup
* ¼ shot Fernet Branca digestive bitter liqueur
* Garnish: Dehydrated blood orange slice

### Blood Orange Margarita

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Notes of tequila, orangey triple sec, bittersweet Campari, blood orange and lime juice all sit in perfect kilter in this tasty riff on the classic Margarita.

* 1½ shot Patrón Silver Tequila (green seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¾ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¼ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* ¾ shot Blood orange juice
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Half salt rim and blood orange slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

### Fruit Cup Spritz

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A light summery spritz with flavours reminiscent of Pimm's.

* 3 shot Martini Prosecco D.O.C.
* ¾ shot Martini Bianco Vermouth
* ½ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Half orange slice, lemon slice & mint sprig

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into ice-filled glass.

---

### Raspberry Frangipane Spritz

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Just like the eponymously named dessert this slightly sweet spritz is flavoured with raspberry, almond, vanilla and coconut. Butterscotch liqueur adds a biscuity note.

* 3 shot Martini Prosecco D.O.C.
* 1¼ shot Lejay Creme de Framboise (raspberry) Liqueur
* ¼ shot Disaronno Originale Amaretto liqueur
* ¼ shot Vanilla liqueur
* ⅛ shot Coconut rum liqueur
* ⅛ shot Teichenné Butterscotch Schnapps Liqueur
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Raspberry on rim

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into ice-filled glass and lightly stir.

---

### Affogato Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Based on the classic Italian dessert of the same name, this after dinner cocktail blends coffee and chocolate with ice-cream, appropriately fortified with a splash of grappa.

* 1½ shot Bepi Tosolini Grappa di Moscato
* ½ shot Coffee liqueur
* ½ shot Gabriel Boudier Dark Creme de Cacao Liqueur
* 1 shot Espresso coffee (freshly made & hot)
* 1 scoop Vanilla ice-cream
* Garnish: Float 3 coffee beans

**Instructions:** BLEND all ingredients with three cubes ice.

---

### Berry Blast (Non-alcoholic)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As the name suggests this non-alcoholic long drink is loaded with berry fruit, presented over the light tannins of a black tea base with a splash of passion fruit syrup adding flavour and a hint of balancing sweetness.

* 8 fresh Raspberries
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¾ shot Giffard Passion Fruit (Fruit de la Passion) Syrup
* 2 shot Freshly brewed cold black English breakfast tea
* 2 shot Cranberry juice
* Garnish: Mint sprig & lemon slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Gennaro's Sidecar

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This Difford version of the established Jamie's Italian Gennaro's Sidecar is predictably boozier than the original, but retains the balance between sweet limoncello liqueur and tart lemon juice.

* 1½ shot Cognac
* 1 shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ½ shot Pallini Limoncello Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Ginger Mojito (Non-alcoholic)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This Mojito may lack alcohol, indeed it's alcohol free, but it’s refreshing, balanced and tasty nonetheless.

* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 3 wedge Fresh lime
* 12 fresh Mint leaves
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** POUR first 2 ingredients into glass. ADD lime wedges (cut in half) & mint leaves. ADD crushed ice and CHURN (stir). TOP with soda and CHURN again.

---

### Jamie's Mojito

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A light mojito made more complex with bianco vermouth.

* 1 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Martini Bianco Vermouth
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 3 wedge Fresh lime
* 12 fresh Mint leaves
* Top up with Martini Prosecco D.O.C.
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** POUR first 4 ingredients into glass. ADD lime wedges & mint and crushed ice. CHURN (stir), TOP with Prosecco and CHURN again.

---

### Flying Frenchman (Absinthe Espresso Martini)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Best described as an energy cocktail on steroids - equal parts absinthe, coffee liqueur and espresso. However, unlike most caffeine laden energy drinks the Flying Frenchman is very tasty.

* 1 shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 1 shot Coffee liqueur
* 1 shot Espresso coffee (freshly made & hot)
* Garnish: Float star anise

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### The Heritage

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Vodka fortifies and supports a well-balanced blend of orange zest, apple, lemon and star anise.

* 1 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur

* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Anise / aniseed syrup
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Float star anise

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Hi Life Spritz

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Borrowing its name from both BA High Life magazine and the Hi-ball glass it is served in, this refreshing long drink combines the botanical complexity of gin with honeyed elderflower liqueur balanced by white wine acidity.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1½ shot Chardonnay (Chablis) white wine
* 1½ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Lime wedge squeezed and dropped in drink

**Instructions:** STIR three ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with soda and lightly stir.

---

### Bonaparte cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Zesty mandarin orange and espresso coffee served as a tall refreshing cocktail.

* 3 shot Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* 1 shot Espresso coffee (freshly made & hot)
* 1½ shot Mandarine Napoleon Grande Liqueur Imperiale
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** POUR chilled soda water into ice-filled glass. Add freshly brewed hot espresso coffee so it layers on the sparkling water. Lastly pour the Mandarin Napoleon liqueur (the tasty part of the Bonaparte) which will sink through the coffee layer, pulling the drink together while leaving the coffee’s crema on the surface.

---

### Surf & Turf Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Fino sherry adds a slight salty ‘surf’ note to this riff on the classic Turf Club Cocktail.

* 1½ shot Tanqueray Old Tom gin
* ¾ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ½ shot Fino sherry
* ¼ shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Turf Club Cocktail (Kappeler's Recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Reminiscent of a Martini but sans vermouth, sweetened with dash of sugar and balanced by heavy use of bitters.

* 2 shot Tanqueray Old Tom gin
* 3 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* 1 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* ⅛ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ¾ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Turf Club Cocktail (Johnson's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Despite the maraschino liqueur this Martini-style cocktail is dry and punchy.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¼ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* 1 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (discarded) & Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Turf Club Cocktail (Crockett's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** According to his 1935 The Old Waldorf-Astoria Bar Book, Albert Stevens Crockett’s recipe was actually 2/3rds jenever to 1/3 sweet vermouth but produces an overly dry drink so we've slightly upped the proportion of vermouth to gin.

* 1¾ shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* 1¼ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Gin Colheita

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The quality and style of your madeira is crucial to the success and balance of this cocktail - don’t skimp – buy a colheita.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Verdelho madeira (medium dry) 10 year old
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅓ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** THROW (pour from one vessel to another from a height) all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Thai Green Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Extracting the juice from the stems and leaves of the coriander is key to both the colour and flavour of this fresh tasting cocktail, inspired by some of the flavours of a Thai Green Curry - only without the chilli heat.

* 1 inch Lemongrass stem
* 7 fresh Coriander seeds
* 3 sprig Coriander (cilantro) leaves
* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Coconut sugar syrup
* Garnish: 3 sprigs coriander

**Instructions:** MUDDLE first 3 ingredients in base of shaker. SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Paddington Bear Martini cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Tangy orange marmalade with gin and pisco rounded with bianco vermouth.

* 2 spoon English orange marmalade
* 1¾ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* ½ shot Martini Bianco Vermouth
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Snowball (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Rich thick and creamy egg yolk freshened with dry sherry, zesty lime cordial and invigorated with champagne.

* 2 shot Brut Champagne
* 1 shot Fino sherry
* ½ shot Rose's lime cordial
* 2 shot Warninks Advocaat liqueur
* Garnish: Lime zest twist (discarded) & dust with chocolate powder

**Instructions:** POUR champagne into ice-filled glass. SHAKE last three ingredients with ice and strain over champagne.

---

### Christmas Cheer-re

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Jenever provides the yuletide spirit base, sweetened and flavoured by cherry liqueur, with Chinato drying and adding wine notes while gin adds freshness and botanical complexity. Maraschino and orange bitters complete this festive tipple.

* 1 shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* 1 shot Cherry Heering cherry brandy liqueur
* 1 shot Cantine Gancia Antica Ricetta Barolo Chinato
* ½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¼ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (discarded) & Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into glass.

---

### Christmas Special

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The perfect after dinner cocktail at any time of year but particularly appropriate over the festive period due to its ingredients – Pedro Ximénez sherry tastes like Christmas pudding, mandarins are not just for Christmas and walnuts are best cracked whilst watching a Christmas special.

* 2 shot Cognac
* ½ shot Pedro Ximénez sherry
* ½ shot Mandarine Napoleon Grande Liqueur Imperiale
* ¼ shot Toschi Nocello Walnut Liqueur de Noix
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (discarded) and float half shelled walnut

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Gingerbread Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A soaking wet Vodka Martini with a festive dose of almond and gingerbread.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¼ shot Disaronno Originale Amaretto liqueur
* ¼ shot Gingerbread sugar syrup
* Garnish: Gingerbread or ginger cookie

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### White Russian Christmas

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As the apt name suggests, this is a Christmassy white Russian – the festive feel courtesy of mincemeat and gingerbread syrup.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 spoon Robertson's mincemeat
* ½ shot Coffee liqueur
* ¼ shot Gingerbread sugar syrup
* 1 shot Single cream / half-and-half
* Garnish: Serve with mince pie

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Randy Old-fashioned

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Port and brandy (rhymes ‘Randy’) are traditionally consumed at Christmas and used to be a popular British pub combo. I've used maple syrup in place of brown sugar syrup to lightly sweeten this festive after dinner combo. The Sazerac was the inspiration for the choice of bitters and use of absinthe.

* 2 shot Cognac
* 1 shot Warre's Otima 10 Year Old Tawny Port
* ¼ shot Maple syrup
* 2 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 2 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherries on stick

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Saison l'Hiver

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The rich wintery flavours of sloe gin and honey are balanced by lemon juice with clove providing seasonal spice and rosé champagne lifting and refreshing all.

* 1 dried Clove
* ⅓ shot Honey water (3 honey to 1 water)
* ½ shot Rutte Sloe Gin liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Top up with Rosé Champagne
* Garnish: Seasonal berries on rim

**Instructions:** MUDDLE clove in base of shaker. Add next 3 ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. TOP with champagne.

---

### Nutty Pear

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As the name suggests pear and almond are the main flavours with calvados providing backbone and hints of apple, while champagne dries and adds flavoursome effervescence.

* 1½ shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* ¼ shot Disaronno Originale Amaretto liqueur
* 1 shot Pear purée
* 2 shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Pear slice on rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 3 ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass over champagne.

---

### Saint-Marc Daiquiri

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** It’s a Daiquiri but with monastic Bénédictine and less than holy absinthe influences – perhaps it’s the saffron in the Bénédictine, perhaps it’s the star anise in the absinthe, but the result is truly a spiritual experience. It’s simply divine.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* ⅛ shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lime slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Triple A

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** So named due to this drink being flavoured with absinthe, apple and almond.

* 1 shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 1 shot Chilled water
* 1 shot Pressed apple juice
* ½ shot Giffard Sirop de Orgeat (Almond) Syrup
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Absinthe Makes The Heart Grow Fonder

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Absinthe and gin delicately lead this subtle cherry flavoured cocktail. Campari adds more colour than flavour while pink grapefruit freshens.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin

* ⅛ shot Cherry Heering cherry brandy liqueur
* ⅛ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ⅛ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Flamed orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Fairy Cream

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Absinthe sits majestically with cream and chocolate in this indulgent after-dinner cocktail.

* 1¼ shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure

---

### White Negroni

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Wayne Collins, this drink’s creator, originally used equal parts as is usual for a classic Negroni and after trying various other formulations we’ve found this works best. Wayne also specifies a grapefruit zest twist and this makes the drink. However, be warned, this is a drink for aficionados of bittersweet aperitifs and Suze. We love it!

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* 1 shot Lillet Blanc French aperitif wine
* Garnish: Pink grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into ice-filled glass and STIR.

---

### Charente White Negroni

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A White Negroni with the cognac replacing half of the gin. Fittingly ‘Charente’ references the Cognac area of France.

* ½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Cognac
* 1 shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* 1 shot Lillet Blanc French aperitif wine
* Garnish: Pink grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into ice-filled glass and STIR.

---

### Velvet Maker

---

### Bloody Negroni

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A classic Negroni consists of equal parts gin, Italian red bitters and sweet vermouth garnished with an orange slice. When in season, a splash of blood orange juice adds a refreshing citrusy tang.

* ¾ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* ¾ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ¾ shot Blood orange juice
* Garnish: Blood orange slice

**Instructions:** Briefly STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Buttercup cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** When made to Lucas Bols original specification: 1 shot Bols Genever, 1 shot Bols Butterscotch liqueur and ¾ shot sweet vermouth, this drink has a great flavour but lacks balls (or perhaps I should say Bols). Hence the formula above which is heavy on the Genever with equal parts butterscotch liqueur and sweet vermouth. It’s even better when an Oude Gevever is used rather than a Jonge as this amplifies the butterscotch notes.

Beware, Bols' original recipe calls for a lemon zest twist garnish but the lemon oils overpower the butterscotch, so if you use a slither of lemon skin to fix our choice of a Werther’s Original to the rim, then don’t express the lemon’s oils over the drink.

Don’t be tempted to use buttercup flowers as a garnish as they are poisonous. They are also poisonous when eaten by livestock but their acrid taste and the blistering of the mouth they cause mean that animals don’t tend to eat them. Interestingly, the toxins degrade when dried, so hay containing dried buttercups is safe for animals to eat.

* 2 shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* ¾ shot Teichenné Butterscotch Schnapps Liqueur
* ¾ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* Garnish: Lemon zest on rim (not sprayed) nestling Werther’s Original butter candy

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Heisenberg Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Like a suitably complex chemistry experiment this Margarita-like cocktail has seven ingredients with mezcal adding smoky notes to tequila and a trio of liqueurs balancing lime sourness.

* 1⅓ shot Patrón Añejo Tequila
* ½ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* ⅓ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ⅔ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Le Sirop de Monin Lavandie - Lavender Sugar Syrup
* ¼ shot Lejay Curacao Bleu (blue curacao) Liqueur
* ⅛ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Blue coloured salt rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. (Most appropriately served in a science beaker.)

---

### Latest Word

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A Last Word made to classic equal parts proportions but with jenever replacing London dry gin. The more robust flavour of jenever stands up well to the other very characterful ingredients.

* ¾ shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* ¾ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ¾ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Lemon Tart

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This bitter-sweet aperitif cocktail harnesses the herbal bitterness of gentian root with gin’s botanical notes and sweetened freshly squeezed lemon juice.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (discarded) & half lemon wheel on rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. SHAKE again without ice (dry shake) and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Marvin's Last Word

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Created bu Christos Chouseas at 42 Bar in Athens, Greece – a bar where The Hitchhiker's Guide to the Galaxy and the work of Douglas Adams influences many of the drink names.

In The Hitchhiker's Guide to the Galaxy book, the number 42 is the "answer to the ultimate question of life, the universe, and everything", while ‘Marvin’ is a paranoid, depressive android.

* ¾ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Skinos Mastiha
* ¾ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Love Heart

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This lavender pink drink is everything you (or your partner) might want for a Valentine’s tipple. It is the right colour, includes parfait amour liqueur (meaning perfect love) and the all-important champagne sparkle. Good luck.

In case he/she asks, parfait amour is a lilac coloured curaçao (orange) liqueur flavoured with rose petals, vanilla pods and almonds.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Lejay Creme de Fraise (Strawberry) Liqueur
* ½ shot Giffard Parfait Amour Liqueur
* Top up with Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Half strawberry on rim with Love Heart sweet pegged to rim

**Instructions:** POUR into chilled glass and lightly stir.

---

### Give Me Fever

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This drink combines the fever quenching G&T with medicinal lavender and flavoursome mezcal from the Mexican territories where us Brits are susceptible to fever… bom, bom, bom… give me fever. What a lovely way to burn.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¾ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ⅛ shot Le Sirop de Monin Lavandie - Lavender Sugar Syrup
* ½ shot Tonic water
* Garnish: Flamed lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 6 ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass. Top with a splash of tonic water.

---

### Pisco Kid

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This short pisco-based spirituous stirred drink was inspired by memories of Nestle’s Milkybars and the 1980s British TV ads featuring the Milkybar Kid promoting the white chocolate bars. White crème de cacao’s sweetness is balanced by dry sherry and the acidity of Sauvignon Blanc wine which also adds grassy floral notes and complexity. The discarded orange zest twist makes the first sip a white chocolate orange experience.

* 2 shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* ¾ shot Creme de cacao liqueur (white)
* ½ shot Sauvignon blanc white wine
* ¼ shot Fino sherry
* ½ shot Chilled water
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (discarded) & Nestle's Milkybar or other white chocolate

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This tasty sour features the distinctive flavour of mastiha.

* 2 shot Skinos Mastiha
* ⅔ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)

* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Fresh Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The perfect digestif Martini. Mastiha and white crème de menthe - both renowned for their digestive properties - add cooling freshness to this wet, lightly sweetened Martini.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Skinos Mastiha
* ⅓ shot Giffard Menthe Pastille white crème de menthe liqueur
* ¾ shot Martini Bianco Vermouth
* 5 drop Bob's Bitters Peppermint bitters
* Garnish: Mint leaf

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Koningsdag cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This very Dutch celebratory cocktail is made using Dutch Ketel One vodka, Dutch orange curacao, Dutch-made King’s Ginger liqueur. The all-important orange hue and subtle flavour comes from carrot juice. For the truly orange King's Day experience make with 50% Ketel One vodka and 50% Ketel One Oranje, or even replace vodka with 100% Ketel One Oranje.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ¾ shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* ¼ shot King's Ginger Liqueur
* 1½ shot Freshly extracted carrot juice
* 5 drop Bob's Bitters Coriander bitters
* Garnish: Coriander sprig

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Alexander

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This gin-laced creamy Alexander has sadly slipped from popularity, partly knocked by its successors, particularly the Brandy Alexander.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Creme de cacao liqueur (white)
* ¾ shot Single cream / half-and-half
* ¼ shot Pasteurised egg white (optional)
* Garnish: Dust with grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Strawberry Fields

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This refreshing vodka-based strawberry cocktail balances tart lemon juice with rich honey. Drops of balsamic and a dusting of black pepper add complexity.

* 2 fresh Small ripe strawberries (hulled)
* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Honey water (3 honey to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Five drops of balsamic vinegar and a dusting of freshly ground black pepper

**Instructions:** MUDDLE strawberry in base of shaker. Add vodka, honey syrup, lemon juice and egg white and SHAKE with ice. Strain back into shaker, DRY SHAKE (without ice) and strain into chilled glass.

### New Orleans Minute cocktail

* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters

### Chanbanger cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Like its creator this drink is hard to classify. A hint of Singapore Sling oriental cherry with some Cuban Daiquiri aged rum and a splash of Papa’s grapefruit citrus sourness.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* ⅔ shot Cherry Heering cherry brandy liqueur
* ⅓ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Pastry War Margarita

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

* Garnish: Lime wedge

### Edison's Medicine cocktail

### Roman Highball

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A refreshing Pimm’s Cup-like. A great long drink to come home to.

* ¾ shot King's Ginger Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Candied ginger or fresh ginger

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 3 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with soda.

---

### Wet cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Superbly refreshing. The pinch of cinnamon adds delicate spice which combines well with cachaça and ginger ale.

* 1⅓ shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca
* ⅓ shot Giffard Sirop de Orgeat (Almond) Syrup
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 1 pinch Ground cinnamon
* Top up with Ginger ale
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into glass filled with crushed ice.

### Greek Celery Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Celery and mastiha pair well, while gin adds a spirituous bite and botanical complexity. A small grind of pepper to finish adds a nuance of spice.

* 1⅔ shot Skinos Mastiha
* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin

* Garnish: Grind of pepper & celery stick

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Caipirissima

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A Daiquiri-like drink made in the style of a Caipirinha.

* ¾ fresh Fresh lime (chopped wedges)
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Serve with 2 short straws

**Instructions:** MUDDLE lime wedges in the base of shaker to release juice and oils in its skin. Add rum and sugar. SHAKE with 6oz scoop crushed ice and pour all without straining into glass.

---

### Gun Metal Blue cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Orange, peach and cinnamon subtly flavour this mezcal based margarita.

* 1½ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon

### Greek Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Mastiha (which after all is botanically flavoured spirit) combines wonderfully with gin and dry vermouth. A splash of ouzo adds more Greek interest.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Skinos Mastiha
* ¾ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ⅛ shot Ouzo 12
* Garnish: Float mint sprig or leaf

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Aristotle cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The thinking man’s mixed drink, this is based on gin with the distinctive flavour of Greek mastiha and lengthened with birch water.

* 3 fresh Mint leaves
* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Skinos Mastiha
* 1½ shot Birch water
* 4 drop Bob's Bitters Peppermint bitters (optional)
* Garnish: Mint leaf

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE mint in base of stirring glass. Add other ingredients, STIR with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Woody cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Named not after the cheery chap in Cheers or even the Beatles’ Norwegian Wood but due to this particularly Woody cocktail containing birch water and mastiha.

* 3 fresh Mint leaves
* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot Skinos Mastiha
* 1 shot Birch water
* ¼ shot Fino sherry
* 8 drop Bob's Bitters Peppermint bitters
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** MUDDLE mint in base of stirring glass. Add other ingredients, STIR with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### South of Heaven cocktail

### Four Skin Daiquiri

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Daiquiris are refreshing but this mastiha influenced example is particularly so. As ‘four’ the name, well it’s a Daiquiri with four ingredients, including mastiha and the brand we used was Skinos, so appropriate, we think you’ll agree.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1¼ shot Skinos Mastiha
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¾ shot Birch water
* Garnish: Lime wedge on rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Reggatta de Blanc

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Dry and boozy.

“White Reggae” was the second, and seminal, album by the English rock band The Police. The album's French name reflects the heavy influence of the country’s products in this cocktail. Happily for approval by our naming committee (my missus), most of the ingredients are also decidedly “Blanc”.

* 1 shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* 1 shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* 1 shot Sauvignon blanc white wine
* ½ shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* ⅛ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Green grapes on stick

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Reverse Vesper Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** More a subtly fortified wine than a true “three and under the guest” Martini but delightfully so with sherry-like wine notes and faint botanical influences. Subtly refined. Despite the ‘Vesper’ name some will say that this should be stirred. Shake boldly on, but with good ice.

* 2 shot Lillet Blanc French aperitif wine
* ⅔ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ⅓ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Alexander The Great

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A tasty combination of coffee, chocolate and cream, laced with vodka.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Coffee liqueur
* ½ shot Creme de cacao liqueur (white)
* ¾ shot Single cream / half-and-half
* ¼ shot Pasteurised egg white (optional)
* Garnish: Dust with freshly grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Call Me Old-Fashioned

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** An Old-Fashioned made with cognac instead of whiskey. Works well.

* 2½ shot Cognac
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR sugar syrup and bitters with two ice cubes in a glass. Add 1½ shots of cognac and two more ice cubes. STIR some more and add another two ice cubes and another shot of cognac. Stir lots more and add more ice.

---

### Andean Dusk cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Dry biscuity champagne adds sparkle to sweet red grapes while pisco fortifies and adds complex distilled grape flavours.

* 3 fresh Red grapes
* 1 shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* ½ fresh Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Rosé Champagne
* Garnish: Drop cold red grape into drink

**Instructions:** MUDDLE grapes in base of shaker. Add next 3 ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. TOP with champagne.

---

### Minty White Lady cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** White crème de menthe and peppermint bitters bring minty freshness to this not so innocent lady in white.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin

* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice

---

### Sailor's Swizzle

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Port wine is further fortified with golden rum and delicately spiced with Pimento Dram in this long swizzled punch.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Oro Superior Gold Rum
* ⅔ shot Ruby port
* ⅛ shot St. Elizabeth Allspice Dram
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: A few dashes Angostura bitters over ice cap crowned with lime zest strings

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into chilled glass and two-thirds fill with crushed ice. SWIZZLE with a swizzle stick (or churn with a barspoon). Add more crushed ice to fill and SWIZZLE some more. Serve with straws.

---

* 1⅔ shot Bán Poitín

### Boozy Suzie

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Bittersweet gentian is the prevalent flavour (hence the 'Suzie' name), toned down by bianco vermouth and freshened with pink grapefruit over a fortifying grainy vodka base. Peychaud’s subtly adds its distinctive flavour.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* ½ shot Martini Bianco Vermouth
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* 2 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* ¼ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Pink grapefruit zest twist (discarded) & 3 spots of Peychaud’s bitters drawn through foamy head

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Sakura Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This Reverse Martini-style drink features a floating salted cherry blossom as a garnish. This is not just for looks, the hint of saltiness it lends this delicate drink replaces that which an olive typically brings to a Martini.

* 2½ shot Junmai ginjō sake
* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¼ spoon Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* Garnish: Salted cherry blossom (or olive)

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.
