### Queen's Park Hotel Super Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Perhaps best described as being a Trinidadian Daiquiri due to its heavy use of Angostura Bitters. Obviously it would also have originally been made with Trinidad gold rum, Canning's Caroni Rum according to Owen Rutter. Preferably make your own pomegranate (grenadine) syrup.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Oro Superior Gold Rum
* ½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* 4 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### The Angel Wore Red

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A most unusual combination of classic Italian red bitter liqueur, bianco vermouth, crème de menthe and lager combine brilliantly in this refreshing aperitif.

* 1⅔ shot Martini Bianco Vermouth
* ⅔ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* ⅓ shot Giffard Menthe Pastille white crème de menthe liqueur
* 2 shot Peroni lager
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR first 3 ingredients with ice. POUR beer into ice-filled glass and then strain stirred ingredients into glass and lightly stir.

---

### Mr Simon

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Your choice of jenever and orange curaçao greatly effects the balance of this cocktail. Salvatore uses Rutte Old Simon which is not only a fantastic jenever with an attractive nutty character but also befits the name. The choice of a drier, high alcohol curaçao obviously produces a correspondingly drier drink.

* 2 shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* ⅔ shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* ⅓ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* 1 spoon AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Eastside Gimlet

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A riff on the Southside using cucumber – an ingredient originally inspired by Hendrick’s Gin having recently launched when this gin cocktail was first created.

* 2 slice English cucumber peeled
* 8 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Mint leaf & cucumber slice

**Instructions:** MUDDLE cucumber in base of shaker. Add gin, lime juice and sugar syrup, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass. TOP with a splash of soda.

---

### Waterloo

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Created by yours truly (Simon Difford) at the Cabinet Room, London, England.

Named after the Battle of Waterloo which was fought on Sunday 18th June 1815 near the town of Waterloo in present-day Belgium, then part of the Netherlands. The French army commanded by Napoleon Bonaparte was defeated by an Anglo-allied army commanded by the Duke of Wellington fittingly alongside a Prussian army commanded by Gebhard Leberecht von Blücher, Prince of Wahlstatt. Napoleon's defeat at Waterloo brought his reign as French Emperor to a sudden end.

* 2 shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* ½ shot Mandarine Napoleon Grande Liqueur Imperiale
* ⅛ shot Jägermeister Liqueur
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (discarded) & float pickled almond

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Division Bell

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A mezcal inspired variation of the Last Word with a refreshing, boozy blend of ingredients.

* 1 shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* ¾ shot Aperol Aperitivo by Fratelli Barbieri
* ½ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Joy Division

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A 2:1 Dry Martini with slug of triple sec and dashes of absinthe contributing zesty orange and subtle aniseed respectively.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ½ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* 3 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Juliet & Romeo

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** You smell rose water but taste gin, lime, cucumber and mint. A refreshing summery cocktail.

* 3 slice English cucumber peeled
* 8 fresh Mint leaves
* 1 pinch Salt
* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Float 3 drops rose water, 3 drops Angostura bitters & mint leaf

**Instructions:** MUDDLE cucumber in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Moon Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Gin and sherry combine harmoniously in this stirred boozy cocktail with a  honeyed touch of jammy peach.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Amontillado sherry
* ⅙ shot Crème de pêche (peach) liqueur
* ¼ shot Honey syrup
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### The Affiliate

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Judicious dashing of orange bitters and hitting the correct dilution will make or break this drink, which is a fine balance between aged rum and rich cherry liqueur versus dry fino sherry and aromatic bitters.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* ¾ shot Fino sherry
* ¾ shot Cherry Heering cherry brandy liqueur
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Alcatraz

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Dry and lightly bitter, this tequila-based sipper makes for a great aperitif cocktail.

* 1½ shot Patrón Añejo Tequila
* ¾ shot Oloroso sherry

* ¼ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* 1 spoon AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* 2 dash Bob's Chocolate Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### The Bennett Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Judicious dashing of bitters makes or breaks this riff on the classic Gimlet.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* ½ shot Chilled water
* Garnish: Float dehydrated lime wheel

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into a chilled glass.

---

### Bijou Cocktail (inspired by Lawor's 1895 recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A boozy sipper of a cocktail that’s medium dry with honeyed richness. Gin based with orange zesty freshness and sweet vermouth adding deep herbal complexity. A great after-dinner cocktail that also works well on-the-rocks.
AKA: Not to be confused with the more commonplace equal parts gin, Chartreuse and vermouth Bijou which first appeared in Harry Johnson's 1900 Bartender's Manual.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* ¾ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Mediocre

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Ripe pineapple, rich vanilla and honey laced with rum. The use of mead in this drink inspired the ‘Mediocre’ name.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%) (infused with vanilla)
* 1 shot Mead
* 1¼ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ¼ shot Honey water (3 honey to 1 water)
* 1 dash Vanilla Bitters
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Canary Flip

* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Pinecone

**Comment:** Honey and pineapple, laced with aromatic pisco and spiced with clove.

* Garnish: Clove studded pineapple wedge

### Well-fortified

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A Bamboo meets a Vodka Martini in this boozy, vodka-laced aromatic aperitif cocktail, so named due to this cocktail packing a trio of fortified wines.

* 1½ shot Moscatel
* 1¼ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ¾ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ½ shot Fino sherry
* ¼ shot Bison grass vodka
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Carré Nouveau

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Reminiscent of a Vieux Carré but with Lillet Blanc replacing sweet vermouth and gentian replacing Angostura bitters.

* ⅙ shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* 3 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Tribute to Martell

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Originally made with Martell Cordon Bleu, this sophisticated champagne cocktail has delicate floral notes.

* ⅙ shot Créme de violette liqueur
* ½ shot Cognac
* 3½ shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Edible flower

**Instructions:** SPRAY violet liqueur onto inside surface of glass and set aside. STIR cognac with ice and strain into chilled glass.

### Mon Dernier Mot (My Last Word)

---

### Banana Split

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A banana flavoured after-dinner sipper of cocktail with coconut water subtly flavouring and smoothing cognac.

* 1½ shot Cognac
* ¾ shot Giffard Banane du Brésil crème de banane liqueur
* ¾ shot Coconut water
* 2 drop Vanilla Bitters
* 2 drop Bob's Chocolate Bitters
* ⅛ shot Single cream / half-and-half
* Garnish: Lightly dust surface of drink with chocolate powder & banana chunk on rim

**Instructions:** STIR first 5 ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass. Shake sealed container of cream and carefully POUR over the back of a spoon to form a small white spot floating in the centre of the drink.

---

### Parmenides

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A sour-style drink served straight-up combining cognac, Green Chartreuse, white wine and lemon.

* 1⅓ shot Cognac
* ⅓ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur

* Garnish: None

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Rock of Sages

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As the name suggests, sage subtly influences this fruity cognac based cocktail served on the rocks. Fruity and easy.

* 3 whole Maraschino cherries
* 4 fresh Sage leaves
* 1½ shot Cognac
* ½ shot Vermouth di Torino
* 1 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* 1 spoon Maraschino syrup (from cherry jar)
* Garnish: Maraschino cherries & sage leaves

**Instructions:** MUDDLE cherries in base of shaker. Add sage leaves and lightly bruise with the muddler. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### The Comeback

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A complex cocktail with apricot fruit to the forefront and underlying Fernet Branca bitterness.

* 1⅓ shot Cognac
* ½ shot De Kuyper Apricot Brandy Liqueur
* ⅙ shot Fernet Branca digestive bitter liqueur
* ¼ shot Maple shrub (1:1.2 cider vinegar to maple syrup)
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### A Rose By Any Other Name

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Best made using Martell Cordon Blue as per the original recipe, this is a dry boozy sipper with faint floral and chocolate notes. Perhaps forgo the grated chocolate garnish in favour of a square of dark chocolate balanced on Turkish Delight.

* 1⅔ shot Cognac
* ⅚ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ⅓ shot Rose petal liqueur
* ⅙ shot Créme de violette liqueur
* 3 drop Bob's Chocolate Bitters
* Garnish: Turkish Delight & grate dark chocolate over drink

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Revolutionary Flip

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Full-bodied both describes this drink and how you’ll feel after consuming this very tasty meal of a drink.

* 1½ shot Cognac
* ½ shot Warre's Otima 10 Year Old Tawny Port
* ⅓ shot Demerara sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1⅓ shot Fuller’s Chiswick Bitter
* 1 fresh Egg (white & yolk)
* Garnish: Dust with freshly grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE without ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Thyme for…

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** It most certainly is! As the name suggests, aromatic thyme subtly influences this spirituous cognac-based cocktail, with Grand Marnier adding rich but delicate zesty orange notes.

* 1 cube Brown sugar
* 3 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* 3 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* 2 sprig Thyme sprig
* 1⅔ shot Cognac
* ½ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* ⅓ shot Carpano Antica Formula Vermouth
* Garnish: Scorched thyme sprig

**Instructions:** DASH bitters over sugar cube in stirring glass and MUDDLE cube to crush. ADD other ingredients and stir to dissolve sugar. Add ice and STIR. Fine strain into chilled glass.

---

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A wonderfully complex marriage of cognac, distilled chocolate, rich Pedro Ximénez and banana liqueur with aromatic bitters and a dash of brine.

* Garnish: Luxardo maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

### Titre Provisoire (Provisional Title)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

* ⅙ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* 1 dash Cider vinegar
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (discard)

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Carnaghino

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Cognac, luxurious chocolate and pistachio. What’s not to like?

* 1½ shot Cognac
* ½ shot Mozart black liqueur
* ½ shot Pistacchino liqueur
* Garnish: Dark chocolate and pistacchio shave.

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass (preferably block ice).

---

### Le Coq d'Or (The Golden Rooster)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Perhaps substitute ¼ shot Demerara sugar syrup for the sugar cube and all that muddling. Whether runny or dry sugar, this flip style cocktail is balanced and complex.

* 1 cube Brown sugar
* 3 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* 2½ shot Cognac
* ⅔ shot Galliano L'Autentico liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* 1 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* 2 dash Dale DeGroff's Pimento Aromatic Bitters
* 1 fresh Egg yolk
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist (discarded) & float star anise

**Instructions:** Saturate sugar cube with Peychaud's in base of shaker and MUDDLE thoroughly. Add cognac and stir to ensure sugar is dissolved. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Don Pone

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Maraschino cherry aromas strike you first as you enjoy this cognac-laced, subtly chocolate and ginger after dinner cocktail.

* ⅙ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* 1½ shot Cognac
* ½ shot Creme de cacao liqueur (white)
* ⅓ shot King's Ginger Liqueur
* Garnish: Crystallised ginger on stick & grated dark chocolate

**Instructions:** RINSE glass with maraschino liqueur. STIR other ingredients with ice and strain into maraschino rinsed glass.

---

### L'Heritage

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Also try this aperitif-style bittersweet cocktail served on-the-rocks.

* 1½ shot Cognac
* 1½ shot Lillet Blanc French aperitif wine
* ⅓ shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (discarded) & Luxardo maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Triomphe d'Anis (Triumph of Aniseed)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A boozy stirred sipper, perhaps after-dinner cognac-based cocktail, with hints of anise coffee and dry sherry complexity.

* ⅙ shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 1 dried Star anise
* 1½ shot Cognac
* ½ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* ½ shot Coffee liqueur
* ¼ shot Fino sherry
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (discarded) & float star anise

**Instructions:** RINSE glass with absinthe. STIR other ingredients with ice and strain into absinthe rinsed glass.

---

### The Good, The Bad and the Ugni

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Perhaps it’s the holier-than-thou Chartreuse that is playing the part of the bad guy in this tasty drink. The cognac (made with Ugni Blanc grapes) play the strong, characterful part.

* 1⅓ shot Cognac
* ½ shot Canadian icewine
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ⅓ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 3 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass (preferably block of ice). Lastly, FLOAT Chartreuse.

---

### White Old Fashioned

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Joerg makes this cocktail using Bacardi Neo but it also works well with the easier to obtain Bacardi Carta Blanca. If you haven't any Sexy Bitters then try with a dash or orange bitters.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ⅓ shot Clément Sirop Sucre de Canne (sugar cane juice syrup)
* 2 dash Sexy bitters
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Gin Old Fashioned

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A couple of shots of bready genever with a spoon of sugar and a couple of dashes of bitters - incredibly simple, equally classic, and with the right genever, incredibly tasty.

* 2 shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Velasco and Sand

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Mezcal adds a faintly smoky note to this riff on the classic Blood & Sand. The proportion of spirit and orange juice is slightly raised from the usual equal parts formula – the extra nip of mezcal adds an uplifting kick to the drink while more orange adds zippy freshness and lightens what can otherwise be a heavy cocktail.

* 1 shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* ¾ shot Cherry Heering cherry brandy liqueur
* ¾ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Smoke & Mirrors (by The Bon Vivants)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Genever and mezcal sit surprisingly well together in this very refreshing drink with mint and lemon.

* 4 fresh Mint leaves
* 1½ shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* ½ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into glass filled with crushed ice.

### Cassini

**Comment:** A simple but pleasant spirituous berry drink. Not a Cassis Martini, but a Cassini.

* 1¾ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ¼ shot Rutte Dry Gin

* 1½ shot Cranberry juice
* Garnish: Blackberry on rim or blackberries on stick

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Apairoteef

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Invigorating, refreshing and very amusing – we do like a pun.

* 1 shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* 1 shot *Special ingredient #1 (see below)
* 1 shot Martini Prosecco D.O.C.
* Garnish: Set of confectionery dentures dropped into glass & lemon zest twist (discarded)

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass (without ice). (Note the sparkling wine should be flat.)

*Special ingredient #1 = Cardamom & Pear Shrub made as follows:
400ml Merlet pare 
300ml Gewürztraminer, Germain. 
7g Cardamom pods
5ml Vanilla curd 
75ml White balsamic 
10g Citric acid 
10g Tartaric acid 
150g Caster sugar 
100g Water 
Blend for 5 minutes and super strain.

### Yuliya Martini

### Floral Daiquiri

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A floral riff on a classic Daiquiri with a hint of berry fruitiness and a lavender pink hue courtesy of a blueberry threesome.

* 1/12 shot Créme de violette liqueur
* 3 fresh Blueberries
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ⅔ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Le Sirop de Monin Lavandie - Lavender Sugar Syrup
* ⅓ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* Garnish: Sprig of dried lavender pegged to rim

**Instructions:** Rinse chilled glass with violet liqueur and set aside ready for drink. MUDDLE blueberries in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into rinsed glass.

---

### Rabo-de-Galo

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The bittersweet herbal notes from the vermouth and Cynar combine harmoniously with the cachaça. Depending on how punchy you like your cocktails you may want to increase or decrease the amount of cachaça (anywhere between 45 and 60ml).

* 1⅔ shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca
* ½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ½ shot Cynar Ricetta Originale Artichoke Amaro Liqueur
* 1 dash Hopped Grapefruit Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** THROW OR STIR (or even shake) all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Picasso Sour

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** We were struck by the photograph that accompanied the recipe sent to us by this cocktail’s creator. The photo depicted the drink's presentation at Burj Al Arab in Dubai where it is served with a tiny wooden artist’s colour palate alongside micro easel holding a print of Picasso’s Portrait of The Absinthe Drinker.

The cocktail itself is an artistic citrus-led riff on a Pisco Sour, but the original presentation amounts to true cocktail artistry.

* 1½ shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* ½ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ⅚ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅔ shot Pasteurised egg white
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 4 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* Garnish: Spray Angostura Bitters through stencil or drip a few drops on surface foam.

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Champs-Elysees Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A great after dinner drink for lovers of cognac and Chartreuse.

* 1½ shot Cognac
* ½ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Daisy de Santiago

* Garnish: Lime wedge

### The Stag

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Boozy and stirred down. Cognac fortifies and combines harmoniously with Jägermeister’s bittersweet herbal and spicy notes. Rich lavender enhances and amplifies these flavours with ginger bitters adding extra zingy spice and toning the blend. Best appreciated as an after-dinner digestive.

* 1½ shot Cognac
* 1 shot Jägermeister Liqueur
* ⅓ shot Le Sirop de Monin Lavandie - Lavender Sugar Syrup
* 5 drop Bob's Bitters Ginger
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (discarded) with cube of candied ginger

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients and strain into chilled glass.

---

---

### Knickerbocker

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Fruity and refreshing – a party drink with rum and raspberry flavours predominating. At its best when made with homemade raspberry syrup.

* 2½ shot Bacardi Carta Oro Superior Gold Rum
* ⅙ shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* ½ shot Raspberry (framboise) sugar syrup
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Squeezed-out half lime shell & seasonal berries: raspberries, blackberries, blueberries

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 4 ingredients with ice and strain into glass 2/3rd filled with cubed ice. Cap with crushed ice, serve with a straw.

---

### A.B.C. Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Wonderfully delicate. Mint gives subtle freshness to the classic port and brandy combo.

* 7 fresh Mint leaves
* 1 shot Warre's Otima 10 Year Old Tawny Port
* 1 shot Cognac
* ¼ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ⅛ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist & Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** TEAR mint and place in shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Dutch Artist's Special

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Bready genever is aromatised with sherry and kirsch while red currant syrup provides the main flavour with its richness balanced by lemon juice.

* 1½ shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* ½ shot Oloroso sherry
* ½ shot G. Miclo Kirsch Vieux Grande Reserve Eau de Vie
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Groseille (redcurrant) syrup
* Garnish: Redcurrant bunch laid across rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Slow Negroni

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As the name suggests, this is simply a classic Negroni with sloe gin introduced as a forth ingredient. Its flavour is exactly as it says on the tin – a sloe berry flavoured Negroni.

* ⅔ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ⅔ shot Rutte Sloe Gin liqueur
* ⅔ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* ⅔ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into ice-filled glass and briefly STIR.

---

### Gin Pahit

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The balance of bitters to sugar is key to the success of this cocktail. Use a Japanese dasher bitters bottle and measure your 2:1 sugar syrup judiciously and you’ll have made something special. Go easy while spraying the lemon zest over the drink – too much lemon oil will wreck its fine balance.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* ½ shot Chilled water
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Oaxacan Negroni

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Mezcal lends a characterful smoky note to this complex riff on a classic Negroni.

* ¾ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* ¾ shot Cantine Gancia Antica Ricetta Barolo Chinato
* 1 dash Bob's Chocolate Bitters
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass (preferably over a chunk of block ice).

---

### Suze you, Sir

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** We do like a pun and appropriately the original recipe for this cocktail specifies Suze gentian liqueur. The flavour of gentian combines brilliantly with tequila while dry vermouth adds herbal complexity.

* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth

* 1/12 shot AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* 1 dash Bittermens Hopped Grapefruit Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

* 1¼ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon

### Tara Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Imagine a delicately clove influenced Daiquiri but with the bready influence of poitín, then you are some way towards imagining the taste of this refreshing and invigorating cocktail.

* 1½ shot Bán Poitín
* ½ shot John D. Taylor's Velvet Falernum Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 3 dash Bob's Abbotts Bitters
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Yellow Cactus Flower

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Jordan Smith, describes his creation as “bright, herbaceous, subtly smoky, and refreshingly bittersweet. The pineapple adds texture and a slight sweetness to balance the tartness of the lime and bitterness of the Suze [Jordan’s gentain liqueur of choice], while the herbaceousness of the Suze is amplified by the Yellow Chartreuse.” We concur! “Bright, herbaceous, subtly smoky, and refreshingly bittersweet” perfectly sums up this challenging aperitif cocktail.

Jordan’s original spec calls for pineapple purée rather than juice. This adds mouthfeel and sweetness – consider muddling a couple of pineapple wedges in base of shaker with a dash of sugar syrup as an alternative.

* 1 shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* ¾ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* ¾ shot Chartreuse Jaune (Yellow Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Yellow Negroni

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As the name suggests, this pisco based, five equal part, vivid yellow bittersweet aperitif was inspired by the classic Negroni and three of the world’s most iconic yellow liqueurs: limoncello, gentian and Chartreuse Jaune.

* ¾ shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* ¾ shot Pallini Limoncello Liqueur
* ¾ shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* ¾ shot Chartreuse Jaune (Yellow Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ¾ shot Martini Bianco Vermouth
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into serving glass, add ice to fill glass, STIR briefly and serve.

---

### Milanese G&T

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A traditional Gin & Tonic with a splash of Campari adding colour and bittersweet herbal fruity complexity.

* 1 shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* Top up with Tonic water
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into ice-filled glass and lightly STIR so as not to lose fizz.

---

### Arte de Volar

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Tequila replaces gin in this riff on an Aviation – ‘Arte de Volar’ is Spanish for ‘Art of Flying. As with the original gin based classic, notes of maraschino and violet subtly influence with lemon juice freshening and adding balance.

* 1¾ shot Patrón Silver Tequila (green seal) 100% agave tequila
* ½ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ¼ shot Créme de violette liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Cadáver Reviver

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The combination of tequila and triple sec make this riff on the classic Corpse Reviver remarkably Margarita-like, only with added complexity and subtlety due to the aromatised wine and faintest hint of absinthe.

* ¾ shot Patrón Silver Tequila (green seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¾ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¾ shot Lillet Blanc French aperitif wine
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 2 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Mexican Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Tequila replaces vodka in this riff on the French Martini. Considering tequila is replacing vodka you’d think blanco tequila would work best, but after trying this and reposado we found añejo tequila works best with the tropical and berry fruits.

* 2 shot Patrón Añejo Tequila
* ⅓ shot Black raspberry liqueur
* 1 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge on rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Dama Blanca

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This tequila (in place of gin) based riff on a White Lady is basically a Margarita made with lemon rather than lime, softened and smoothed by egg white. This is a delightful drink. Go easy spraying the zest as this can overly dominate the drink. It also works best with a light agave syrup as the darker versions affect its virgin-like hue and can add unwanted caramel notes.

* 1½ shot Patrón Silver Tequila (green seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¾ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅓ shot AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Negroni Bianco

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This white Negroni is not quite as dry and bitter as a traditional red Negroni and has additional pleasing creamy honeysuckle notes.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Luxardo Bitter Bianco Liqueur
* 1 shot Martini Bianco Vermouth
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into ice-filled glass and lightly STIR.

---

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Luxardo Bitter Bianco Liqueur
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into ice-filled glass and lightly STIR.

### Ginger Last Word

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As the name suggests this is simply a Last Word with a hint of ginger. Simple can be beautiful.

* 2 slice Fresh root ginger (thumbnail sized)
* ¾ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ¾ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist (discarded)

**Instructions:** MUDDLE ginger with gin in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Creme Egg Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As befits the name, this chocolate and vanilla vodka-based Easter Egg of a cocktail has both cream and egg – the later in the form of Dutch advocaat.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka (infused with vanilla)
* ½ shot Lightly spiced vanilla liqueur
* ½ shot Creme de cacao liqueur (white)
* ½ shot Warninks Advocaat liqueur
* ½ shot Single cream / half-and-half
* Garnish: Coat rim of glass with chocolate – use a microwave to melt a few squares of dark chocolate in a saucer and then and dip the rim of the glass into the melted chocolate. Grate chocolate over surface of the drink and add half a Cadbury Creme Egg skewered on a stick. It’s easier to cut the chocolate egg when straight from the refrigerator (a good test for how sharp your knife is). Spear the egg with a metal cocktail stick that has been heated under hot water.

**Instructions:** 1. To flavour your vodka with a vanilla pod. Simply cut the vanilla pod lengthways to expose the flavoursome seeds inside and drop the scored vanilla pod into your bottle of vodka. Reseal and shake bottle several times a day for at least two days, preferably a week.
2. SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Jäger Negroni

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A lightly spicy Negroni perfectly suited to the after-dinner “digestive” moment. If it doesn’t aid your digestion it will aid your sleep.

* ¾ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ¾ shot Jägermeister Liqueur
* ¼ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into ice-filled glass and briefly STIR. (Ideally, pre-mix ingredients and age in medium toasted oak barrel for one week.)

---

### Duchess

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Aniseed and liquorice notes from absinthe pervade this vermouth based cocktail, even though we have dramatically reduced the amount used from the original recipe which calls for equal parts of each ingredient. The Duchess is a drink for absinthe lovers.

* 1½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ½ shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* ½ shot Chilled water
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist.

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Smoking Gun Vesper

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Delicately smoky and almost meaty – be sure to serve with cured meat. A great aperitif cocktail.

* 1½ shot Oak Smoked Vodka
* ½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¼ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 1 dash Jerry Thomas bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist & small strip cured smoked pork on a skewer.

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Celery Sour

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This aptly named drink is beautifully balanced with delicate celery flavours.

* 1½ shot Rutte Celery Dry Gin
* ⅔ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅓ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1/12 shot Fee Brothers Celery Bitters
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Celery stick

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Celery Gimlet #2

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Sweet ‘n’ sour, salt ‘n’ vinegar served with dry celery gin crunch – a cocktail to awaken your senses.

* 6 inch Celery stick (chopped) (chopped)
* 1 pinch Salt
* 1½ shot Rutte Celery Dry Gin
* ¼ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ⅛ shot Chardonnay white wine vinegar
* 2 dash Fee Brothers Celery Bitters
* Garnish: Celery stick

**Instructions:** MUDDLE celery with salt in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Espresso Martini (simple 3 equal parts recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Balanced, tasty and enlivening, this cocktail is incredibly quick and easy to make using just three ingredients that should be every day essentials in every domestic kitchen.

* 1 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot Coffee liqueur
* 1 shot Espresso coffee (freshly made & hot)
* Garnish: Float 3 coffee beans on surface

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Ill Viaggio

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The ingredients might suggest that this cocktail should be stirred – we did try, but it benefits from the dilution and life that shaking imparts. After some elbow grease you’ll have a delicious bittersweet, herbal almond, after dinner drink.

* 1½ shot Disaronno Originale Amaretto liqueur
* 1 shot Rabarbaro
* 3 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass (preferably over a chunk of block ice).

as a bloody shark attack (or use grenadine)

### The Artist's Muse

* Garnish: Atomise absinthe over surface of cocktail

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

### For Sake's Sake

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Being dyslexic I’m bewildered as to how to spell dyslexic, while also amused by sake (the beverage brewed from rice) being spelt the same way as sake (as in for fuck’s sake!). Hopefully, you’ll find this aromatic, subtly orange influenced sake and rum-based cocktail both delightful to drink and easy to spell.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1½ shot Junmai ginjō sake
* ⅓ shot Italicus Rosolio di Bergamotto Liqueur
* ⅓ shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* Garnish: Float thin apple slice

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

### Bamboo Cocktail (Stuart's 1904 recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Thought to be the original Bamboo recipe with 2 parts dry fino sherry to 1 part rich sweet vermouth (modern recipes are usually equal parts). Balanced and complex, heavier than Bamboo recipes with dry vermouth.

* 2 shot Fino sherry
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** 

---

### Kiwi Caipirinha

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Fruity and refreshing, perfect for a summer’s afternoon.

* ½ fresh Fresh lime (chopped)
* 3 spoon Caster sugar
* ½ fresh Kiwi fruit (chopped)
* 2 shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca (from freezer)
* Garnish: Stirrer (spoon, wooden lolly stick or stick cut from sugar cane)

**Instructions:** 1. Cut lime in half (from pole to pole) and then slice one of the halves into eight 3-4mm thick half-moon shaped segments and drop into the base of a robust rocks glass.

2. Add 3 bar spoons caster sugar (or ½oz/15ml sugar syrup 2:1) and MUDDLE.

3. Add slices of kiwi and MUDDLE some more.

4. When sure fruit juice is fully extracted and the sugar dissolved, transfer the muddled fruit and sugar into serving glass (preferably a 30cl / 10oz hi-ball glass).

5. POUR cachaça (stored in the freezer) into the rocks glass (used to muddle) and swirl to rinse glass before pouring cachaça into serving glass. STIR to ensure all ingredients are well mixed.

6. Crack (rather than crush) four to five large ice cubes and drop into serving glass. STIR before topping with more ice and serve with a stirrer (but no straws).

---

### Purple Stag

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Easy drinking and neither bitter or too sweet, it’s hard not to like this rich herbal fruity cocktail.

* 1⅔ shot Jägermeister Liqueur

* 1 spoon Blackcurrant jam (preserve)
* Garnish: 3 blackberries

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

* 2 drop Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (discarded) & olive - preferably pimiento-stuffed (‘pimola’ olive)

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

### Pomegranate Daiquiri

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Freshly pressed pomegranate juice is essential to the success of this deliciously fruity but dry daiquiri. Sadly, packaged juice doesn’t produce the same drink.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ¾ shot Pomegranate juice
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Lime wedge & pomegranate seeds

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Scandinavian Daiquiri

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A caraway influenced riff on a daiquiri with aquavit replacing rum. Very refreshing and suited to a summer’s afternoon, or an early evening aperitif.

* 2 shot Lysholm Linie Aquavit
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Star anise

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with and strain into chilled glass.

### Courtside

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Easy drinking, fruity, refreshing and lightly sweet. Bring on the summer’s afternoon.

* 1 fresh Small ripe strawberries (hulled)
* 3 fresh Raspberries
* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* 1½ shot Pressed apple juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Top with berries and mint sprig

**Instructions:** MUDDLE berries in base of shaker. Add next five ingredients (all but soda), SHAKE with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with soda.

---

### Watermelon Caipirinha

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The melon flavours are very subtle in this delicious Caipirinha.

* ½ fresh Fresh lime (chopped)
* 3 spoon Caster sugar
* ½ cupful Fresh watermelon (chopped)
* 2 shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca (from freezer)
* Garnish: Stirrer (spoon, wooden lolly stick or stick cut from sugar cane)

**Instructions:** 1. Cut lime in half (from pole to pole) and then slice one of the halves into eight 3-4mm thick half-moon shaped segments and drop into the base of a robust rocks glass.

2. Add 3 bar spoons caster sugar (or ½oz / 15ml sugar syrup 2:1) and MUDDLE.

3. Add watermelon and MUDDLE some more.

4. When sure fruit juice is fully extracted and the sugar dissolved, transfer the muddled fruit and sugar into serving glass (preferably a 30cl / 10oz hi-ball glass).

5. POUR cachaça (stored in the freezer) into the rocks glass (used to muddle) and swirl to rinse glass before pouring cachaça into serving glass. STIR to ensure all ingredients are well mixed.

6. Crack (rather than crush) four to five large ice cubes and drop into serving glass. STIR before topping with more ice and serve with a stirrer (but no straws).

---

### Melon Caipirinha

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Exactly as the name suggests, a fruity, melon flavoured Caipirinha.

* ½ fresh Fresh lime (chopped)
* 3 spoon Caster sugar
* 1 slice Cantaloupe melon
* 2 shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca (from freezer)
* Garnish: Stirrer (spoon, wooden lolly stick or stick cut from sugar cane)

**Instructions:** 1. Cut lime in half (from pole to pole) and then slice one of the halves into eight 3-4mm thick half-moon shaped segments and drop into the base of a robust rocks glass.

2. Add 3 bar spoons caster sugar (or ½oz / 15ml sugar syrup 2:1) and MUDDLE.

3. Add melon and MUDDLE some more.

4. When sure fruit juice is fully extracted and the sugar dissolved, transfer the muddled fruit and sugar into serving glass (preferably a 30cl / 10oz hi-ball glass).

5. POUR cachaça (stored in the freezer) into the rocks glass (used to muddle) and swirl to rinse glass before pouring cachaça into serving glass. STIR to ensure all ingredients are well mixed.

6. Crack (rather than crush) four to five large ice cubes and drop into serving glass. STIR before topping with more ice and serve with a stirrer (but no straws).

---

### Melon & Apple Caipirinha

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Melon and lime dominate this deliciously fruity Caipirinha.

* ½ fresh Fresh lime (chopped)
* 3 spoon Caster sugar
* 1 slice Cantaloupe melon (chopped)
* ¼ shot Pressed apple juice
* 2 shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca
* Garnish: Stirrer (spoon, wooden lolly stick or stick cut from sugar cane)

**Instructions:** 1. Cut lime in half (from pole to pole) and then slice one of the halves into eight 3-4mm thick half-moon shaped segments and drop into the base of a robust rocks glass.

2. Add 3 bar spoons caster sugar (or ½oz / 15ml sugar syrup 2:1) and MUDDLE.

3. Add melon and MUDDLE some more.

4. When sure fruit juice is fully extracted and the sugar dissolved, transfer the muddled fruit and sugar into serving glass (preferably a 30cl / 10oz hi-ball glass).

5. POUR cachaça (stored in the freezer) into the rocks glass (used to muddle) and swirl to rinse glass before pouring cachaça into serving glass. Add apple juice and STIR to ensure all ingredients are well mixed.

6. Crack (rather than crush) four to five large ice cubes and drop into serving glass. STIR before topping with more ice and serve with a stirrer (but no straws).

---

### Pineapple Caipirinha

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Natural acids from the pineapple make this more tart in flavour than some other fruit Caipirinhas, those with a sweet tooth may want to add an extra ½ spoon of sugar.

* ½ fresh Fresh lime (chopped)
* 3 spoon Caster sugar
* ½ slice Pineapple (fresh) (chopped)
* 2 shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca (from freezer)
* Garnish: Stirrer (spoon, wooden lolly stick or stick cut from sugar cane)

**Instructions:** 1. Cut lime in half (from pole to pole) and then slice one of the halves into eight 3-4mm thick half-moon shaped segments and drop into the base of a robust rocks glass.

2. Add 3 bar spoons caster sugar (or ½oz / 15ml sugar syrup 2:1) and MUDDLE.

3. Add pineapple and MUDDLE some more.

4. When sure fruit juice is fully extracted and the sugar dissolved, transfer the muddled fruit and sugar into serving glass (preferably a 30cl / 10oz hi-ball glass).

5. POUR cachaça (stored in the freezer) into the rocks glass (used to muddle) and swirl to rinse glass before pouring cachaça into serving glass. STIR to ensure all ingredients are well mixed.

6. Crack (rather than crush) four to five large ice cubes and drop into serving glass. STIR before topping with more ice and serve with a stirrer (but no straws).

---

### Difford's Fruit Cup No.3 (Cognac based)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Cognac works well in this fruit cup, rounding the other ingredients to present as a more harmonious blend when compared to the same recipe made with gin. However, it’s more of a winter’s cup, without the freshening edge expected of a summer’s fruit cup.

* 1 shot Cognac
* 1 shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* 2 shot Ginger ale
* 2 shot Coca-Cola
* Garnish: Lemon, orange & strawberry slices, mint sprig & borage

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into glass. Half fill glass with ice. Add a citrus slice and a couple of mint leaves from garnish before filling to brim with ice. Finish with rest of garnish.

---

### Difford's Fruit Cup No.6 (Vodka based)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Vodka’s clean neutrality allows the fruity flavours in this summery cocktail to shine. It’s not surprising, that of the original line-up of seven different Pimm’s spirit bases, only No.1 (gin) and No.6 (vodka) survive.

* 1 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* 2 shot Ginger ale
* 2 shot Coca-Cola
* Garnish: Lemon, orange & strawberry slices, mint sprig & borage

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into glass. Half fill glass with ice. Add a citrus slice and a couple of mint leaves from garnish before filling to brim with ice. Finish with rest of garnish.

---

### Difford's Fruit Cup No.12 (Genever based)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Given the use of genever and orange curaçao, this cocktail should be named “Dutch Fruit Cup”. Genever’s sweet maltiness adds a bready character to this fruit cup.

* 1 shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* 1 shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* 2 shot Ginger ale
* 2 shot Coca-Cola
* Garnish: Lemon, orange & strawberry slices, mint sprig & borage

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into glass. Half fill glass with ice. Add a citrus slice and a couple of mint leaves from garnish before filling to brim with ice. Finish with rest of garnish.

---

### Pineapple Martini (1990s recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Deliciously simple, fruity and ridiculously easy to drink. The quality and freshness of your pineapple juice is key to the success of this cocktail, which can also be made by muddling fresh pineapple.

We'd also suggest you try our own Pineapple Martini Recipe.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1½ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge on rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### La Sang Jaune (The Yellow Blood)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Spirituous apple and rich elderflower with herbal dry vermouth and gentian complexity, finished with the merest hint of anise courtesy of a dash of absinthe.

* 1⅔ shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* ⅔ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ½ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* ⅙ shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* 1 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* Garnish: Lemon & orange zest twists

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain to ice-filled glass.

---

### Czechmate

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The herbal notes of Becherovka are noted for combining harmoniously with beer, fittingly in this recipe a pilsner (Becherovka is Czech, as are the origins of pilsner). This combo is fortified with vodka and freshened with lemon juice to produce a long refreshing cocktail which makes a great alternative to merely drinking beer.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Becherovka Original (Carlsbad Becher) Liqueur
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 shot Budweiser Budvar Pilsner
* Garnish: Lemon wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 4 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with pilsner.

---

### Shadow Boxer

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As the name suggests this is a punchy cocktail – spirituous and bittersweet with a long bitter finish. Far from being a crowd-pleaser.

* 1½ shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca
* ¾ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* ¾ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ¼ shot Pamplemousse rosé (pink grapefruit) liqueur
* ¼ shot Eau-de-Vie d'Abricot
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass (preferably over a chunk of block ice).

---

### French 75 (Judge Jr's 1927 recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Judge Jr’s original 1927 recipe calls for "2 jiggers Gordon water; 1 part lemon juice; a spoonful of powdered sugar; cracked ice. Fill up the rest of a tall glass with champagne!" I’ve loosely interpreted this recipe to the one above (with the 3 spoons of powdered sugar being flat 5ml measuring spoons). The result is dangerously quaffable gin spiked champagne with a zesty lemon bite. The powered sugar adds an attractive sherbet note, but if you prefer to use sugar syrup then substitute with ½oz/15ml (2:1).

* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 3 spoon Powdered sugar (or use 5ml of 2:1 sugar syrup per spoon)
* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 3 shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Lemon slice

**Instructions:** STIR powdered sugar with lemon juice in base of shaker until sugar dissolves. Add gin, SHAKE with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with champagne and lightly stir.

---

### Lemon Sherbet Margarita

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This margarita does indeed have a sherbet flavour with a lemony citrus bite.

* 1½ shot Patrón Silver Tequila (green seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¾ shot Pallini Limoncello Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅓ shot AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* 1 scoop Lemon sorbet
* Garnish: Float lemon sorbet balls (made with melon baller)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Brazuca Remedy

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Bittersweet and complex with underlying cachaça character. Perfect as an aperitivo.

* ⅓ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1 spoon Runny honey
* 1½ shot Capucana Handcrafted Cachaca
* ⅔ shot Pallini Limoncello Liqueur
* ⅔ shot Aperol Aperitivo by Fratelli Barbieri
* 3 fresh Basil leaves
* ½ fresh Egg white
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist & float basil leaf

**Instructions:** POUR lemon and honey into shaker and stir until honey dissolves. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Renaissance

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Spirituous and bittersweet with a cleansing citrusy bite and underlying cognac complexity, this cocktail is suited to both aperitif and after-dinner occasions.

* 1½ shot Cognac
* ¼ shot Pallini Limoncello Liqueur
* ½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 2 dash Peach bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Red Earl

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This vodka laced, rich (but not overly sweet) raspberry cocktail is a crowd pleaser.

* 10 fresh Raspberries
* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Pallini Limoncello Liqueur
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Float raspberry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### French 125 (French '75' with cognac) Jones' 1977 recipe

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Jones' original 1977 built in the glass recipe, which consists: 2oz/60ml cognac, 1oz/30ml lemon juice and 2 spoons sugar, topped with champagne, is a powerful drink. Hence, we hope Jones would approve of our tweaking his recipe. The result still has plenty of oomph behind it, but with the extra dilution of shaking, is a tad more harmonious.

* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 3 spoon Powdered sugar (or use 5ml of 2:1 sugar syrup per spoon)
* 1½ shot Cognac
* 3 shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR powdered sugar with lemon juice in base of shaker until sugar dissolves. Add bourbon, SHAKE with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with champagne and lightly stir.

---

### Pineapple Daiquiri (simple but tasty recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Light rum provides vibrancy while aged rum adds rich complexity. Pineapple juice adds tropical fruitiness and replaces the dilution necessary to open and amplify a classic Daiquiri.

* 1 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* ½ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Fin de Siècle (End of Century) Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Dry, spirituous and zesty, this is a cocktail that lends itself equally to aperitif or after dinner occasions.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* ¼ shot Picon Amer
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Beginning of the End

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Burnt orange oils add smoky notes, complexity and balance to this bitter-sweet drink. A perfect after-dinner cocktail.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* ½ shot Carpano Antica Formula Vermouth
* ⅓ shot Picon Amer
* ⅓ shot Oloroso sherry
* Garnish: Flamed orange zest twist

**Instructions:** FLAME an orange zest twist into empty glass to line the inside with smoky oils. Then STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into the pre-prepared glass.

---

### Slow Comfortable Screw Against a Cold Hard Wall

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Sloe gin is the 'Slow', Sothern Comfort is the 'Comfortable', vodka and orange juice are the 'Screw' (as in Screwdriver), ice is the 'Cold', overproof rum the 'Hard' and Galliano the 'Wall' (as in Harvey Wallbanger). The result is a much better drink than the sleazy name might suggest, at least it is when freshly squeezed orange juice is used.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Rutte Sloe Gin liqueur
* ½ shot Southern Comfort Liqueur
* 3 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ¼ shot Galliano L'Autentico liqueur
* ¼ shot White overproof rum
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** STIR first 4 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. Then FLOAT Galliano and overproof rum.

---

### Slow Comfortable Screw Against The Wall With A Bang

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** One of the better Sloe Comfortable Screw derivations - Overproof rum provides the “Bang”. Boozy fruity and balanced rather than sweet – what’s not to like?

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot White overproof rum
* ½ shot Rutte Sloe Gin liqueur
* ½ shot Southern Comfort Liqueur
* 3 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ½ shot Galliano L'Autentico liqueur
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** STIR first 5 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. Finish with a FLOAT of Galliano.

---

### Slow Comfortable Mexican Screw Against the Wall

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Tequila adds a Mexican touch to the Slow Screw family to create a tasty riff on a Screwdriver. Great for a lazy summer afternoon or a barbeque.

* ¾ shot Patrón Silver Tequila (green seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¾ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Southern Comfort Liqueur
* 3 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ½ shot Rutte Sloe Gin liqueur
* ½ shot Galliano L'Autentico liqueur
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** STIR first 4 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. FLOAT sloe gin on surface so it bleeds into drink. Finish with Galliano FLOAT.

---

### Slow Comfortable Screw Between the Sheets

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The rum and cognac combo from Between the Sheets
served as part of the Slow Comfortable genre. As with so many of the Slow Comfortable family of cocktails, when made with freshly squeezed orange juice, this is a tasty, fruity and balanced long drink.

* ½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Cognac
* ½ shot Southern Comfort Liqueur
* ½ shot Rutte Sloe Gin liqueur
* 3½ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Gin Tonica

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Something of a Spanish phenomenon, where the G&T (which in England has been traditionally served in a tall slim Collins glass) tends to be served in a huge goldfish bowl of a glass – big enough to house garnishes ranging from cardamom pods and juniper berries to fruit peels and slices of ginger.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 5 shot Tonic water
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist, lime wedge & 3 cardamom pods

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into ice-filled glass and lightly stir.

---

### Red Earl (Salvatore's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Fresh ginger adds a hint to spice which combines well with raspberry fruit in this crowd-pleasing vodka-based cocktail which is freshened by a dash of limoncello.

* 1 slice Fresh root ginger (thumbnail sized)
* 10 fresh Raspberries
* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ⅔ shot Pallini Limoncello Liqueur
* 1/12 shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water) (optional)
* Garnish: Float raspberry

**Instructions:** MUDDLE ginger and then raspberries in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Eclipse Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Beautifully balanced bitter-sweetness with tequila and mezcal sitting harmoniously with cherry and aperitivo liqueurs, with lemon freshness. A perfect aperitivo cocktail.

* 1 shot Patrón Añejo Tequila
* ¾ shot Cherry Heering cherry brandy liqueur
* ¾ shot Aperol Aperitivo by Fratelli Barbieri
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Del Maguey VIDA de San Luis del Rio 100% agave blanco mezcal Buy from amazon
* Garnish: None

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 4 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass (preferably over a chunk of block ice). FLOAT mezcal on surface of drink.

---

### Negrino

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A riff on the classic Negroni from Vietnam which brilliantly set the richness of sloe gin against bone dry fino sherry while harnessing the herbal bitterness of gentian. Hit the right dilution, and by the third sip, when your palate has adjusted, you’ll not be able to stop sipping this bitter aperitif cocktail.

* 1⅓ shot Rutte Sloe Gin liqueur
* 1 shot Fino sherry
* ⅔ shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* Garnish: Pink grapefruit wedge & scorched rosemary sprig

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into ice-filled glass and STIR.

---

### Pirate Queen

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Lightly spicy with an attractive underlying bready fruitiness from the fresh strawberry and genever.

* 1 fresh Small ripe strawberries (hulled)
* 1 shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* 1 shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ⅙ shot Honey syrup
* 1/12 shot Ginger sugar syrup
* 1/12 shot Cinnamon sugar syrup
* 1 dash Creole bitters
* Garnish: Dust with freshly grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** MUDDLE strawberry in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass over chunk of block ice.

---

### Fade To Black Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A Rum Sour blackened with blackberries and activated charcoal. The black charcoal which makes this cocktail black does little for the taste and given the potential issues with charcoal this tasty cocktail is perhaps best appreciated without its addition (as illustrated photographed here).

* 5 fresh Blackberries
* 2 shot Bacardi OakHeart Spiced Rum
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* 1 spoon Activated charcoal powder
* Garnish: Float 3 drops Angostura Bitters

**Instructions:** MUDDLE blackberries in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Le Premier Word Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A riff on a last word with a splash of cider, which depending on your cider will produce a boozy cocktail that’s on the dry side.

* ¾ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur
* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 1½ shot Medium dry apple cider
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist & mist with Islay scotch

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 3 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass (preferably over a chunk of block ice). TOP with cider and light stir.

---

### Dr. Rieux

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Rounded, citrusy and delicately spicy with an attractive underlying funk from Swedish punch.

* 1 shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* 1 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)

* ¼ shot Demerara sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist & demerara sugar rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled and rimmed glass.

---

### Macca Margarita

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Orange juice adds fruity dilution to what could also be called a Breakfast Margarita. Sir Paul McCartney is said to like his Margaritas made with a splash of freshly squeezed orange juice, hence this recipe is named in his honour.

* 1½ shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¾ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* 1/12 shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Half salted rim with split lime & orange wheels on rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### The Italian Job Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Bittersweet and boozy with a dry finish. Striking the right degree of dilution is key to the success of this cocktail – stir a little longer than usual and if using ice straight from the freezer perhaps consider adding a dash of chilled water.

* ¾ shot Smith & Cross Traditional Pot Still Jamaican Rum
* ¾ shot Aperitivo Cocchi Americano Bianco
* ¾ shot Aperol Aperitivo by Fratelli Barbieri
* ¾ shot Byrrh Grand Quinquina Aromatized Wine
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (discarded) & dehydrated orange wheel

**Instructions:** STIR all the ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Swiss Watch

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As Peter Konkoly, this cocktail’s creator says, it is reminiscent of a Last Word. However, we prefer this tasty drink served on-the-rocks as an aperitif alternative to a Negroni, rather than straight-up as originally specified by Peter.

* 1 shot G. Miclo Kirsch Vieux Grande Reserve Eau de Vie
* 1 shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* 1 shot Chartreuse Jaune (Yellow Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ⅔ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Garnish: Powdered sugar rim. (Note: Lemon zest can be floated on the drink, halved with the shape of 'V', to show the time 2pm)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into ice-filled sugar rimmed glass.

* Garnish: Thyme spring

### Jersey's Best Dancers

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Three equal part ingredients, the holy grail of cocktail recipes, makes for a dry spirituous aperitif cocktail. Three equal part ingredients, the holy grail of cocktail recipes, makes for a dry spirituous aperitif cocktail. This cocktail is very similar to a Maximiliano Cocktail.

Incidentally, Jersey's Best Dancers is the third studio album by the New Jersey band Lifetime (released June 1997).

* 1 shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon

### Castle Cobbler

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A fruity bittersweet aperitif with “orchard fruit, citrus and bittersweet gentian sipped through a sarsaparilla-like layer of Peychaud’s Bitters.”

* 1½ shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* 1 shot Byrrh Grand Quinquina Aromatized Wine
* ½ shot Crème de pêche (peach) liqueur
* ⅙ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅙ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* 9 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* Garnish: Mint sprig & lemon wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 5 ingredients with ice and strain into glass filled with pebble ice. Float Peychaud's on drink.

---

### The Duchess Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Gin’s light gin botanical spice combines with rich orange and complex vinous notes from the combination of Sauvignon Blanc wine and dry vermouth.

* ¾ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* ¾ shot Sauvignon blanc white wine
* ¾ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Mexican Duchess

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Spirituous and lightly vinous with subtle agave notes, bready genever and spicy gin all refreshed by zesty orange curaçao. Five equal parts is a faff to measure for individual cocktails but a dream to batch.

* ⅔ shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ⅔ shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* ⅔ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ⅔ shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* ⅔ shot Dopo Teatro Cocchi Vermouth Amaro
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Dutch Orange Cup

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Easy drinking, fruity, summery and gin laced with caramel vermouth freshened by zesty orange.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* 2½ shot Ginger ale
* Garnish: Orange slice, strawberry slices, mint sprig, orange zest twist & borage when in season

**Instructions:** POUR all ingredients into glass half filled with ice. Add a orange slice and a couple of mint leaves from the garnish before filling to the brim with more ice and rest of garnish.

---

### Mai Dutch Tai

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Wonderfully fruity with underlying bready genever replacing the almond notes from the orgeat syrup almond notes of a classic Trader Vic Mai Tai.

* 1½ shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* 1 shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* 1½ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 2 dash La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* Garnish: Mint sprig, lime shell & fruit stick

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. Crown with crushed ice.

---

### No Borders

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A tasty bittersweet Negroni-style aperitif.

* 1 shot Freya Birch Spirit
* ⅔ shot Suze gentian liqueur Buy from amazon
* ⅔ shot Italicus Rosolio di Bergamotto Liqueur
* ⅓ shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* Garnish: Fresh bay leaf

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Wild & Dirty Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Pine (birch) notes mix well with the vermouth in this 2:1 Martini with lemon bitters adding citrus freshness the olive and rosemary sprig garnish adding to the cocktails aroma and complexity.

* 2 shot Freya Birch Spirit
* 1 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 1 dash Lemon bitters
* Garnish: Kalamata olive & rosemary sprig

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Pan Galactic Gargle Blaster

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Orange, basil and red berries laced with vodka makes for a well-balanced, easy drinking fruity cocktail - arguably too easy for a drink titled Pan Galactic Gargle Blaster which is said to be like "having your brains smashed in by a slice of lemon wrapped round a large gold brick". Remember, Beeblebrox advises "never drink more than two Pan Galactic Gargle Blasters unless you are a thirty ton mega elephant with bronchial pneumonia".

* 10 fresh Basil leaves
* ⅔ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ⅔ shot Black raspberry liqueur
* ½ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ⅙ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* 1⅔ shot Cranberry juice
* 1⅔ shot Strawberry puree
* Garnish: Dust with lots of freshly grounded black pepper

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into glass filled with crushed ice.

---

### Del Famoso (The Famous)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Adapted from a recipe created in June 2017 by Nathan Hinze at 99 Hanover Street, Edinburgh, Scotland. The cocktail’s name is inspired by the wording on the Fernet Branca label.

* 1½ shot Patrón Silver Tequila (green seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¾ shot Fernet Branca digestive bitter liqueur
* ½ shot Carpano Antica Formula Vermouth
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: None

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

### First Emperor

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Grassy spirituous agricole rhum is mellowed by fruity pineapple, sweet herbal liqueur and vinous herbal vermouth.

* 1½ shot Lillet Blanc French aperitif wine
* ½ shot Clément Canne Bleue 2016 Martinique Rhum blanc Agricole
* ¼ shot Chartreuse Jaune (Yellow Chartreuse) Liqueur
* ¼ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### The Windfall

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** An autumnal sounding cocktail to be enjoyed in place of a Daiquiri at any time of the year. Yes, it’s appley with delicate armagnac undertones and complexity, but it is made interesting by the birch spirit which gives this drink faint pine, almost smoky bacon notes.

* 1⅔ shot Freya Birch Spirit
* ⅓ shot Armagnac brandy
* 1⅔ shot Pressed apple juice
* Garnish: Dehydrated apple

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Sage Sazerac

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Subtle notes of pine, pastis and sage combine in this pre-dinner sipper of a cocktail.

* ⅙ shot Ricard Pastis de Marseille
* 3 fresh Sage leaves
* 1⅔ shot Freya Birch Spirit
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 drop Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Fresh sage leaf

**Instructions:** Rinse chilled glass Pastis and set aside. MUDDLE sage in base of stirring glass. Add other ingredients, STIR with ice and fine strain into the pre-rinsed glass over fresh ice (preferably a chunk of block ice).

---

### Claridge Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Gin for strength, vermouth for dryness and liqueur to sweeten - an interesting combination.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* ½ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ½ shot De Kuyper Apricot Brandy Liqueur
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice & fine strain into chilled glass.

### Classic Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Reminiscent of a Sidecar with Maraschino.

* 2 shot Cognac
* ½ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* ½ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (& optional sugar rim)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Death Star

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This equal parts stirred down cocktail is either a boozy aperitif or a bittersweet digestif come nightcap. Whatever classification, it’s tasty.

* 1 shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco
* 1 shot Liquore Strega Giuseppe Alberti
* 1 shot Cynar Ricetta Originale Artichoke Amaro Liqueur
* 1 dash Bittermens Hopped Grapefruit Bitters
* Garnish: Float Star anise

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Purpurina Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** With a whole measure of watermelon syrup, you may expect this cocktail to be on the sweet side. Instead, it is beautifully balanced with delicate Jalapeño heat – at least it is if you go easy with the amount of Jalapeño you infuse in your pisco.

* 2 shot BarSol Supremo Mosto Verde Italia Pisco (Jalapeño chilli infused)
* 1 shot Giffard Watermelon Liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Dehydrated jalapeño slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Four Poster Red

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This deep cherry red Negroni-like aperitivo is equally tasty shaken and served straight-up – indeed that’s how it was originally made, like a Shakerato. If served shaken, then a white head should cover the drink’s surface, or it’s not been shaken hard enough. The cocktail should then be consumed before the head fades. Either shaken or stirred, sweet vermouth/port predominates with Campari providing balances bitterness.

* 1 shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1 shot Dolin Chambéryzette Aperitif A La Fraise
* 1 shot Warre's Otima 10 Year Old Tawny Port
* 1 shot Campari Bitter Liqueur
* Garnish: Maraschino cherry or strawberry

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass (preferably over a chunk of block ice).

---

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Gin laced, tangy, herbal, fruity and citrusy.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Liquore Strega Giuseppe Alberti
* ½ shot De Kuyper Apricot Brandy Liqueur
* ½ shot G. Miclo Kirsch Vieux Grande Reserve Eau de Vie
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice

* Garnish: Apricot wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Collins

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Some say the John/Tom Collins was originally made with jenever. So is this the original or an adaptation on the Tom Collins. We will probably never know, but it tastes great.

* 2 shot Rutte Old Simon Genever
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Orange slice & Luxardo Maraschino cherry on stick (sail)

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 3 ingredients with ice & strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with soda, stir and serve with straws.

---

### Lo Stregone

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Crodino and Strega make a very tasty and very Italian aperitivo. Go easy on the Angostura.

* 1 shot Liquore Strega Giuseppe Alberti
* 1 shot Crodino
* 4 drop Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Grapefruit zest twist & mint sprig

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into ice-filled glass and briefly stir.
