### Egg Sour

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A well-balanced sour with brandy and orange zestiness shaken with a whole egg. Try it. This combo is tastier than it sounds.

* 1 shot Cognac
* 1 shot Pierre Ferrand Ancienne Methode Dry Curacao
* ⅓ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 whole Egg (white & yolk)
* Garnish: Float 3 small dashes Angostura bitters on surface of drink

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Velvet Revolver

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As Robb, the creator of this drink, says, it is “short strong and fruity, pulls out all the deeper notes from the cognac.”

* 1 spoon Strawberry conserve jam (heaped)
* 1⅔ shot Cognac
* ⅔ shot Pinot Noir red wine
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Half strawberry & mint sprig

**Instructions:** STIR strawberry conserve and cognac in base of shaker until conserve is dissolved. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Mariposa

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This rum laced cocktail has attractive savoury flavours with a tangy sourness and floral elderflower.

* 1 fresh Cherry tomato (chopped)
* 4 fresh Basil leaves
* 1⅔ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ⅚ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅚ shot St-Germain Elderflower Liqueur
* ⅙ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Half cherry tomato & small basil sprig on rim

**Instructions:** MUDDLE tomato in base of shaker and then muddle basil leaves. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Cherry Springer

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** We do like a pun, especially a tasty pun. Sweet and sour cherry fortified with gin notes and subtle freshening crème de menthe and delicate chocolate.

* 1⅓ shot Luxardo Sour Cherry Gin
* ⅓ shot Giffard Menthe Pastille white crème de menthe liqueur
* ⅓ shot Cherry Heering cherry brandy liqueur
* ⅔ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 2 dash Bob's Chocolate Bitters
* Garnish: Mint sprigs & Luxardo maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Champagne Piña Colada

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Deliciously creamy pineapple and coconut enlivened by champagne with rum notes shining through.

Variables such as the coconut sorbet used, the pineapple cordial in the original recipe (we’ve substituted with pineapple liqueur) and how generous the scoops of both sorbet and crushed ice, mean that we highly recommend you experience the original cocktail at London’s Coupette.

* ⅚ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ⅙ shot Clément Canne Bleue 2016 Martinique Rhum blanc Agricole
* ⅔ shot Giffard Premium Caribbean Pineapple Liqueur Buy from amazon
* ½ shot Brut Champagne
* 1½ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* 2 scoop *Special ingredient #1 (see below)
* 1½ shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Raw coconut (or toasted coconut flakes)

**Instructions:** BLEND first 6 ingredients with 4oz scoop of crushed ice (including 15ml/ ½oz champagne) and pour into chilled glass which has been pre-charged with 45ml/ 1½oz of chilled champagne.

Special ingredient #1: Coconut Sorbet 
Blend 100ml cream of coconut, 200ml coconut milk and 200ml coconut water on medium speed until fully mixed, then POUR into an ice-cream maker to chill and churn until desired consistency is obtained.

---

### Accoutrement

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Chris originally garnished this Calavdos Sidecare/Applecart-like cocktail with brandied cherries but Strega’s excellent chocolates seem a far more fitting accoutrement.

* 2 shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* ¾ shot Liquore Strega Giuseppe Alberti
* ½ shot Clément Créole Shrubb Liqueur D'Orange
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 2 dash Peychaud's Aromatic Bitters Buy from amazon
* Garnish: Strega chocolate across rim (or brandied cherries)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Champagne Julep

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Lower in strength than most old-school julep cocktails, champagne adds a zing if not a sparkle.

* 8 fresh Mint leaves
* ½ shot Cognac
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* 3 shot Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist (discarded) & mint sprigs dusted with icing sugar

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 4 ingredients with ice. Add champagne and more to shaker, then throw twice before straining into julep tin filled with crushed ice. Serve with a metal straw.

---

### Twelve Miles Out Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Stir or shake (as originally stipulated in The Savoy Cocktail Book) this cocktail it’s still boozy. However, it’s also wonderfully aromatic with all three ingredients combining harmoniously.

* ¾ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ¾ shot Carlshamns Flaggpunsch Original Swedish Punsch
* ¾ shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Lost Plane

* ¾ shot Goslings Black Seal Rum
* ¾ shot Aperol Aperitivo by Fratelli Barbieri

* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Black Daiquiri

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** More golden than black in appearance, this Daquiri takes its name from the black rum (well dark brown rum) it’s made from. Pungent rum notes sit well with zingy citrus.

* 1⅔ shot Goslings Black Seal Rum
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ⅓ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Lime wedge on rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Bloody Mary (no sugar & low-calorie)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** With vitamin loaded tomato and lemon juices, this sugar-free, low-calorie Mary is almost a healthy option.

Be sure to use a tomato juice with no added sugar and be aware that adding Worcestershire sauce will also contribute a very small amount of sugar.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* 3½ shot Tomato juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar-free sweetener
* 2 pinch Celery salt
* 3 grind Black pepper
* 10 drop Hot pepper sauce
* 4 dash Worcestershire sauce (optional)
* Garnish: Spiked cocktail onion, cherry tomato and lemon wedge with celery stick stirrer (optional salt & pepper rim)

**Instructions:** ROLL (rotate) all ingredients with ice in shaker (rather than shake) and strain into ice-filled glass. Use ice freshly from freezer to fill glass (not ice directly from ice-machine) to avoid unwanted dilution from melting ice.

---

### Daiquiri (no sugar & low-calorie)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Light and delicate, and not overly citrusy so allowing the rum to shine. And it’s sugar-free! At least it is if you choose your rum carefully.

* 1⅔ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar-free sweetener
* ⅓ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Lime wedge on rim

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Espresso Martini (no sugar & low-calorie)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Slightly thinner in mouthfeel than a regular sugar loaded Espresso Martini but equally as tasty.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1½ shot Espresso coffee (freshly made & hot)
* ⅖ shot Sugar-free sweetener
* ½ pinch Salt
* Garnish: Float 3 coffee beans

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Gimlet (no sugar & low-calorie)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Fresh lime juice replaces cordial in this vitamin C loaded, almost healthy gin laced sugar-free version of a classic Gimlet.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar-free sweetener
* Garnish: Express lime zest or two into glass and discard before pouring cocktail. Then place lime wedge on rim.

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Gin Basil Smash (no sugar & low-calorie)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Herbal and refreshing. Basil, gin and lemon sit harmoniously, balanced by sugar-free sweetener.

* 8 fresh Basil leaves
* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅖ shot Sugar-free sweetener
* Garnish: Basil leaf or sprig

**Instructions:** Gently MUDDLE basil in base of SHAKER with Gin. ADD other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Gin Sling (no sugar & low-calorie)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Light and refreshing with lemon freshening gin while a splash of sugar-free sweetener provides balance.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar-free sweetener
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Lemon slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 3 ingredients with ice and fine strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with soda water.

---

### Long Island Iced Tea (no sugar & low-calorie)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As the cola falls and bleeds its way through the otherwise clear drink (it takes noticeably long to fall than full sugar cola), it does end up looking remarkably like week black tea and indeed the taste isn’t so far removed from spirit laced weak tea with citrus fruit.

* ⅓ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ⅓ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ⅓ shot Ketel One Vodka
* ⅓ shot Patrón Silver Tequila (green seal) 100% agave tequila
* ⅓ shot Giffard Agave Sec liqueur
* ½ shot Sugar-free sweetener
* ⅖ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅖ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 2 shot Coca-Cola
* Garnish: Lemon wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 8 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with cola and briefly stir.

---

### Margarita (no sugar & low-calorie)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Tasty, zingy, low-calorie and sugar-free. What more can you ask of a Margarita?

* 1⅓ shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ½ shot Giffard Agave Sec liqueur
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ⅓ shot Sugar-free sweetener
* ½ pinch Salt
* Garnish: Salt rim (optional) & lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

* 1½ shot Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Mint sprigs

### Tom Collins (no sugar & low-calorie)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** If opting to make this Tom Collins with an Old Tom gin (as it should be), beware which brand you choose as many Old Tom gins contain sugar.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅔ shot Sugar-free sweetener
* 3 shot Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Orange slice & cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 3 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with soda and briefly stir.

---

### Vodka Sour (no sugar & low-calorie)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** As with most sours, adding a couple of dashes aromatic bitters greatly contributes to the cocktail’s flavour but this also adds trace amounts of sugar.

* 1½ shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ⅔ shot Sugar-free sweetener
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters (optional)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Lemon slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Coolman Cocktail

* 1¾ shot Ketel One Vodka

### Cosmopolitan Cocktail (Difford's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The Cosmopolitan was originally made with citrus vodka but this recipe works just as well with unflavoured vodka, and when a good quality cranberry juice is used, we prefer the simplicity of unflavoured vodka in this cocktail.

* 1 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* 1½ shot Cranberry juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters (optional)
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (flamed)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Aku Aku

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This Tiki classic looks a little like frozen stagnant pond water but tastes minty fresh and rather good.

### Algeria

* ½ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur

* ¾ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Almond Old Fashioned (tequila based)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** One to please fans of both tequila and the Old Fashioned drinks genre with amaretto adding the headline hint of almond.

* 2 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ¼ shot Disaronno Originale Amaretto liqueur
* ¼ shot AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* 3 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR one shot of tequila with two ice cubes in a glass. Add amaretto, agave syrup, bitters and two more ice cubes. Stir some more then add another two ice cubes and the remaining tequila. Stir lots more so as to melt ice then add more ice. The melting and stirring in of ice cubes is essential to the dilution and taste of the drink.

---

### Angel Face

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Rich apricot and apple with a backbone of botanical gin. Balanced rather than dry or sweet.

This drink looks better when stirred but the original 1930 recipe is shaken and we think it tastes better for it - that is unless you add some water to increase the dilution of the stirred recipe.

* 1 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* 1 shot De Kuyper Apricot Brandy Liqueur
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Apple wedge

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and fine strain into a chilled glass.

---

### Angel's Share #1

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Tangy citrus fruit and cognac smoothed with a hint of vanilla.

* 1 spoon English orange marmalade
* 2 shot Cognac
* ¼ shot Lightly spiced vanilla liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR heaped spoon of orange marmalade with cognac in base of shaker until marmalade dissolves. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Angel's Share #2

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A fabulous drink, especially when VEP Chartreuse, family reserve cognac and 20 year old tawny port are used as per the original Starlight Room recipe.

* ¼ shot Chartreuse Verte (Green Chartreuse) Liqueur
* 1½ shot Cognac
* ¾ shot Toschi Nocello Walnut Liqueur de Noix
* ½ shot Warre's Otima 10 Year Old Tawny Port
* Garnish: None

**Instructions:** POUR the Chartreuse into glass and coat the inside of the glass with the liqueur by tilting and rotating it. DISCARD excess liqueur. Carefully set the liqueur on the inside of the glass alight and allow it to BURN for a few seconds. Extinguish flame by placing a saucer over the glass, add other ingredients and SWIRL to mix. Beware of hot glass rim.

---

### Bermuda Rum Swizzle

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Your five-a-day fruits in a glass, laced with pungent rums and spice infused sweet Falernum.

* 1 shot Bacardi Carta Oro Superior Gold Rum
* 1 shot Goslings Black Seal Rum
* ¾ shot John D. Taylor's Velvet Falernum Liqueur
* 1 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 2 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge & Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into glass and two-thirds fill with crushed ice. SWIZZLE with a swizzle stick or CHURN (stir) with a bar spoon. Fill glass with more crushed ice and repeat. Serve with straws.

Soda and lightly STIR so as not to lose fizz.

### Dr Zeus

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Not that far removed from a Sazerac cocktail, this is innovative and great tasting.

* 1 shot Fernet Branca digestive bitter liqueur
* 20 dried Raisins
* 2 shot Cognac
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ⅛ shot Coffee liqueur
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: None

**Instructions:** POUR Fernet Branca into ice-filled glass. Separately MUDDLE raisins in base of shaker, add other ingredients and SHAKE with ice. Finally DISCARD contents of glass and strain contents of shaker into the Fernet Branca coated glass.

---

### Dry Martini - The 'Naked' or 'Direct' Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The quantities of gin and vermouth stated in this recipe produce a Dry Martini with a 30:1 ratio of gin to vermouth. A small amount of dilution is achieved as the ice coating the frozen glass melts. Both glass and gin must be freezing cold so that the temperature masks the strength of the alcohol. Thus the drink does not taste nearly as strong as it is – you have been warned.

* ⅙ shot Chilled water
* 1/12 shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* 2½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* Garnish: Chilled olive on stick or lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** 1. Place glass and bottle of gin in freezer for at least two hours before making drink.
2. An hour before making drink POUR water into frozen glass, swirl around to coat and place back in freezer. Preferably do this with a little of the water at a time. Continue to swill around during freeing process to coat the sides of the glass.
3. When ready to serve drink, POUR chilled vermouth into icy glass and swirl to coat with vermouth.
4. POUR frozen gin into glass, garnish and serve immediately.

---

### Easter Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Chocolate cocktail with extra interest thanks to vanilla and cardamom.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka

* ½ shot Chilled water
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Dust with chocolate powder or crumbled Cadbury's Flake bar with mini chocolate eggs in orange zest nest on rim.

**Instructions:** MUDDLE cardamom pods in base of shaker. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and strain back into shaker. DRY SHAKE (without ice) and fine strain into chilled glass.

### Estilo Viejo

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Even better when made with añejo tequila.

* 2½ shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* ½ shot AquaRiva Organic Agave Syrup
* 3 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lime zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR half of the tequila with two ice cubes in a glass. Add agave syrup and Angostura and two more ice cubes. Stir some more and add another two ice cubes and the rest of the tequila. Stir lots more and add more ice. The melting and stirring of the ice is essential to the dilution and taste of the drink.

---

### Fish House Punch #2

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Over the decades the recipe the Fish House Punch has constantly morphed. The inclusion of cold tea is a contemporary adaptation.

* 1 shot Cognac
* 1 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Crème de pêche (peach) liqueur
* 1½ shot Freshly brewed cold black English breakfast tea
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Lemon slice & dust with grated nutmeg

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Florida Daiquiri

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This classic blend of rum, lime and sugar, but with a hint of freshly squeezed grapefruit juice and maraschino. A user-friendly version of a Hemingway Special.

* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ⅛ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* ¾ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Flutter

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The three ingredients combine brilliantly.

* 2 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* 1 shot Coffee liqueur
* 1¼ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Fog Cutter #2

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A well-balanced (neither too strong nor too sweet), short, fruity drink which is reminiscent of the modern day Bramble.

* 1 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Cognac
* ½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ¼ shot Cherry Heering cherry brandy liqueur
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 5 ingredients with ice and strain into glass filled with crushed ice. DRIZZLE cherry brandy over drink and serve with straws.

---

### Fosbury Flip

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This richly flavoured, velvety cocktail is almost custardy in consistency but with a refreshing hint of lime.

* 2 shot Bacardi Ocho Anos Gran Reserva Rum
* ¾ shot De Kuyper Apricot Brandy Liqueur
* ¾ shot Frangelico Hazelnut Liqueur
* 2 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ⅔ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ⅛ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* 1 fresh Egg yolk
* Garnish: Apricot slice

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Freddy Fudpucker

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A Harvey Wallbanger made with tequila in place of vodka. Squeeze quality oranges just before making and you'll be amazed just how good this cocktail is.

It's usual to build this drink and 'float' Galliano over the top. However, its better to separately stir the tequila and orange and then strain over fresh ice. Then add the Galliano.

* 2 shot Patrón Reposado (orange seal) 100% agave tequila
* 3½ shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ½ shot Galliano L'Autentico liqueur
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** STIR tequila and orange juice with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. Float Galliano.

---

### French Daiquiri

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A classic Daiquiri made fruity with the addition of black raspberry liqueur and pineapple juice.

* 2½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Black raspberry liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1½ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* 3 dash Difford's Daiquiri Bitters by Bob's Bitters
* Garnish: Pineapple wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### French Mojito

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A classic Mojito with a hint of berry fruit.

* 12 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Black raspberry liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Raspberries & mint sprig

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE mint in base of glass (just to bruise). Add rum, liqueur and lime juice. Half-fill glass with crushed ice and CHURN (stir) with bar spoon. Continue to add crushed ice and churn until drink is level with glass rim.

---

### Frisky Bison

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Sweet 'n' sour, fruity, minty and fresh.

* 7 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Bison grass vodka
* 1 shot Berentzen Apfel Korn (apple schnapps) liqueur
* 1 shot Pressed apple juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Apple slice

**Instructions:** Lightly MUDDLE mint in base of shaker (just to bruise). Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Gibson Dry Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A classic Dry Martini with cocktail onions in place of an olive or a twist.

* 2½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ½ shot Martini Extra Dry vermouth
* Garnish: Two cocktail onions on stick

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Gimlet (Schumann's recipe)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Generously laced with gin and wonderfully tart.

* 2½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1¼ shot Rose's lime cordial
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Gin & It

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Remembering both vermouth and gin are flavoured with similar botanicals, they obviously have an affinity for each other. This drink may be simple but made with a full-bodied Vermouth di Torino it's a fabulously tasty combination of botanicals, wine and spirit.

* 1½ shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1½ shot Martini Rosso sweet vermouth
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Orange slice (if served straight-up use a lemon zest twist)

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Gin & Tonic

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This might not be considered a cocktail by most, but it is actually classified as a Highball. Whatever, it's one of the simplest and best drinks ever devised, hence its lasting popularity.

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* Top up with Tonic water
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into ice-filled glass and serve.

---

### Gin Sour

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** This 4:2:8 formula is a tad sourer than the classic sour proportions of 3:4:8: three quarter part of the sour ingredient (lemon juice), one part of the sweet ingredient (sugar syrup) and two parts of the strong ingredient (gin).

* 2 shot Rutte Dry Gin
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* 3 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* Garnish: Lemon slice & cherry on stick (sail)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Goombay Smash

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Smashes are usually short drinks that include muddled mint, but this potent Tiki-style drink features rum, coconut and fruit.

* 2 shot Navy rum (54.5% alc./vol.)
* ½ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ¾ shot Coconut rum liqueur
* 3 shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ¼ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass.

---

### Grand Cosmopolitan

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The rich flavours of Grand Marnier shine through what is indeed a 'grand' Cosmopolitan.

* 1 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* 1½ shot Cranberry juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 1 dash Angostura Orange Bitters (optional)
* Garnish: Orange zest twist (flamed)

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Grand Sidecar

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A riff on the classic Sidecar that's even simpler to make but equally tasty. 

Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge consists of 51% cognac so there is no need to add cognac to make a great Sidecar, simply add lemon juice. This drink benefits from a touch of dilution so also works well served on-the-rocks in an old-fashioned glass.

* 2 shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Chilled water (omit if using wet ice)
* Garnish: Half sugar rim (if you must) & orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Grande Champagne Cosmo

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** 'Grande Champagne' refers to the top cru of the Cognac region: this drink is suitably elite.

* 1½ shot Cognac
* ¾ shot Grand Marnier Cordon Rouge Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 1 shot Cranberry juice
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Grape Escape

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A cracking drink - subtle and refreshing.

* 8 fresh Seedless white grapes
* 5 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 shot Cognac
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Brut Champagne
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** MUDDLE grapes and mint in base of shaker. Add cognac and sugar, SHAKE with ice and strain into glass filled with crushed ice. TOP with champagne, stir and serve with straws.

---

### Grapefruit Julep

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Wonderfully refreshing. Bring on the sun.

* 1 spoon Runny honey
* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 4 fresh Mint leaves
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¾ shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ½ shot Giffard Sirop Grenadine (Grenadine Syrup)
* Garnish: Mint sprig

**Instructions:** STIR honey with vodka in base of shaker until honey dissolves. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and strain into glass filled with crushed ice.

---

### Green Fairy

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** An Absinthe Sour style drink served straight-up.

* 1 shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* 1 shot Chilled water
* ¾ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 1 dash Angostura Aromatic Bitters
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Lemon zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Green Swizzle

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Robustly flavoured ingredients brought together harmoniously in a tall, most refreshing swizzle. Worthy of its legendary status.

* 1½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot White overproof rum
* ¼ shot La Fée Parisienne Absinthe Superieure
* 1 shot John D. Taylor's Velvet Falernum Liqueur
* ⅛ shot De Kuyper Green Crème de Menthe Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* Garnish: Crown with 3 dashes Angostura bitters over the drink’s ice cap, a lime wedge and mint sprig

**Instructions:** POUR ingredients into chilled glass and two-thirds fill with crushed ice. SWIZZLE with a swizzle stick (or churn with a barspoon). Add more crushed ice to fill and SWIZZLE some more. Serve with straws.

---

### Harvard Cooler

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Refreshing and not too sweet. Lime and sugar enhance the appley spirit.

* 2 shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Top up with Soda (club soda) or sparkling water
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE first 3 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. TOP with soda, stir and serve with straws.

---

### Harvey Wallbanger

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Like the Screwdriver, the Harvey Wallbanger has sadly waned in popularity, probably due to it being served with packaged orange juice. When made with freshly squeezed orange juice and Galliano L'Autentico (rather than Galliano Vanilla) this cocktail is worthy of a renaissance.

This drink is traditionally made without the sugar syrup or bitters, but is  a better drink with them. Shaking (rather than stirring) the first 4 ingredients makes the drink too thin.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 3 shot Freshly squeezed orange juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* ½ shot Galliano L'Autentico liqueur
* Garnish: Orange slice

**Instructions:** STIR first 4 ingredients with ice and strain into ice-filled glass. FLOAT Galliano on the surface.

---

### Havanatheone

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A flavoursome Daiquiri featuring honey, apple and mint.

* 10 fresh Mint leaves
* 2 spoon Runny honey
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¾ shot Pressed apple juice
* Garnish: Mint leaf

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Hemingway Special Daiquiri (Papa Doble)

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A true Hemingway Special should be served without the addition of sugar. However, Hemingway had a hardened palate and more delicate drinkers may prefer the recipe above.

* 3½ shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed pink grapefruit juice
* ¾ shot Luxardo Maraschino Originale Liqueur
* 1 shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Honey Daiquiri

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Sweet honey replaces sugar syrup in this natural Daiquiri. Try experimenting with different honeys. We favour orange blossom honey.

* 2 spoon Runny honey
* 2 shot Bacardi Carta Blanca Superior White Rum (37.5%)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ½ shot Chilled water
* Garnish: Lime wedge

**Instructions:** STIR honey with rum in base of shaker until honey dissolves. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Honeymoon

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** A romantic combination of apple, orange, lemon and herbs.

* ¾ shot Benedictine D.O.M. Liqueur
* 1½ shot Berneroy Fine Calvados
* ¼ shot De Kuyper Triple Sec Liqueur
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lemon juice
* ½ shot Pasteurised egg white
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Apricot Cosmo

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** The apricot preserve adds a flavoursome tang to the contemporary classic.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 spoon Apricot jam (preserve)
* 1 shot Cranberry juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* 2 dash Angostura Orange Bitters
* Garnish: Apricot slice

**Instructions:** STIR apricot preserve with vodka until preserve dissolves. Add other ingredients, SHAKE with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Hunk Cocktail

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Pineapple and vanilla combine wonderfully. American readers may notice more than a passing resemblance to a Key Lime Pie served without the Graham Cracker rim.

* 2 shot Absolut Vanilia Vodka
* 1¾ shot Fresh pressed pineapple juice
* ½ shot Freshly squeezed lime juice
* ¼ shot Sugar syrup (2 sugar to 1 water)
* Garnish: Luxardo Maraschino cherry

**Instructions:** SHAKE all ingredients with ice and fine strain into chilled glass.

---

### Ice 'T' Knee

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Honeyed palate topped off with tannin and jasmine.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1½ shot Cold jasmine tea
* ¾ shot Canadian icewine
* Garnish: Orange zest twist

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.

---

### Iced Sake Martini

(Rating: 4.5 / 5)

**Comment:** Icewine adds interesting and wonderfully subtle honeyed notes to this Sake Martini.

* 2 shot Ketel One Vodka
* 1 shot Junmai ginjō sake
* ¼ shot Canadian icewine
* Garnish: Cucumber slices

**Instructions:** STIR all ingredients with ice and strain into chilled glass.
